
    void openUserProfileSurface() {
        logEvent(launcherShell.activate(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.PROFILE, "main menu profile"));
        if (userProfile != null && userProfile.wrapperDetected) {
            String body = UserProfileAuthority.openProfile(userProfile);
            logEvent(body);
            showTimedAlert("USER PROFILE", body + " " + userProfile.provider + " // " + userProfile.shortId(), 5200);
        } else {
            FallbackProfileManagementAuthority.openProfileManager(this, userProfile, options, jvmRuntimeProfile, renderScaling, this::repaint);
            logEvent("Fallback local profile manager opened.");
        }
        repaint();
    }


    void openWorldSelection() {
        logEvent(launcherShell.activate(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.START, "main menu start"));
        logEvent(launcherRuntime.prepareLocalServer("main menu start"));
        availableWorlds = WorldSaveInfo.listExistingWorlds();
        selectedWorldIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedWorldIndex, Math.max(0, availableWorlds.size()-1)));
        if (availableWorlds.isEmpty()) {
            pendingWorldSetup = WorldSetupSettings.standard();
            lastWorldSetupReport = "No saved world definitions found. Configure and generate a new arcology world first.";
            setScreen(Screen.WORLD_SETUP);
        } else {
            lastWorldSetupReport = "Found " + availableWorlds.size() + " saved world definition(s). Select one or generate a new world.";
            setScreen(Screen.WORLD_SELECT);
        }
    }

    void useSelectedWorldForCharacterCreation() {
        if (availableWorlds.isEmpty()) { openWorldSelection(); return; }
        WorldSaveInfo info = availableWorlds.get(Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedWorldIndex, availableWorlds.size()-1)));
        seed = info.seed;
        worldSetup = info.settings.copy();
        WorldGenerationApi.setActiveSettings(worldSetup);
        NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.setActiveOperatorProfileName(resolveOperatorProfileName());
        atlas = new WorldAtlas(seed, worldSetup);
        worldSelectedForCharacter = true;
        selectedWorldSummary = info.summaryLine();
        generateCandidates(); candidateIndex = 0; jobIndex = 0; jobDossierScroll = 0; jobDossierTab = 0;
        logEvent("WORLD SELECTED: " + selectedWorldSummary);
        DebugLog.audit("WORLD_SELECTED_FOR_CHARACTER", selectedWorldSummary);
        setScreen(Screen.CHARACTER);
    }

    void deleteSelectedWorldDefinition() {
        if (availableWorlds == null || availableWorlds.isEmpty()) {
            lastWorldSetupReport = "No saved world definition is selected for deletion.";
            repaint();
            return;
        }
        int idx = Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedWorldIndex, availableWorlds.size() - 1));
        WorldSaveInfo info = availableWorlds.get(idx);
        String summary = info == null ? "unknown world" : info.summaryLine();
        try {
            Path worldDir = CampaignWorldApi.worldDir().toAbsolutePath().normalize();
            Path target = info.path.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
            String name = target.getFileName() == null ? "" : target.getFileName().toString();
            if (!target.startsWith(worldDir) || !name.endsWith(".mechworld")) {
                throw new IOException("Refusing to delete path outside generated-world directory: " + target);
            }
            Files.deleteIfExists(target);
            DebugLog.audit("WORLD_DEFINITION_DELETED", "path=" + target + " summary=" + summary);
            lastWorldSetupReport = "Deleted world definition: " + summary;
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            DebugLog.error("WORLD_DEFINITION_DELETE_FAILED", "Could not delete selected world definition: " + summary, ex);
            lastWorldSetupReport = "Could not delete selected world definition: " + ex.getMessage();
        }
        availableWorlds = WorldSaveInfo.listExistingWorlds();
        selectedWorldIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(idx, Math.max(0, availableWorlds.size() - 1)));
        if (availableWorlds.isEmpty()) {
            pendingWorldSetup = WorldSetupSettings.standard();
            lastWorldSetupReport += " No saved worlds remain; generate a new arcology world before character creation.";
        }
        repaint();
    }

    void generateConfiguredWorldForCharacterCreation() {
        worldSetup = pendingWorldSetup == null ? WorldSetupSettings.standard() : pendingWorldSetup.copy();
        WorldGenerationApi.setActiveSettings(worldSetup);
        seed = System.currentTimeMillis() ^ Objects.hash(worldSetup.encode(), availableWorlds.size(), eventLog.size());
        NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.setActiveOperatorProfileName(resolveOperatorProfileName());
        atlas = new WorldAtlas(seed, worldSetup);
        worldSelectedForCharacter = true;
        selectedWorldSummary = atlas.hiveWorld.summary();
        lastWorldSetupReport = "Generated " + selectedWorldSummary;
        generateCandidates(); candidateIndex = 0; jobIndex = 0; jobDossierScroll = 0; jobDossierTab = 0;
        logEvent("WORLD GENERATED: " + selectedWorldSummary);
        DebugLog.audit("WORLD_GENERATED_FOR_CHARACTER", selectedWorldSummary + " setup=" + worldSetup.encode());
        setScreen(Screen.CHARACTER);
    }

    void drawWorldSelect(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.BACKGROUND)); g.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, 20, 20, W-40, H-40, "outer");
        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(24f, Math.min(38f, H / 15f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE)); center(g, "SELECT ARCOLOGY WORLD", W/2, Math.max(62, H/8));
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        center(g, "World files are listed above; action buttons are deliberately kept below the list.", W/2, Math.max(92, H/8 + 28));
        int margin = Math.max(34, W / 22);
        int panelY = Math.max(126, H / 4);
        int panelH = Math.max(165, Math.min(H - panelY - 124, 290));
        int panelW = Math.min(760, W - margin * 2);
        int x = (W - panelW) / 2;
        drawPanelBox(g, x, panelY, panelW, panelH, "WORLD FILES");
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (availableWorlds.isEmpty()) lines.add("No generated world files found. Choose GENERATE NEW.");
        else {
            for (int i=0; i<availableWorlds.size(); i++) lines.add((i==selectedWorldIndex?"> ":"  ") + availableWorlds.get(i).summaryLine());
        }
        lines.add("");
        lines.add("Selected world settings persist into the run: NPC density, zone size, room density, prices, crafting difficulty, Hoarder mode, and simulation age.");
        drawScrollableWrappedLines(g, lines, x+18, panelY+42, panelW-36, panelH-62, 0, "world-select");
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, lastWorldSetupReport, W/2, H-42);
    }

    void drawWorldSetup(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.BACKGROUND)); g.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, 20, 20, W-40, H-40, "outer");
        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(24f, Math.min(38f, H / 15f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE)); center(g, "GENERATE ARCOLOGY WORLD", W/2, Math.max(58, H/8));
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        center(g, "Simulation information stays left; controls stay right so low-resolution layouts do not trample themselves.", W/2, Math.max(90, H/8 + 28));
        int margin = Math.max(34, W / 22);
        int top = Math.max(122, H / 5);
        int gap = Math.max(14, W / 55);
        int totalW = W - margin * 2;
        int infoW = Math.max(360, (int)(totalW * 0.58));
        int buttonX = margin + infoW + gap;
        int buttonW = Math.max(190, W - buttonX - margin);
        int panelH = Math.max(310, H - top - 92);
        drawPanelBox(g, margin, top, infoW, panelH, "WORLD GENERATION SETTINGS");
        drawPanelBox(g, buttonX, top, buttonW, 82, "GENERATE");
        drawPanelBox(g, buttonX, top + 96, buttonW, Math.max(180, panelH - 96), "ACTIONS");
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        int ly = top + 50;
        for (String line : pendingWorldSetup.detailLines()) { drawUiTextLine(g, line, margin+24, ly); ly += Math.max(23, H/24); }
        // World-size gauge: Compact to Sprawling, shown as a live percentage fill with numeric endpoints.
        int barX = margin + 24;
        int barY = ly + 10;
        int barW = Math.max(180, infoW - 48);
        int barH = 24;
        int idx = Math.max(0, Math.min(3, pendingWorldSetup.zoneSize));
        int pct = (int)Math.round((idx / 3.0) * 100.0);
        g.setColor(new Color(7,10,10,230)); g.fillRect(barX, barY, barW, barH);
        g.setColor(new Color(92,78,48)); g.drawRect(barX, barY, barW, barH);
        g.setColor(new Color(156,104,48)); g.fillRect(barX+1, barY+1, Math.max(1, (barW-2) * pct / 100), barH-2);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, "WORLD SIZE " + WorldSetupSettings.ZONE_SIZE[idx].toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + " — " + pct + "%", barX + barW/2, barY + 17);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "Min: " + WorldSetupSettings.ZONE_SIZE[0] + " / 0%", barX, barY + 44);
        drawUiTextLine(g, "Max: " + WorldSetupSettings.ZONE_SIZE[3] + " / 100%", barX + Math.max(120, barW - 178), barY + 44);
        int noteY = barY + 70;
        g.setColor(new Color(190,150,100));
        for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap("Simulation age runs additional history batches before world save/start. Higher values improve provenance ledgers but cost generation time. Hoarder mode decouples personal inventory from Strength and Endurance.", Math.max(42, (infoW-48)/8))) { drawUiTextLine(g, line, margin+24, noteY); noteY += 21; }
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, lastWorldSetupReport, W/2, H-42);
    }
    Rectangle mainMenuSubtitleRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int cx = W / 2;
        BufferedImage title = images.get("title_mechanist_rebase");
        if (title == null) title = images.get("title_mechanist");
        int titleTop = mainMenuTitleTop(H);
        int drawnTitleBottom = titleTop + 112;
        if (title != null) {
            Dimension titleSize = mainMenuTitleDrawSize(title, W, H);
            drawnTitleBottom = titleTop + titleSize.height;
        }
        BufferedImage subtitle = images.get("subtitle_rebase");
        if (subtitle == null) return new Rectangle(cx - 360, drawnTitleBottom + 3, 720, 74);
        Dimension subSize = mainMenuSubtitleDrawSize(subtitle, W, H);
        int sy = drawnTitleBottom + 3;
        return new Rectangle(cx - subSize.width / 2, sy, subSize.width, subSize.height);
    }

    Rectangle mainMenuButtonFrameRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        Rectangle subtitle = mainMenuSubtitleRect();
        int frameW = Math.max(520, Math.min(subtitle.width, W - 120));
        int minY = subtitle.y + subtitle.height + 8;
        int runtimeReserveTop = H - Math.max(70, Math.min(96, H / 10));
        int availableH = runtimeReserveTop - minY;
        // 0.9.10ip: prefer a taller launcher bay so six route buttons plus EXIT get
        // discrete rows. If the splash stack consumes too much space, reclaim from the bottom
        // first before allowing the route frame to collapse.
        int desiredH = Math.max(142, Math.min(196, H / 5));
        int frameH = Math.max(128, Math.min(desiredH, availableH - 4));
        int y = minY;
        if (availableH < 136) {
            frameH = Math.max(118, Math.min(154, runtimeReserveTop - subtitle.y - subtitle.height - 4));
            y = Math.max(subtitle.y + subtitle.height + 4, runtimeReserveTop - frameH);
        }
        return new Rectangle((W - frameW) / 2, y, frameW, frameH);
    }

    int mainMenuTitleTop(int H) {
        return Math.max(24, Math.min(54, H / 16));
    }

    Dimension mainMenuTitleDrawSize(BufferedImage title, int W, int H) {
        int maxTitleW = Math.min(1170, W - 54);
        int maxTitleH = Math.max(132, Math.min(285, (int)(H * 0.40)));
        double scale = Math.min(maxTitleW / (double)Math.max(1, title.getWidth()), maxTitleH / (double)Math.max(1, title.getHeight()));
        int tw = Math.max(620, (int)Math.round(title.getWidth() * scale));
        int th = Math.max(118, (int)Math.round(title.getHeight() * scale));
        return new Dimension(tw, th);
    }

    Dimension mainMenuSubtitleDrawSize(BufferedImage subtitle, int W, int H) {
        int maxSubW = Math.min(1050, W - 84);
        int maxSubH = Math.max(70, Math.min(150, H / 5));
        double subScale = Math.min(maxSubW / (double)Math.max(1, subtitle.getWidth()), maxSubH / (double)Math.max(1, subtitle.getHeight()));
        int sw = Math.max(640, (int)Math.round(subtitle.getWidth() * subScale));
        int sh = Math.max(60, (int)Math.round(subtitle.getHeight() * subScale));
        return new Dimension(sw, sh);
    }

    void drawModsSurface(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        Rectangle modal = uiLayout().modal;
        g.setColor(new Color(3,4,4,246));
        g.fillRect(modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "mods-tools-route", modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height);
        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Math.max(30f, Math.min(42f, H/18f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, "EDITOR / MOD PACKAGING", W/2, modal.y + 52);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        java.util.List<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        lines.add("The editor suite now opens inside the main game surface. It owns records, room-grid painting, palette selection, new-entry creation, undo/redo state, and mod-packaging status without launching a detached desktop window.");
        lines.add("Room Editor: choose a palette item, left-click the room grid to place it, right-click to erase it. All editor tabs use a standard NEW entry flow so fresh records are created consistently.");
        lines.add("The older external editor launcher path is closed for player-facing use. Any remaining desktop editor classes are development-only legacy code until they are removed or converted into game-owned surfaces.");
        lines.add("Mod packaging remains data-backed by the editor repository and deployment manager; player-facing access must stay inside this in-game menu before future Workshop/export polish.");
        int actionW = Math.max(250, Math.min(330, modal.width / 4));
        int textW = Math.max(420, modal.width - actionW - 108);
        int y = modal.y + 84;
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        for (String paragraph : lines) {
            for (String line : GuiLayoutApi.wrapText(paragraph, fm, textW)) {
                drawUiTextLine(g, line, modal.x + 42, y);
                y += 20;
                if (y > modal.y + modal.height - 160) break;
            }
            y += 6;
            if (y > modal.y + modal.height - 160) break;
        }
        int actionX = modal.x + modal.width - actionW - 36;
        int actionY = modal.y + modal.height - 150;
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,132));
        g.fillRoundRect(actionX, actionY, actionW, 118, 12, 12);
        g.setColor(new Color(120,105,70,150));
        g.drawRoundRect(actionX, actionY, actionW, 118, 12, 12);
        g.drawLine(modal.x + 36, modal.y + 112, modal.x + modal.width - 36, modal.y + 112);
    }



    java.util.List<String> inGameEditorNames() { return SimulationEditorRepository.EDITORS; }
    String inGameEditorName() {
        java.util.List<String> names = inGameEditorNames();
        if (names.isEmpty()) return "Room Editor";
        inGameEditorTabIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(names.size() - 1, inGameEditorTabIndex));
        return names.get(inGameEditorTabIndex);
    }
    java.util.List<SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity> inGameEditorEntities() { return inGameEditorRepository.entities(inGameEditorName()); }
    SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity inGameEditorEntity() {
        java.util.List<SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity> entities = inGameEditorEntities();
        if (entities.isEmpty()) return null;
        inGameEditorEntityIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(entities.size() - 1, inGameEditorEntityIndex));
        return entities.get(inGameEditorEntityIndex);
    }
    SimulationEditorRepository.EntityRef inGameEditorRef() {
        SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity e = inGameEditorEntity();
        return e == null ? null : new SimulationEditorRepository.EntityRef(inGameEditorName(), e.id());
    }
    void selectInGameEditorTab(int idx) {
        java.util.List<String> names = inGameEditorNames();
        inGameEditorTabIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(Math.max(0, names.size()-1), idx));
        inGameEditorEntityIndex = 0;
        inGameEditorStatus = "Editor tab: " + inGameEditorName() + ".";
        repaint();
    }
    void selectInGameEditorEntity(int idx) {
        inGameEditorEntityIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(Math.max(0, inGameEditorEntities().size()-1), idx));
        SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity e = inGameEditorEntity();
        inGameEditorStatus = e == null ? "No entry selected." : "Selected " + e.name() + ".";
        repaint();
    }
    void createNewInGameEditorEntry() {
        SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity created = inGameEditorRepository.createBlankEntity(inGameEditorName());
        java.util.List<SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity> entities = inGameEditorEntities();
        for (int i=0;i<entities.size();i++) if (entities.get(i).id().equals(created.id())) { inGameEditorEntityIndex = i; break; }
        inGameEditorStatus = "Created new " + inGameEditorName().replace(" Editor", "") + " entry: " + created.name() + ".";
        DebugLog.audit("INGAME_EDITOR_NEW", inGameEditorName() + " id=" + created.id());
        repaint();
    }
    void inGameEditorUndo() { inGameEditorUndoRedo.undo(); inGameEditorStatus = "Undo: " + inGameEditorUndoRedo.compactState(); repaint(); }
    void inGameEditorRedo() { inGameEditorUndoRedo.redo(); inGameEditorStatus = "Redo: " + inGameEditorUndoRedo.compactState(); repaint(); }

    Rectangle inGameEditorOuterRect() {
        Rectangle m = uiLayout().modal;
        return new Rectangle(Math.max(18, m.x - 18), Math.max(18, m.y - 10), Math.min(getWidth()-36, m.width + 36), Math.min(getHeight()-36, m.height + 18));
    }
    Rectangle inGameEditorTabRect() { Rectangle r = inGameEditorOuterRect(); return new Rectangle(r.x + 20, r.y + 54, r.width - 40, 34); }
    Rectangle inGameEditorLeftRect() { Rectangle r = inGameEditorOuterRect(); int top = r.y + 98; int h = r.height - 154; int w = Math.max(210, Math.min(280, r.width / 4)); return new Rectangle(r.x + 22, top, w, h); }
    Rectangle inGameEditorRightRect() { Rectangle r = inGameEditorOuterRect(); int top = r.y + 98; int h = r.height - 154; int w = Math.max(260, Math.min(360, r.width / 3)); return new Rectangle(r.x + r.width - w - 22, top, w, h); }
    Rectangle inGameEditorCenterRect() { Rectangle l = inGameEditorLeftRect(); Rectangle rr = inGameEditorRightRect(); int x = l.x + l.width + 16; return new Rectangle(x, l.y, Math.max(260, rr.x - x - 16), l.height); }
    Rectangle inGameEditorStatusRect() { Rectangle r = inGameEditorOuterRect(); return new Rectangle(r.x + 22, r.y + r.height - 42, r.width - 44, 26); }
    Rectangle inGameRoomGridRect() { Rectangle c = inGameEditorCenterRect(); return new Rectangle(c.x + 18, c.y + 76, c.width - 36, Math.max(140, c.height - 122)); }

    String[][] inGameEditorPalettes() {
        return new String[][]{
                {"Items", "sealed ration", "stubcarbine", "logic Engine core", "repair kit", "water canister", "scrap bundle"},
                {"Entity Spawners", "civilian spawn", "guard patrol node", "scavenger camp node", "bound Labor Automaton route", "trader counter", "hostile ambush"},
                {"Floor Tiles", "worn-plasteel", "oil-stained iron", "stone and brass", "deck plating", "ceramite tile", "sump grate"},
                {"Wall Tiles", "hab partition", "bulkhead wall", "gothic stone", "corrugated barricade", "sealed hatch", "service conduit"},
                {"Objects", "cot", "sink", "dresser", "cabinet", "generator", "pillar", "altar", "terminal", "crate", "candle rack"}
        };
    }
    String inGameEditorPaletteCategory() {
        String[][] p = inGameEditorPalettes();
        inGameEditorPaletteTab = Math.max(0, Math.min(p.length-1, inGameEditorPaletteTab));
        return p[inGameEditorPaletteTab][0];
    }
    String inGameEditorSelectedPaletteItem() {
        String[][] p = inGameEditorPalettes();
        inGameEditorPaletteTab = Math.max(0, Math.min(p.length-1, inGameEditorPaletteTab));
        int max = Math.max(1, p[inGameEditorPaletteTab].length - 1);
        inGameEditorPaletteIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(max-1, inGameEditorPaletteIndex));
        return p[inGameEditorPaletteTab][inGameEditorPaletteIndex + 1];
    }
    void selectInGameEditorPaletteTab(int idx) { inGameEditorPaletteTab = Math.max(0, Math.min(inGameEditorPalettes().length-1, idx)); inGameEditorPaletteIndex = 0; inGameEditorStatus = "Palette category: " + inGameEditorPaletteCategory() + "."; repaint(); }
    void selectInGameEditorPaletteItem(int idx) { inGameEditorPaletteIndex = Math.max(0, idx); inGameEditorStatus = "Palette item: " + inGameEditorSelectedPaletteItem() + "."; repaint(); }

    void rebuildInGameEditorButtons() {
        Rectangle outer = inGameEditorOuterRect();
        Rectangle tabs = inGameEditorTabRect();
        Rectangle left = inGameEditorLeftRect();
        Rectangle right = inGameEditorRightRect();
        int gap = Math.max(5, scaled(5));
        java.util.List<String> names = inGameEditorNames();
        int tabW = Math.max(84, (tabs.width - gap * Math.max(0, names.size()-1)) / Math.max(1, names.size()));
        for (int i=0;i<names.size();i++) {
            final int idx = i;
            String label = (i == inGameEditorTabIndex ? "▶ " : "") + names.get(i).replace(" Editor", "").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox(label, tabs.x + i*(tabW+gap), tabs.y, tabW, tabs.height, "Switch to " + names.get(i) + ".", () -> selectInGameEditorTab(idx)));
        }
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("BACK", outer.x + 18, outer.y + 14, 110, 30, "Return to Mods / Tools.", () -> setScreen(Screen.MODS)));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("NEW " + inGameEditorName().replace(" Editor", "").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT), left.x + 12, left.y + 36, left.width - 24, 28, "Create a fresh blank entry for the active editor.", this::createNewInGameEditorEntry));
        java.util.List<SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity> entities = inGameEditorEntities();
        int rowH = Math.max(24, Math.min(30, (left.height - 92) / Math.max(4, Math.min(10, Math.max(1, entities.size())))));
        int listY = left.y + 76;
        int visible = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, (left.y + left.height - listY - 12) / Math.max(1, rowH)));
        for (int i=0;i<Math.min(visible, entities.size());i++) {
            final int idx = i;
            String label = (i == inGameEditorEntityIndex ? "▶ " : "") + entities.get(i).name();
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox(label, left.x + 12, listY + i*rowH, left.width - 24, rowH - 3, "Select editor record " + entities.get(i).id() + ".", () -> selectInGameEditorEntity(idx)));
        }
        int cmdX = right.x + 12;
        int cmdW = right.width - 24;
        int y = right.y + right.height - 112;
        int bw = Math.max(86, (cmdW - gap) / 2);
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("UNDO", cmdX, y, bw, 26, "Undo the last editor command.", this::inGameEditorUndo));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("REDO", cmdX + bw + gap, y, bw, 26, "Redo the last editor command.", this::inGameEditorRedo));
        y += 32;
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("HELP " + (inGameEditorHelpVisible ? "ON" : "OFF"), cmdX, y, cmdW, 26, "Show or hide the editor explanation banner.", () -> { inGameEditorHelpVisible = !inGameEditorHelpVisible; repaint(); }));
        if ("Room Editor".equals(inGameEditorName())) {
            String[][] p = inGameEditorPalettes();
            int py = right.y + 38;
            int catH = 24;
            for (int i=0;i<p.length;i++) {
                final int idx = i;
                buttons.add(new ButtonBox((i == inGameEditorPaletteTab ? "▶ " : "") + p[i][0], cmdX, py + i*(catH+3), cmdW, catH, "Choose room-editor palette category " + p[i][0] + ".", () -> selectInGameEditorPaletteTab(idx)));
            }
            int itemY = py + p.length*(catH+3) + 10;
            int itemH = 23;
            String[] active = p[Math.max(0, Math.min(p.length-1, inGameEditorPaletteTab))];
            for (int i=1; i<active.length && i<=8; i++) {
                final int idx = i - 1;
                buttons.add(new ButtonBox((idx == inGameEditorPaletteIndex ? "▶ " : "") + active[i], cmdX, itemY + idx*(itemH+3), cmdW, itemH, "Select palette item; left-click grid to place, right-click to erase.", () -> selectInGameEditorPaletteItem(idx)));
            }
        }
    }

    void drawInGameEditorSurface(Graphics2D g) {
        Rectangle outer = inGameEditorOuterRect();
        Rectangle tabs = inGameEditorTabRect();
        Rectangle left = inGameEditorLeftRect();
        Rectangle center = inGameEditorCenterRect();
        Rectangle right = inGameEditorRightRect();
        Rectangle status = inGameEditorStatusRect();
        g.setColor(new Color(3,4,4,248));
        g.fillRect(outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "in-game-editor-suite", outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height);
        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Math.max(26f, Math.min(38f, getHeight()/20f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, "IN-GAME EDITORS", outer.x + outer.width/2, outer.y + 38);
        if (inGameEditorHelpVisible) {
            g.setFont(smallFont);
            g.setColor(new Color(10,10,8,220));
            g.fillRoundRect(outer.x + 150, outer.y + 10, outer.width - 300, 30, 10, 10);
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel("Editors are owned by the main game surface. Room grid: left-click paints selected palette item, right-click erases. New creates a blank entry in the active editor.", g.getFontMetrics(), outer.width - 330), outer.x + outer.width/2, outer.y + 30);
        }
        drawSlicedFrame(g, left.x, left.y, left.width, left.height, "inner");
        drawSlicedFrame(g, center.x, center.y, center.width, center.height, "inner");
        drawSlicedFrame(g, right.x, right.y, right.width, right.height, "inner");
        g.setFont(uiFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(14f, uiFont.getSize2D()-2f)));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "RECORDS", left.x + 14, left.y + 24);
        drawUiTextLine(g, inGameEditorName().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT), center.x + 14, center.y + 24);
        drawUiTextLine(g, "COMMANDS / INSPECTOR", right.x + 14, right.y + 24);
        SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity entity = inGameEditorEntity();
        if (entity == null) {
            g.setFont(smallFont);
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            drawUiTextLine(g, "No entry exists. Use NEW.", center.x + 18, center.y + 60);
        } else if ("Room Editor".equals(inGameEditorName())) {
            drawInGameRoomEditor(g, entity, center);
        } else {
            drawInGameGenericEditor(g, entity, center);
        }
        drawInGameEditorInspector(g, entity, right);
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,170));
        g.fillRoundRect(status.x, status.y, status.width, status.height, 8, 8);
        g.setColor(new Color(130,112,70,150));
        g.drawRoundRect(status.x, status.y, status.width, status.height, 8, 8);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(inGameEditorStatus + " | " + inGameEditorRepository.auditLine() + " | " + inGameEditorUndoRedo.compactState(), g.getFontMetrics(), status.width - 16), status.x + 8, status.y + 18);
    }

    void drawInGameGenericEditor(Graphics2D g, SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity entity, Rectangle center) {
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        drawUiTextLine(g, entity.name() + "  [" + entity.id() + "]", center.x + 18, center.y + 58);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        int y = center.y + 90;
        for (Map.Entry<String,Object> e : entity.properties().entrySet()) {
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(e.getKey() + ":", g.getFontMetrics(), 160), center.x + 24, y);
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(String.valueOf(e.getValue()), g.getFontMetrics(), center.width - 210), center.x + 178, y);
            y += 24;
            if (y > center.y + center.height - 24) break;
        }
    }

    void drawInGameRoomEditor(Graphics2D g, SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity entity, Rectangle center) {
        Map<String,Object> props = entity.properties();
        int roomW = editorInt(props.get("width"), 1, 32, 8);
        int roomH = editorInt(props.get("height"), 1, 32, 6);
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        drawUiTextLine(g, entity.name() + "  [" + roomW + "x" + roomH + "]", center.x + 18, center.y + 58);
        Rectangle grid = inGameRoomGridRect();
        g.setColor(new Color(10, 10, 10, 235));
        g.fillRect(grid.x, grid.y, grid.width, grid.height);
        g.setColor(new Color(130,112,70,150));
        g.drawRect(grid.x, grid.y, grid.width, grid.height);
        int cell = Math.max(10, Math.min(42, Math.min((grid.width - 12) / Math.max(1, roomW), (grid.height - 12) / Math.max(1, roomH))));
        int gridW = cell * roomW;
        int gridH = cell * roomH;
        int ox = grid.x + (grid.width - gridW) / 2;
        int oy = grid.y + (grid.height - gridH) / 2;
        Map<String,String> cells = decodeEditorGrid(String.valueOf(props.getOrDefault("layoutCells", "")));
        String floor = String.valueOf(props.getOrDefault("floorMaterial", "worn-plasteel"));
        for (int y=0; y<roomH; y++) for (int x=0; x<roomW; x++) {
            boolean wall = x == 0 || y == 0 || x == roomW-1 || y == roomH-1;
            int px = ox + x*cell, py = oy + y*cell;
            g.setColor(wall ? new Color(88,72,48) : editorFloorColor(floor));
            g.fillRect(px, py, cell, cell);
            String placed = cells.get(x + "," + y);
            if (placed != null && !placed.isBlank()) {
                BufferedImage placedImg = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForAssetId(ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForEditorPalette(inGameEditorPaletteCategory(), placed));
                if (placedImg != null) {
                    g.drawImage(placedImg, px+3, py+3, Math.max(4, cell-6), Math.max(4, cell-6), null);
                    g.setColor(new Color(12, 12, 8, 130));
                    g.drawRoundRect(px+3, py+3, Math.max(4, cell-6), Math.max(4, cell-6), 6, 6);
                } else {
                    g.setColor(new Color(42, 86, 74, 215));
                    g.fillRoundRect(px+3, py+3, Math.max(4, cell-6), Math.max(4, cell-6), 6, 6);
                    g.setColor(new Color(235, 212, 128));
                    String mark = placed.length() <= 2 ? placed : placed.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
                    center(g, mark, px + cell/2, py + cell/2 + 5);
                }
            }
            g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,140));
            g.drawRect(px, py, cell, cell);
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "Palette: " + inGameEditorPaletteCategory() + " / " + inGameEditorSelectedPaletteItem() + " | assetId=" + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForEditorPalette(inGameEditorPaletteCategory(), inGameEditorSelectedPaletteItem()), center.x + 18, center.y + center.height - 28);
    }

    void drawInGameEditorInspector(Graphics2D g, SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity entity, Rectangle right) {
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        if (entity == null) return;
        if ("Room Editor".equals(inGameEditorName())) {
            String assetId = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForEditorPalette(inGameEditorPaletteCategory(), inGameEditorSelectedPaletteItem());
            BufferedImage icon = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForAssetId(assetId);
            int box = Math.max(64, Math.min(96, right.width / 3));
            int ix = right.x + right.width - box - 16;
            int iy = right.y + 42;
            g.setColor(new Color(8, 10, 9, 235));
            g.fillRect(ix, iy, box, box);
            g.setColor(new Color(130,112,70,180));
            g.drawRect(ix, iy, box, box);
            if (icon != null) g.drawImage(icon, ix + 4, iy + 4, box - 8, box - 8, null);
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            drawUiTextLine(g, "Palette assetId=" + assetId, right.x + 14, iy + box + 18);
        }
        int y = right.y + ("Room Editor".equals(inGameEditorName()) ? 322 : 44);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "SELECTED", right.x + 14, y); y += 22;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(entity.name(), g.getFontMetrics(), right.width - 28), right.x + 14, y); y += 22;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(entity.id(), g.getFontMetrics(), right.width - 28), right.x + 14, y); y += 24;
        int maxY = right.y + right.height - 126;
        for (Map.Entry<String,Object> e : entity.properties().entrySet()) {
            if (y > maxY) break;
            String value = String.valueOf(e.getValue());
            if ("layoutCells".equals(e.getKey())) value = decodeEditorGrid(value).size() + " painted cells";
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(e.getKey() + ": " + value, g.getFontMetrics(), right.width - 28), right.x + 14, y);
            y += 20;
        }
    }

    int editorInt(Object raw, int min, int max, int fallback) {
        int v = fallback;
        if (raw instanceof Number n) v = n.intValue();
        else if (raw != null) try { v = Integer.parseInt(String.valueOf(raw).trim()); } catch (NumberFormatException ignored) {}
        return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, v));
    }
    Color editorFloorColor(String floor) {
        String f = floor == null ? "" : floor.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (f.contains("oil")) return new Color(44, 48, 36);
        if (f.contains("stone")) return new Color(62, 55, 46);
        if (f.contains("deck")) return new Color(48, 56, 58);
        if (f.contains("ceramite")) return new Color(64, 64, 60);
        if (f.contains("sump")) return new Color(38, 56, 48);
        return new Color(50, 54, 48);
    }
    Map<String,String> decodeEditorGrid(String raw) {
        LinkedHashMap<String,String> out = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        if (raw == null || raw.isBlank()) return out;
        for (String part : raw.split(";")) {
            int eq = part.indexOf('=');
            if (eq <= 0) continue;
            String key = part.substring(0, eq).trim();
            String val = part.substring(eq+1).trim();
            if (key.matches("\\d+,\\d+") && !val.isBlank()) out.put(key, val);
        }
        return out;
    }
    String encodeEditorGrid(Map<String,String> cells) {
        if (cells == null || cells.isEmpty()) return "";
        ArrayList<String> keys = new ArrayList<>(cells.keySet());
        keys.sort((a,b) -> {
            String[] aa=a.split(","); String[] bb=b.split(",");
            int ay=Integer.parseInt(aa[1]), by=Integer.parseInt(bb[1]);
            if (ay != by) return Integer.compare(ay, by);
            return Integer.compare(Integer.parseInt(aa[0]), Integer.parseInt(bb[0]));
        });
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        for (String k : keys) {
            if (sb.length() > 0) sb.append(';');
            sb.append(k).append('=').append(cells.get(k).replace(';', ',').replace('=', ':'));
        }
        return sb.toString();
    }
    Point inGameEditorGridCellAt(int mx, int my) {
        if (!"Room Editor".equals(inGameEditorName())) return null;
        SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity entity = inGameEditorEntity();
        if (entity == null) return null;
        Map<String,Object> props = entity.properties();
        int roomW = editorInt(props.get("width"), 1, 32, 8);
        int roomH = editorInt(props.get("height"), 1, 32, 6);
        Rectangle grid = inGameRoomGridRect();
        int cell = Math.max(10, Math.min(42, Math.min((grid.width - 12) / Math.max(1, roomW), (grid.height - 12) / Math.max(1, roomH))));
        int ox = grid.x + (grid.width - cell * roomW) / 2;
        int oy = grid.y + (grid.height - cell * roomH) / 2;
        if (mx < ox || my < oy || mx >= ox + cell*roomW || my >= oy + cell*roomH) return null;
        return new Point((mx - ox) / cell, (my - oy) / cell);
    }
    boolean handleInGameEditorGridPaint(int mx, int my, boolean erase) {
        Point cell = inGameEditorGridCellAt(mx, my);
        if (cell == null) return false;
        SimulationEditorRepository.EntityRef ref = inGameEditorRef();
        if (ref == null) return false;
        Object old = inGameEditorRepository.property(ref, "layoutCells");
        Map<String,String> cells = decodeEditorGrid(String.valueOf(old == null ? "" : old));
        String key = cell.x + "," + cell.y;
        if (erase) cells.remove(key); else cells.put(key, inGameEditorSelectedPaletteItem());
        String next = encodeEditorGrid(cells);
        inGameEditorUndoRedo.execute(new EditorCommand.PropertyChange(inGameEditorRepository, ref, "layoutCells", old == null ? "" : old, next, inGameEditorEventBus));
        inGameEditorStatus = (erase ? "Erased" : "Placed " + inGameEditorSelectedPaletteItem()) + " at room cell " + cell.x + "," + cell.y + ".";
        repaint();
        return true;
    }


    Rectangle sectorAuditMapRect() { return uiLayout().map; }

    Point screenPointToAuditTile(int sx, int sy) {
        if (auditWorld == null) return null;
        Rectangle map = inputMapRect();
        int cellW = auditMapCellW(null);
        int cellH = auditMapCellH(null);
        int cols = Math.max(1, (map.width - 18) / Math.max(1, cellW));
        int rows = Math.max(1, (map.height - 18) / Math.max(1, cellH));
        int camX = Math.max(0, Math.min(auditWorld.w - cols, auditCursorX - cols / 2));
        int camY = Math.max(0, Math.min(auditWorld.h - rows, auditCursorY - rows / 2));
        int ox = map.x + 10, oy = map.y + 10;
        int drawW = cols * Math.max(1, cellW);
        int drawH = rows * Math.max(1, cellH);
        if (sx < ox || sy < oy || sx >= ox + drawW || sy >= oy + drawH) return null;
        int tx = camX + Math.floorDiv(sx - ox, Math.max(1, cellW));
        int ty = camY + Math.floorDiv(sy - oy, Math.max(1, cellH));
        if (!auditWorld.inBounds(tx, ty)) return null;
        return new Point(tx, ty);
    }

    void drawSectorAuditSurface(Graphics2D g) {
        advanceAuditTracePlaybackIfNeeded();
        if (auditWorld == null) regenerateSectorAuditWorld("draw missing audit world");
        UiLayout L = uiLayout();
        Rectangle map = L.map;
        g.setFont(auditAsciiFont());
        int cellW = auditMapCellW(g);
        int cellH = auditMapCellH(g);
        int cols = Math.max(1, (map.width - 18) / Math.max(1, cellW));
        int rows = Math.max(1, (map.height - 18) / Math.max(1, cellH));
        int camX = auditWorld == null ? 0 : Math.max(0, Math.min(auditWorld.w - cols, auditCursorX - cols / 2));
        int camY = auditWorld == null ? 0 : Math.max(0, Math.min(auditWorld.h - rows, auditCursorY - rows / 2));
        g.setColor(Color.BLACK);
        g.fillRect(map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "zone-audit-map", map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height);
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(map.x + 7, map.y + 7, map.width - 14, map.height - 14);
        int ox = map.x + 10;
        int oy = sectorAuditTileIconMode() ? map.y + 10 : map.y + 10 + g.getFontMetrics(auditAsciiFont()).getAscent();
        if (auditWorld != null) {
            World oldWorld = world;
            boolean[][] oldVisibleTiles = visibleTiles;
            boolean[][] oldRememberedTiles = rememberedTiles;
            world = auditWorld;
            visibleTiles = SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.fullBrightMask(auditWorld);
            rememberedTiles = visibleTiles;
            try {
                for (int sy = 0; sy < rows; sy++) {
                    int y = camY + sy;
                    if (y < 0 || y >= auditWorld.h) continue;
                    for (int sx = 0; sx < cols; sx++) {
                        int x = camX + sx;
                        if (x < 0 || x >= auditWorld.w) continue;
                        char ch = auditWorld.tiles[x][y];
                        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) drawMapTileIcon(g, ch, x, y, ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH, cellW, cellH, 1.0f, true);
                        else { g.setColor(colorForTile(x, y, ch)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(ch), ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH); }
                    }
                }
                if (auditWorld.mapObjects != null) {
                    for (MapObjectState mo : auditWorld.mapObjects) {
                        if (mo == null || mo.x < camX || mo.y < camY || mo.x >= camX + cols || mo.y >= camY + rows) continue;
                        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) drawMapFeatureIcon(g, mo, ox + (mo.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (mo.y - camY) * cellH, cellW, cellH, new Color(100, 210, 160, 70));
                        else { g.setColor(new Color(170, 215, 155)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(mo.glyph), ox + (mo.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (mo.y - camY) * cellH); }
                    }
                }
                if (auditWorld.lightSources != null) drawZoneLightFixtureObjects(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                if (auditWorld.hazardWarnings != null) drawEnvironmentalHazardOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                if (auditWorld.trapRecords != null) drawTrapWarningOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                if (auditWorld.npcs != null) {
                    for (NpcEntity npc : auditWorld.npcs) {
                        if (npc == null || npc.x < camX || npc.y < camY || npc.x >= camX + cols || npc.y >= camY + rows) continue;
                        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) drawNpcMapIcon(g, npc, ox + (npc.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (npc.y - camY) * cellH, cellW, cellH);
                        else { g.setColor(npcColor(npc.faction)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(npc.symbol), ox + (npc.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (npc.y - camY) * cellH); }
                    }
                }
                drawSectorAuditDiagnosticOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                drawSectorAuditTraceMarker(g, camX, camY, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                drawZoneAuditGenerationLogOverlay(g, map, camX, camY, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            } finally { world = oldWorld; visibleTiles = oldVisibleTiles; rememberedTiles = oldRememberedTiles; }
            int sx = auditCursorX - camX, sy = auditCursorY - camY;
            if (sx >= 0 && sy >= 0 && sx < cols && sy < rows) {
                int rx = ox + sx * cellW, ry = oy + sy * cellH;
                g.setColor(new Color(245, 210, 95));
                g.drawRect(rx - 2, ry - 2, cellW + 4, cellH + 4);
                g.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry - 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + Math.max(2, cellH/4));
                g.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH + 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH - Math.max(2, cellH/4));
                g.drawLine(rx - 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
                g.drawLine(rx + cellW + 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + cellW - Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
            }
        }
        g.setClip(oldClip);
        drawSectorAuditCommandPanel(g, L);
        drawSectorAuditInfoPanel(g, L);
        drawSectorAuditZoneDropdown(g, L);
    }



    java.util.List<String> auditTileInspectionLines(int x, int y) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (auditWorld == null || !auditWorld.inBounds(x, y)) return lines;
        char ch = auditWorld.tiles[x][y];
        int roomId = auditWorld.roomIdAt(x, y);
        RoomProfile rp = roomId >= 0 && roomId < auditWorld.roomProfiles.size() ? auditWorld.roomProfiles.get(roomId) : null;
        Faction owner = auditWorld.roomFaction(roomId);
        CompiledTileDescriptor d = TileDataCompilationAuthority.resolve(auditWorld, x, y, ch);
        lines.add("Observed tile: glyph '" + ch + "' floor/wall layer=" + (d == null ? "unknown" : d.baseLayer + "/" + d.family) + " roomId=" + roomId + " owner=" + (owner == null ? "none" : owner.label) + ".");
        if (rp != null) lines.add("Room: " + rp.name + " — " + rp.descriptor + " features=" + rp.featureText + ".");
        ArrayList<String> occupants = new ArrayList<>();
        NpcEntity npc = auditWorld.npcAt(x, y);
        if (npc != null) occupants.add("entity=" + npc.name + " / " + npc.role + " / " + (npc.faction == null ? "none" : npc.faction.label));
        MapObjectState mo = auditWorld.mapObjectAt(x, y);
        if (mo != null) occupants.add("object=" + mo.summary() + " | assetId=" + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForMapObject(mo));
        if (auditWorld.lightSources != null) for (ZoneLightSourceRecord l : auditWorld.lightSources) if (l != null && l.x == x && l.y == y) occupants.add("light=" + l.stockState() + " | assetId=" + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForLight(l));
        if (auditWorld.trapRecords != null) for (TrapRecord t : auditWorld.trapRecords) if (t != null && t.x == x && t.y == y) occupants.add("trap=" + t.label + " / " + t.type + " / " + t.state + " / effect=" + t.effect + " severity=" + t.severity + " | assetId=" + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForTrap(t));
        if (auditWorld.hazardWarnings != null) for (EnvironmentalHazardRecord hz : auditWorld.hazardWarnings) if (hz != null && hz.x == x && hz.y == y) occupants.add("hazard=" + hz.label + " / " + hz.severityText() + " / " + hz.warningText());
        if (occupants.isEmpty()) lines.add("Tile contents: no entity, object/container, light, trap, or hazard record on the selected cell.");
        else lines.addAll(occupants);
        return lines;
    }

    void drawSectorAuditTraceMarker(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.Step step = currentAuditTraceStep();
        if (step == null || auditWorld == null || !auditWorld.inBounds(step.x, step.y)) return;
        int sx = ox + (step.x - camX) * cellW;
        int sy = oy + (step.y - camY) * cellH;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(Math.max(2f, cellW / 9f)));
        if (step.ghostRect != null) {
            Rectangle gr = step.ghostRect;
            int gx1 = Math.max(gr.x, camX), gy1 = Math.max(gr.y, camY);
            int gx2 = Math.min(gr.x + gr.width, camX + Math.max(1, (mapRect().width - 18) / Math.max(1, cellW)));
            int gy2 = Math.min(gr.y + gr.height, camY + Math.max(1, (mapRect().height - 18) / Math.max(1, cellH)));
            if (gx1 < gx2 && gy1 < gy2) {
                int rx = ox + (gx1 - camX) * cellW;
                int ry = oy + (gy1 - camY) * cellH;
                int rw = Math.max(1, (gx2 - gx1) * cellW);
                int rh = Math.max(1, (gy2 - gy1) * cellH);
                gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver.derive(step.rejected ? 0.18f : 0.16f));
                gg.setColor(step.rejected ? new Color(255, 70, 45) : new Color(245, 225, 95));
                gg.fillRect(rx, ry, rw, rh);
                gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver.derive(0.82f));
                gg.drawRect(rx, ry, Math.max(1, rw - 1), Math.max(1, rh - 1));
            }
        }
        if (sx + cellW >= ox && sy + cellH >= oy && sx <= ox + Math.max(1, auditWorld.w) * cellW && sy <= oy + Math.max(1, auditWorld.h) * cellH) {
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver);
            if (step.rejected) {
                gg.setColor(new Color(255, 70, 45, 230));
                gg.drawLine(sx + 3, sy + 3, sx + cellW - 4, sy + cellH - 4);
                gg.drawLine(sx + cellW - 4, sy + 3, sx + 3, sy + cellH - 4);
            } else {
                gg.setColor(new Color(245, 225, 95, 235));
                gg.drawRect(sx + 2, sy + 2, Math.max(3, cellW - 5), Math.max(3, cellH - 5));
                gg.drawLine(sx + cellW / 2, sy - Math.max(2, cellH / 3), sx + cellW / 2, sy + cellH + Math.max(2, cellH / 3));
                gg.drawLine(sx - Math.max(2, cellW / 3), sy + cellH / 2, sx + cellW + Math.max(2, cellW / 3), sy + cellH / 2);
            }
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void drawZoneAuditGenerationLogOverlay(Graphics2D g, Rectangle map, int camX, int camY, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (auditTraceSteps == null || auditTraceSteps.isEmpty()) return;
        int current = Math.max(0, Math.min(auditTraceSteps.size() - 1, auditTraceIndex));
        int lines = Math.max(6, Math.min(12, map.height / 42));
        int start = Math.max(0, current - lines + 2);
        int end = Math.min(auditTraceSteps.size(), start + lines);
        int panelW = Math.max(330, Math.min(560, map.width / 2));
        int lineH = Math.max(15, g.getFontMetrics(smallFont).getHeight() + 2);
        int panelH = 14 + (end - start) * lineH;
        int px = map.x + 18;
        int py = map.y + 18;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setColor(new Color(0, 0, 0, 178));
        gg.fillRoundRect(px, py, panelW, panelH, 10, 10);
        gg.setColor(new Color(145, 118, 64, 155));
        gg.drawRoundRect(px, py, panelW, panelH, 10, 10);
        gg.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D() - 3f)));
        FontMetrics fm = gg.getFontMetrics();
        int y = py + 12 + fm.getAscent();
        for (int i = start; i < end; i++) {
            SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.Step st = auditTraceSteps.get(i);
            boolean selected = i == current;
            if (selected) {
                gg.setColor(new Color(145, 118, 64, 210));
                gg.fillRect(px + 6, y - fm.getAscent() - 2, panelW - 12, lineH);
            }
            gg.setColor(st.rejected ? new Color(255, 145, 115) : (selected ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN)));
            String line = st.line(auditTraceSteps.size());
            int maxChars = Math.max(24, (panelW - 18) / Math.max(5, fm.charWidth('W')));
            if (line.length() > maxChars) line = line.substring(0, Math.max(0, maxChars - 1)) + "…";
            drawUiTextLine(gg, line, px + 10, y);
            y += lineH;
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void drawSectorAuditDiagnosticOverlays(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (auditWorld == null || auditOverlayMode == 0) return;
        int mode = Math.floorMod(auditOverlayMode, SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.OVERLAY_LABELS.length);
        Composite oldComposite = g.getComposite();
        Stroke oldStroke = g.getStroke();
        if (mode == 2) { // rooms
            for (int i = 0; i < auditWorld.rooms.size(); i++) {
                Rectangle rr = auditWorld.rooms.get(i);
                int x1 = Math.max(rr.x, camX), y1 = Math.max(rr.y, camY);
                int x2 = Math.min(rr.x + rr.width, camX + cols), y2 = Math.min(rr.y + rr.height, camY + rows);
                if (x1 >= x2 || y1 >= y2) continue;
                boolean flagged = false;
                if (auditSnapshot != null) for (SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.AuditFinding f : auditSnapshot.findings) if (f.category.equals("ROOM") && f.label.contains(" " + i)) { flagged = true; break; }
                g.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver.derive(flagged ? 0.28f : 0.15f));
                g.setColor(flagged ? new Color(230, 80, 70) : new Color(90, 150, 230));
                g.fillRect(ox + (x1 - camX) * cellW, oy + (y1 - camY) * cellH, Math.max(1, (x2 - x1) * cellW), Math.max(1, (y2 - y1) * cellH));
                g.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver.derive(0.72f));
                g.drawRect(ox + (x1 - camX) * cellW, oy + (y1 - camY) * cellH, Math.max(1, (x2 - x1) * cellW - 1), Math.max(1, (y2 - y1) * cellH - 1));
            }
        } else if (mode == 3 || mode == 4 || mode == 5 || mode >= 6) {
            for (int sy=0; sy<rows; sy++) {
                int y = camY + sy;
                if (y < 0 || y >= auditWorld.h) continue;
                for (int sx=0; sx<cols; sx++) {
                    int x = camX + sx;
                    if (x < 0 || x >= auditWorld.w) continue;
                    char ch = auditWorld.tiles[x][y];
                    CompiledTileDescriptor d = TileDataCompilationAuthority.resolve(auditWorld, x, y, ch);
                    Color color = null;
                    float alpha = 0.0f;
                    if (mode == 3) { // roads
                        if (ch == RoadGridIntegrationAuthority.ROAD_LANE) { color = "intersection".equals(d == null ? null : d.shape) ? new Color(245, 210, 80) : new Color(80, 165, 245); alpha = 0.28f; }
                        else if (ch == RoadGridIntegrationAuthority.SIDEWALK) { color = new Color(120, 220, 130); alpha = 0.20f; }
                    } else if (mode == 4) { // boundary
                        if (ch == InterstitialInfrastructureApi.VOID_SPACE) { color = new Color(120, 90, 200); alpha = 0.28f; }
                        else if (d != null && "exterior_maintenance_bulkhead".equals(d.family)) { color = new Color(240, 180, 75); alpha = 0.30f; }
                        else if (ch == '-') { color = new Color(85, 210, 190); alpha = 0.18f; }
                    } else if (mode == 5) { // descriptors
                        if (d != null && "fallback".equals(d.baseLayer)) { color = new Color(245, 70, 95); alpha = 0.36f; }
                        else if (d != null && d.hasOverlay()) { color = new Color(210, 100, 245); alpha = 0.22f; }
                    } else if (mode == 6) { // interactables
                        if (auditTileHasInteractable(x, y)) { color = new Color(90, 240, 170); alpha = 0.30f; }
                    } else if (mode == 7) { // containers
                        if (auditTileHasContainer(x, y)) { color = new Color(225, 185, 90); alpha = 0.32f; }
                    } else if (mode == 8) { // lights
                        if (auditTileHasLight(x, y)) { color = new Color(255, 238, 130); alpha = 0.36f; }
                    } else if (mode == 9) { // traps
                        if (auditTileHasTrap(x, y)) { color = new Color(245, 80, 80); alpha = 0.36f; }
                    } else if (mode == 10) { // entities
                        if (auditTileHasEntity(x, y)) { color = new Color(125, 180, 255); alpha = 0.34f; }
                    } else if (mode == 11) { // transitions
                        if (auditTileHasTransition(x, y, ch)) { color = new Color(255, 150, 75); alpha = 0.36f; }
                    }
                    if (color != null) {
                        g.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver.derive(alpha));
                        g.setColor(color);
                        g.fillRect(ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH, cellW, cellH);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        if (mode == 1 && auditSnapshot != null) {
            for (int i=0; i<auditSnapshot.findings.size(); i++) {
                SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.AuditFinding f = auditSnapshot.findings.get(i);
                if (f.x < camX || f.y < camY || f.x >= camX + cols || f.y >= camY + rows) continue;
                int rx = ox + (f.x - camX) * cellW, ry = oy + (f.y - camY) * cellH;
                boolean selected = i == Math.floorMod(auditFindingIndex, Math.max(1, auditSnapshot.findings.size()));
                g.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver.derive(selected ? 0.82f : 0.48f));
                g.setColor(f.severity.equals("ERROR") ? new Color(245, 75, 65) : new Color(245, 210, 75));
                g.setStroke(new BasicStroke(selected ? 3f : 1.5f));
                g.drawRect(rx + 1, ry + 1, Math.max(3, cellW - 2), Math.max(3, cellH - 2));
                if (selected) {
                    g.drawLine(rx, ry, rx + cellW, ry + cellH);
                    g.drawLine(rx + cellW, ry, rx, ry + cellH);
                }
            }
        }
        g.setStroke(oldStroke);
        g.setComposite(oldComposite);
    }


    boolean auditTileHasInteractable(int x, int y) {
        if (auditWorld == null) return false;
        MapObjectState mo = auditWorld.mapObjectAt(x, y);
        if (mo != null) return true;
        char ch = auditWorld.inBounds(x, y) ? auditWorld.tiles[x][y] : 0;
        return auditWorld.isDoorSymbol(ch) || ch == 'S' || ch == 'E' || ch == 'v' || ch == '<' || ch == '>';
    }

    boolean auditTileHasContainer(int x, int y) {
        if (auditWorld == null || auditWorld.mapObjects == null) return false;
        for (MapObjectState mo : auditWorld.mapObjects) {
            if (mo == null || mo.x != x || mo.y != y) continue;
            String low = ((mo.type == null ? "" : mo.type) + " " + (mo.label == null ? "" : mo.label) + " " + (mo.stockState == null ? "" : mo.stockState)).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
            if (low.contains("container") || low.contains("crate") || low.contains("stock") || low.contains("vault") || low.contains("cache") || low.contains("corpse")) return true;
        }
        char ch = auditWorld.inBounds(x, y) ? auditWorld.tiles[x][y] : 0;
        return ch == 'b' || ch == 's' || ch == 'q' || ch == '?' || ch == '$' || ch == 'r';
    }

    boolean auditTileHasLight(int x, int y) {
        if (auditWorld == null || auditWorld.lightSources == null) return false;
        for (ZoneLightSourceRecord l : auditWorld.lightSources) if (l != null && l.x == x && l.y == y) return true;
        return false;
    }

    boolean auditTileHasTrap(int x, int y) {
        if (auditWorld == null) return false;
        if (auditWorld.trapRecords != null) for (TrapRecord t : auditWorld.trapRecords) if (t != null && t.x == x && t.y == y) return true;
        if (auditWorld.mapObjects != null) for (MapObjectState mo : auditWorld.mapObjects) {
            if (mo == null || mo.x != x || mo.y != y) continue;
            String low = ((mo.type == null ? "" : mo.type) + " " + (mo.label == null ? "" : mo.label)).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
            if (low.contains("trap") || low.contains("mine") || low.contains("explosive") || low.contains("alarm")) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    boolean auditTileHasEntity(int x, int y) {
        return auditWorld != null && auditWorld.npcAt(x, y) != null;
    }

    boolean auditTileHasTransition(int x, int y, char ch) {
        if (auditWorld == null) return false;
        if (auditWorld.isDoorSymbol(ch) && (ch == 'D' || x <= 1 || y <= 1 || x >= auditWorld.w - 2 || y >= auditWorld.h - 2)) return true;
        return ch == 'S' || ch == 'E' || ch == 'v' || ch == '<' || ch == '>';
    }

    Rectangle zoneAuditDropdownOuterRect(UiLayout L) {
        if (L == null) L = uiLayout();
        ZoneType[] zones = ZoneType.values();
        int screenPad = Math.max(8, scaled(8));
        int cols = zones.length > 14 ? 2 : 1;
        int rowH = Math.max(22, Math.min(28, L.command.height / 24));
        int rows = Math.max(1, (int)Math.ceil(zones.length / (double)Math.max(1, cols)));
        int w = Math.min(Math.max(360, getWidth() - screenPad * 2), Math.max(300, cols * 190 + 36));
        int h = Math.min(Math.max(160, L.command.height - 18), Math.max(110, 20 + rows * rowH + Math.max(0, rows - 1) * 4));
        int x = Math.max(screenPad, L.command.x - w - 10);
        if (x + w > getWidth() - screenPad) x = Math.max(screenPad, getWidth() - screenPad - w);
        int y = Math.max(screenPad, L.command.y + 10);
        if (y + h > getHeight() - screenPad) y = Math.max(screenPad, getHeight() - screenPad - h);
        return new Rectangle(x, y, w, h);
    }

    Rectangle zoneAuditDropdownInnerRect(UiLayout L) {
        Rectangle r = zoneAuditDropdownOuterRect(L);
        return new Rectangle(r.x + 10, r.y + 10, Math.max(1, r.width - 20), Math.max(1, r.height - 20));
    }

    boolean isZoneAuditDropdownButton(ButtonBox b) {
        if (b == null || b.label == null || !auditZoneDropdownOpen || screen != Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT) return false;
        ZoneType[] zones = ZoneType.values();
        String label = b.label.replace("▶", "").trim();
        for (ZoneType z : zones) if (label.equals(z.label)) return true;
        return false;
    }

    void drawSectorAuditZoneDropdown(Graphics2D g, UiLayout L) {
        if (!auditZoneDropdownOpen || L == null) return;
        ZoneType[] zones = ZoneType.values();
        if (zones.length == 0) return;
        Rectangle outer = zoneAuditDropdownOuterRect(L);
        Rectangle inner = zoneAuditDropdownInnerRect(L);
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,232));
        g.fillRoundRect(outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height, 10, 10);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "zone-audit-zone-selector", outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-3f)));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int colGap = Math.max(6, Math.min(10, inner.width / 38));
        int rowGap = Math.max(3, Math.min(5, inner.height / 80));
        int cols = Math.max(1, Math.min(3, (inner.width + colGap) / 170));
        int rows = Math.max(1, (int)Math.ceil(zones.length / (double)cols));
        int cellW = Math.max(120, (inner.width - colGap * Math.max(0, cols - 1)) / cols);
        int cellH = Math.max(18, Math.min(25, (inner.height - rowGap * Math.max(0, rows - 1)) / rows));
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(outer.x + 6, outer.y + 6, outer.width - 12, outer.height - 12);
        for (int i = 0; i < zones.length; i++) {
            int col = i % cols;
            int row = i / cols;
            int x = inner.x + col * (cellW + colGap);
            int y = inner.y + row * (cellH + rowGap);
            ZoneType z = zones[i];
            boolean selected = i == auditZoneTypeIndex;
            g.setColor(selected ? new Color(60,48,24,235) : new Color(10,10,10,188));
            g.fillRoundRect(x, y, cellW, cellH, 6, 6);
            g.setColor(selected ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel((selected ? "▶ " : "") + z.label, fm, cellW - 10), x + 6, y + Math.max(13, fm.getAscent() + 2));
        }
        g.setClip(oldClip);
    }

    void drawSectorAuditCommandPanel(Graphics2D g, UiLayout L) {
        // 0.9.10iq: the sector-audit command frame is now button-only. The former
        // explanatory body copy lived under the buttons and made the right rail read
        // like a collision bug at Windows test density.
        drawRightPanelFrame(g);
    }

    void drawSectorAuditInfoPanel(Graphics2D g, UiLayout L) {
        Rectangle t = L.tactical;
        g.setColor(new Color(6,7,7,238));
        g.fillRect(t.x, t.y, t.width, t.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, t.x, t.y, t.width, t.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "zone-audit-report", t.x, t.y, t.width, t.height);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(9f, smallFont.getSize2D()-2f)));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "ZONE AUDIT REPORT", t.x + 12, t.y + 20);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-3f)));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (auditWorld == null) lines.add("No audit world generated.");
        else {
            char ch = auditWorld.inBounds(auditCursorX, auditCursorY) ? auditWorld.tiles[auditCursorX][auditCursorY] : '?';
            CompiledTileDescriptor d = TileDataCompilationAuthority.resolve(auditWorld, auditCursorX, auditCursorY, ch);
            lines.add("Zone: " + auditWorld.zoneType.label + " | " + auditWorld.w + "x" + auditWorld.h + " | weight " + WorldGenerationApi.worldgenWeightBandLabel(auditZoneSizeIndex) + " | density " + WorldSetupSettings.ZONE_DENSITY[Math.max(0, Math.min(3, auditZoneDensityIndex))] + " | overlay " + SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.overlayLabel(auditOverlayMode) + ".");
            SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.Step step = currentAuditTraceStep();
            if (step != null) lines.add(step.line(auditTraceSteps == null ? 0 : auditTraceSteps.size()) + (auditTracePlaying ? " | playing." : " | paused."));
            lines.add("Cursor: " + auditCursorX + "," + auditCursorY + " glyph '" + ch + "' room " + auditWorld.roomIdAt(auditCursorX, auditCursorY) + " faction " + auditWorld.roomFaction(auditWorld.roomIdAt(auditCursorX, auditCursorY)).label + ".");
            if (d != null) lines.add("Tile descriptor: " + d.inspectLine() + ".");
            lines.addAll(auditTileInspectionLines(auditCursorX, auditCursorY));
            lines.addAll(SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.compactPanelLines(auditSnapshot, auditFindingIndex));
            lines.add(auditReport);
        }
        int y = t.y + 42;
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(t.x + 8, t.y + 28, t.width - 16, t.height - 36);
        FontMetrics reportMetrics = g.getFontMetrics();
        for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap(String.join(" ", lines), Math.max(54, (t.width - 24) / Math.max(6, reportMetrics.charWidth('W'))))) {
            if (y > t.y + t.height - 8) break;
            drawUiTextLine(g, line, t.x + 12, y);
            y += Math.max(12, reportMetrics.getHeight() + 1);
        }
        g.setClip(old);
    }

    Rectangle multiplayerMenuPanelRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int marginX = Math.max(34, Math.min(70, W / 22));
        int marginY = Math.max(44, Math.min(76, H / 14));
        int panelW = Math.min(1280, Math.max(760, W - marginX * 2));
        int panelH = Math.min(Math.max(520, H - marginY * 2), H - Math.max(72, marginY));
        return new Rectangle((W - panelW) / 2, Math.max(42, (H - panelH) / 2), panelW, panelH);
    }

    Rectangle multiplayerContentRect(Rectangle panel) {
        int pad = Math.max(24, Math.min(36, panel.width / 32));
        int gap = Math.max(16, Math.min(24, panel.width / 52));
        int actionW = Math.max(270, Math.min(390, (panel.width - pad * 2 - gap) / 3));
        int contentW = Math.max(360, panel.width - pad * 2 - gap - actionW);
        return new Rectangle(panel.x + pad, panel.y + 66, contentW, Math.max(180, panel.height - 132));
    }

    Rectangle multiplayerActionRect(Rectangle panel) {
        Rectangle content = multiplayerContentRect(panel);
        int gap = Math.max(16, Math.min(24, panel.width / 52));
        int x = content.x + content.width + gap;
        return new Rectangle(x, content.y, Math.max(240, panel.x + panel.width - 24 - x), content.height);
    }

    void drawMultiplayerSurface(Graphics2D g) {
        multiplayerPainter.paint(g, this);
    }

    // Old manual rendering loop removed algorithmically
    void REPLACED_OLD_MULTIPLAYER(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth();
        Rectangle panel = multiplayerMenuPanelRect();
        Rectangle content = multiplayerContentRect(panel);
        Rectangle action = multiplayerActionRect(panel);
        g.setColor(new Color(0, 0, 0, 196));
        g.fillRoundRect(panel.x, panel.y, panel.width, panel.height, 16, 16);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, panel.x, panel.y, panel.width, panel.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "multiplayer-menu", panel.x, panel.y, panel.width, panel.height);
        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(24f, Math.min(38f, panel.height / 12f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, "MULTIPLAYER CONNECTION", W / 2, panel.y + 42);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();

        g.setColor(new Color(12, 14, 13, 226));
        g.fillRoundRect(content.x, content.y, content.width, content.height, 12, 12);
        g.setColor(new Color(145, 118, 64, 135));
        g.drawRoundRect(content.x, content.y, content.width, content.height, 12, 12);
        g.setColor(new Color(12, 14, 13, 220));
        g.fillRoundRect(action.x, action.y, action.width, action.height, 12, 12);
        g.setColor(new Color(145, 118, 64, 125));
        g.drawRoundRect(action.x, action.y, action.width, action.height, 12, 12);

        int leftX = content.x + 14;
        int textW = Math.max(240, content.width - 28);
        int y = content.y + 26;
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(content.x + 8, content.y + 8, content.width - 16, content.height - 16);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        g.drawString("Direct address:", leftX, y); y += fm.getHeight() + 4;
        String direct = (multiplayerMenu.inputActive() ? "> " : "  ") + multiplayerMenu.directInput() + (multiplayerMenu.inputActive() && (System.currentTimeMillis() / 450) % 2 == 0 ? "_" : "");
        g.setColor(new Color(18, 22, 20, 230));
        g.fillRoundRect(leftX, y - fm.getAscent() - 5, textW, fm.getHeight() + 12, 8, 8);
        g.setColor(multiplayerMenu.inputActive() ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        g.drawString(GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(direct, fm, Math.max(220, textW - 12)), leftX + 8, y);
        y += fm.getHeight() + 24;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        g.drawString("IPv4 example: 192.168.1.10:25565", leftX, y); y += fm.getHeight();
        g.drawString("IPv6 example: [2001:db8::1]:25565", leftX, y); y += fm.getHeight() + 18;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        g.drawString("Recent servers:", leftX, y); y += fm.getHeight() + 4;
        java.util.List<MultiplayerMenuController.ConnectionHistoryItem> history = multiplayerMenu.history();
        for (int i = 0; i < Math.min(5, history.size()); i++) {
            boolean selected = i == multiplayerMenu.historyIndex();
            g.setColor(selected ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            g.drawString((selected ? "> " : "  ") + GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(history.get(i).shortLine(), fm, Math.max(220, textW - 8)), leftX, y);
            y += fm.getHeight() + 2;
        }
        if (history.isEmpty()) { g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM)); g.drawString("  No connection history yet.", leftX, y); y += fm.getHeight() + 2; }
        y += 14;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        g.drawString("Favorites:", leftX, y); y += fm.getHeight() + 4;
        java.util.List<MultiplayerMenuController.FavoriteServer> favs = multiplayerMenu.favorites();
        for (int i = 0; i < Math.min(5, favs.size()); i++) {
            boolean selected = i == multiplayerMenu.favoriteIndex();
            g.setColor(selected ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            g.drawString((selected ? "> " : "  ") + GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(favs.get(i).shortLine(), fm, Math.max(220, textW - 8)), leftX, y);
            y += fm.getHeight() + 2;
        }
        if (favs.isEmpty()) { g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM)); g.drawString("  No favorite servers saved.", leftX, y); y += fm.getHeight() + 2; }

        int statusY = Math.max(y + 14, content.y + content.height - 74);
        g.setColor(new Color(18, 22, 20, 225));
        g.fillRoundRect(leftX, statusY, textW, 60, 10, 10);
        g.setColor(new Color(145, 118, 64, 120));
        g.drawRoundRect(leftX, statusY, textW, 60, 10, 10);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        java.util.List<String> wrapped = GuiLayoutApi.wrapText(multiplayerMenu.status(), fm, Math.max(220, textW - 18));
        int yy = statusY + 20;
        for (int i = 0; i < Math.min(2, wrapped.size()); i++) { g.drawString(wrapped.get(i), leftX + 9, yy); yy += fm.getHeight(); }
        g.setColor(multiplayerMenu.hasActiveHost() ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        g.drawString(GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(multiplayerMenu.activeHostLine(), fm, Math.max(220, textW - 18)), leftX + 9, statusY + 50);
        g.setClip(oldClip);

        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(9f, smallFont.getSize2D() - 2f)));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, "CONNECTION COMMANDS", action.x + action.width / 2, action.y + 22);
    }

    void drawMenu(Graphics2D g) {

    }

        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();

        g.setColor(new Color(130,105,55,150));
        g.drawRoundRect(panelX, panelY, panelW, panelH, 9, 9);
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "launcher-runtime-compact", panelX, panelY, panelW, panelH);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(7f, Math.min(8.5f, smallFont.getSize2D()-4f))));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineY = panelY + 14;
        int maxLines = Math.max(1, (panelH - 8) / Math.max(10, fm.getHeight()));
        for (int i=0; i<shellLines.size() && i<maxLines; i++) {
            g.setColor(i == 0 ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(shellLines.get(i), fm, panelW - 20), cx, lineY);
            lineY += Math.max(10, fm.getHeight());
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
    }

    void drawIntroCrawl(Graphics2D g) {
