    // Old manual rendering loop removed algorithmically
    void REPLACED_OLD_INTRO_CRAWL(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        long elapsed = Math.max(0L, System.currentTimeMillis() - introCrawlStartMillis);
        BufferedImage backdrop = images.get("new_world_backdrop_rebase");
        if (backdrop != null) {
            double scale = Math.max(W / (double)Math.max(1, backdrop.getWidth()), H / (double)Math.max(1, backdrop.getHeight()));
            int bw = Math.max(W, (int)Math.round(backdrop.getWidth() * scale));
            int bh = Math.max(H, (int)Math.round(backdrop.getHeight() * scale));
            g.drawImage(backdrop, (W-bw)/2, (H-bh)/2, bw, bh, null);
        } else {
            g.setColor(new Color(5, 6, 8)); g.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        }
        drawIntroCloudLayer(g, images.get("clouds_slow_rebase"), elapsed, 0.012, 34, 0.48f);
        drawIntroCloudLayer(g, images.get("clouds_fast_rebase"), elapsed, 0.026, 0, 0.38f);
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,126)); g.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, 26, 26, W-52, H-52, "outer");

        int panelW = Math.min(Math.max(520, W - 240), W - 130);
        int panelX = (W - panelW) / 2;
        int panelY = Math.max(96, H / 5);
        int panelH = Math.max(280, H - panelY - 86);
        g.setColor(new Color(5,7,7,186)); g.fillRoundRect(panelX, panelY, panelW, panelH, 18, 18);
        g.setColor(new Color(156,132,78,190)); g.drawRoundRect(panelX, panelY, panelW, panelH, 18, 18);

        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(26f, Math.min(42f, H / 14f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE));
        center(g, "NEW WORLD INSERTION", W/2, Math.max(60, panelY - 44));
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(11f, Math.min(15f, H / 48f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, active == null ? "Unnamed operator" : active.name + " // " + active.job, W/2, Math.max(82, panelY - 18));

        if (introCrawlLines.isEmpty()) introCrawlLines = images.loadIntroCrawlLines();
        Font crawlFont = smallFont.deriveFont(Font.PLAIN, Math.max(13f, Math.min(17f, H / 42f)));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics(crawlFont);
        ArrayList<String> wrapped = new ArrayList<>();
        int wrapChars = Math.max(38, (panelW - 84) / Math.max(7, fm.charWidth('M')));
        for (String line : introCrawlLines) {
            String cleaned = line == null ? "" : line.trim();
            if (cleaned.isEmpty()) { wrapped.add(""); continue; }
            wrapped.addAll(TextSurfaceApi.wrap(cleaned, wrapChars));
            wrapped.add("");
        }
        while (!wrapped.isEmpty() && wrapped.get(wrapped.size()-1).isEmpty()) wrapped.remove(wrapped.size()-1);
        if (wrapped.isEmpty()) wrapped.add("The arcology opens beneath you.");

        final long leadInMs = 900L;
        final long blankMs = 760L;
        final long linePauseMs = 460L;
        final long charMs = introCrawlCharMillisForTarget(wrapped, leadInMs, blankMs, linePauseMs, INTRO_CRAWL_TEXT_TARGET_MS);
        int lineH = Math.max(24, fm.getHeight() + 8);
        long t = Math.max(0L, elapsed - leadInMs);
        long cursor = 0L;
        int currentLine = 0;
        int visibleChars = 0;
        float liftFraction = 0f;
        boolean finished = false;
        for (int i = 0; i < wrapped.size(); i++) {
            String line = wrapped.get(i);
            long typeMs = line.isEmpty() ? blankMs : Math.max(780L, line.length() * charMs);
            if (t < cursor) {
                currentLine = Math.max(0, i - 1);
                visibleChars = wrapped.get(currentLine).length();
                liftFraction = 0f;
                break;
            }
            if (t < cursor + typeMs) {
                currentLine = i;
                if (line.isEmpty()) visibleChars = 0;
                else if (options.instantDialogueText) visibleChars = line.length();
                else visibleChars = Math.max(0, Math.min(line.length(), (int)((t - cursor) / Math.max(1L, charMs))));
                liftFraction = 0f;
                break;
            }
            if (t < cursor + typeMs + linePauseMs) {
                currentLine = i;
                visibleChars = line.length();
                liftFraction = (float)((t - cursor - typeMs) / (double)Math.max(1L, linePauseMs));
                break;
            }
            cursor += typeMs + linePauseMs;
            if (i == wrapped.size() - 1) {
                currentLine = i;
                visibleChars = line.length();
                liftFraction = 1f;
                finished = true;
            }
        }

        Graphics2D clip = (Graphics2D)g.create();
        clip.setClip(panelX + 28, panelY + 22, panelW - 56, panelH - 44);
        clip.setFont(crawlFont);
        int baseY = panelY + panelH - 44;
        int lift = Math.round(liftFraction * lineH);
        for (int i = Math.max(0, currentLine - 22); i <= currentLine && i < wrapped.size(); i++) {
            String line = wrapped.get(i);
            String shown = line;
            if (i == currentLine && visibleChars < line.length()) shown = line.substring(0, Math.max(0, Math.min(visibleChars, line.length())));
            int yy = baseY - (currentLine - i) * lineH - lift;
            if (yy < panelY + 18 || yy > panelY + panelH - 8) continue;
            if (shown.isEmpty()) continue;
            int distanceFromCenter = Math.abs((panelY + panelH / 2) - yy);
            int alpha = Math.max(72, Math.min(238, 238 - distanceFromCenter / 3));
            clip.setColor(options.highContrastText ? Color.WHITE : new Color(224, 213, 166, alpha));
            center(clip, shown, panelX + panelW/2, yy);
        }
        // Subtle typewriter cursor on the actively printing line. It is centered
        // with the line so the crawl remains cinematic instead of becoming a
        // left-aligned terminal dump.
        if (currentLine < wrapped.size()) {
            String line = wrapped.get(currentLine);
            if (!line.isEmpty() && visibleChars < line.length() && ((elapsed / 360L) % 2L == 0L)) {
                String shown = line.substring(0, Math.max(0, Math.min(visibleChars, line.length())));
                int yy = baseY - lift;
                int sw = clip.getFontMetrics().stringWidth(shown);
                int cx = panelX + panelW / 2;
                int cursorX = cx - sw / 2 + sw + 4;
                if (yy >= panelY + 18 && yy <= panelY + panelH - 8) {
                    clip.setColor(new Color(224, 213, 166, 185));
                    clip.drawLine(cursorX, yy - fm.getAscent() + 2, cursorX, yy + 3);
                }
            }
        }
        clip.dispose();

        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.PLAIN, Math.max(10f, Math.min(12f, H / 62f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        center(g, "SKIP remains available in the lower right.", W/2, H-54);

        long textTotalMs = introCrawlTextDurationMillis(wrapped, leadInMs, charMs, blankMs, linePauseMs);
        long fullCrawlMs = Math.max(textTotalMs + INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_TAIL_SAFETY_MS, INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_EXPECTED_MS + INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_TAIL_SAFETY_MS);
        if (elapsed > fullCrawlMs) continueFromIntroCrawl();
    }

    long introCrawlTextDurationMillis(ArrayList<String> wrapped, long leadInMs, long charMs, long blankMs, long linePauseMs) {
        long totalMs = leadInMs;
        for (String line : wrapped) totalMs += (line.isEmpty() ? blankMs : Math.max(780L, line.length() * charMs)) + linePauseMs;
        return totalMs;
    }

    long introCrawlCharMillisForTarget(ArrayList<String> wrapped, long leadInMs, long blankMs, long linePauseMs, long targetMs) {
        long fixedMs = leadInMs;
        long characterCount = 0L;
        for (String line : wrapped) {
            fixedMs += linePauseMs;
            if (line.isEmpty()) fixedMs += blankMs;
            else characterCount += Math.max(1, line.length());
        }
        if (characterCount <= 0L) return 55L;
        long budget = Math.max(characterCount, targetMs - fixedMs);
        return Math.max(34L, Math.min(96L, Math.round(budget / (double)characterCount)));
    }

    void drawIntroCloudLayer(Graphics2D g, BufferedImage cloud, long elapsed, double pxPerMs, int yOffset, float alpha) {
        if (cloud == null) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D)g.create();
        gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.max(0.05f, Math.min(1f, alpha))));
        int W = getWidth();
        int targetH = Math.max(120, getHeight() / 3);
        int targetW = Math.max(1, cloud.getWidth() * targetH / Math.max(1, cloud.getHeight()));
        int y = 28 + yOffset;
        int offset = (int)Math.floor((elapsed * pxPerMs) % Math.max(1, targetW));
        for (int x = -offset - targetW; x < W + targetW; x += targetW) gg.drawImage(cloud, x, y, targetW, targetH, null);
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void continueFromIntroCrawl() {
        logEvent("New World insertion crawl acknowledged.");
        if (introCrawlQueuedZoneSplash) setScreen(Screen.ZONE_SPLASH);
        else setScreen(Screen.GAME);
    }


    LinkedHashMap<String, KnowledgeTree> liveKnowledgeBranches() {
        return KnowledgeMenu.createBranches(knowledgeCredits, unlockedKnowledges);
    }

    KnowledgeTree activeKnowledgeTreeSnapshot() {
        LinkedHashMap<String, KnowledgeTree> branches = liveKnowledgeBranches();
        KnowledgeTree tree = branches.get(activeKnowledgeBranchId);
        if (tree == null && !branches.isEmpty()) {
            tree = branches.values().iterator().next();
            activeKnowledgeBranchId = tree.id();
        }
        return tree;
    }

    KnowledgeNode selectedKnowledgeNode(KnowledgeTree tree) {
        if (tree == null || selectedKnowledgeNodeId == null) return null;
        return tree.node(selectedKnowledgeNodeId);
    }

    Rectangle knowledgeModalRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int mx = Math.max(34, W / 28);
        int my = Math.max(38, H / 22);
        return new Rectangle(mx, my, Math.max(420, W - mx * 2), Math.max(320, H - my * 2));
    }

    Rectangle knowledgeBranchBarRect() {
        Rectangle r = knowledgeModalRect();
        return new Rectangle(r.x + 22, r.y + 52, r.width - 44, 34);
    }

    Rectangle knowledgeLeftPaneRect() {
        Rectangle r = knowledgeModalRect();
        int w = Math.max(210, Math.min(275, r.width / 4));
        return new Rectangle(r.x + 22, r.y + 98, w, r.height - 124);
    }

    Rectangle knowledgeRightPaneRect() {
        Rectangle r = knowledgeModalRect();
        int w = Math.max(260, Math.min(330, r.width / 3));
        return new Rectangle(r.x + r.width - 22 - w, r.y + 98, w, r.height - 124);
    }

    Rectangle knowledgeCanvasRect() {
        Rectangle left = knowledgeLeftPaneRect();
        Rectangle right = knowledgeRightPaneRect();
        Rectangle modal = knowledgeModalRect();
        int gap = 14;
        int x = left.x + left.width + gap;
        int w = Math.max(180, right.x - gap - x);
        return new Rectangle(x, left.y, w, left.height);
    }

    void resetKnowledgeTreeView() {
        knowledgeTreeScale = 1.0;
        knowledgeTreePanX = 70.0;
        knowledgeTreePanY = 68.0;
        knowledgeTreeLastDrag = null;
        knowledgeTreeDragging = false;
    }

    void panKnowledgeTree(int dx, int dy) {
        knowledgeTreePanX += dx;
        knowledgeTreePanY += dy;
    }

    void zoomKnowledgeTreeAt(int sx, int sy, double wheelRotation) {
        Rectangle canvas = knowledgeCanvasRect();
        if (!canvas.contains(sx, sy)) { scrollActivePanel((int)Math.signum(wheelRotation), false); return; }
        double old = knowledgeTreeScale;
        double next = Math.max(0.35, Math.min(2.75, old * Math.pow(1.10, -wheelRotation)));
        if (Math.abs(next - old) < 0.0001) return;
        double wx = (sx - canvas.x - knowledgeTreePanX) / old;
        double wy = (sy - canvas.y - knowledgeTreePanY) / old;
        knowledgeTreeScale = next;
        knowledgeTreePanX = sx - canvas.x - wx * next;
        knowledgeTreePanY = sy - canvas.y - wy * next;
        repaint();
    }

    void rebuildKnowledgeScreenButtons() {
        Rectangle modal = knowledgeModalRect();
        Rectangle bar = knowledgeBranchBarRect();
        LinkedHashMap<String, KnowledgeTree> branches = liveKnowledgeBranches();
        int count = Math.max(1, branches.size());
        int gap = Math.max(6, Math.min(10, bar.width / 80));
        int tabW = Math.max(82, (bar.width - gap * Math.max(0, count - 1)) / count);
        int i = 0;
        for (KnowledgeTree tree : branches.values()) {
            final String id = tree.id();
            int bx = bar.x + i * (tabW + gap);
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox(tree.displayName().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT), bx, bar.y, tabW, bar.height, "Switch Knowledge Tree branch inside the game UI.", () -> { activeKnowledgeBranchId = id; selectedKnowledgeNodeId = null; resetKnowledgeTreeView(); repaint(); }));
            i++;
        }
        Rectangle right = knowledgeRightPaneRect();
        Rectangle left = knowledgeLeftPaneRect();
        KnowledgeTree tree = activeKnowledgeTreeSnapshot();
        KnowledgeNode node = selectedKnowledgeNode(tree);
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("UNLOCK NODE", right.x + 18, right.y + right.height - 58, Math.max(120, right.width - 36), 34, "Spend character knowledge credits to unlock the selected node.", this::attemptKnowledgeUnlock));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("CENTER TREE", left.x + 18, left.y + left.height - 48, Math.max(120, left.width - 36), 30, "Reset pan and zoom for the active tree.", () -> { resetKnowledgeTreeView(); repaint(); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("BACK", modal.x + 18, modal.y + 14, 106, 30, "Close Knowledge and return to the previous in-game surface.", this::closeKnowledgeScreen));
    }

    void closeKnowledgeScreen() {
        Screen target = knowledgeReturnScreen == null ? Screen.CHARACTER : knowledgeReturnScreen;
        if (target == Screen.KNOWLEDGE || target == Screen.BOOT || target == Screen.LOADING) target = world == null ? Screen.CHARACTER : Screen.GAME;
        setScreen(target);
    }

    void attemptKnowledgeUnlock() {
        KnowledgeTree tree = activeKnowledgeTreeSnapshot();
        KnowledgeNode node = selectedKnowledgeNode(tree);
        if (tree == null || node == null) { logEvent("Knowledge unlock blocked: select a node first."); repaint(); return; }
        if (unlockedKnowledges.contains(node.id())) { logEvent("Knowledge already known: " + node.name() + "."); repaint(); return; }
        if (!tree.prerequisitesMet(node)) { logEvent("Knowledge unlock blocked: prerequisites are not met for " + node.name() + "."); repaint(); return; }
        if (knowledgeCredits < node.pointCost()) { logEvent("Knowledge unlock blocked: " + node.name() + " costs " + node.pointCost() + " knowledge credit(s); you have " + knowledgeCredits + "."); repaint(); return; }
        purchaseKnowledge(node.id(), node.pointCost());
        selectedKnowledgeNodeId = node.id();
        repaint();
    }

    boolean handleKnowledgeTreeClick(int mx, int my) {
        Rectangle canvas = knowledgeCanvasRect();
        if (!canvas.contains(mx, my)) return false;
        KnowledgeTree tree = activeKnowledgeTreeSnapshot();
        KnowledgeNode hit = knowledgeNodeAt(tree, mx, my);
        if (hit != null) {
            selectedKnowledgeNodeId = hit.id();
            sounds.play("tab", options);
            repaint();
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    KnowledgeNode knowledgeNodeAt(KnowledgeTree tree, int mx, int my) {
        if (tree == null) return null;
        Rectangle canvas = knowledgeCanvasRect();
        double wx = (mx - canvas.x - knowledgeTreePanX) / knowledgeTreeScale;
        double wy = (my - canvas.y - knowledgeTreePanY) / knowledgeTreeScale;
        for (KnowledgeNode n : tree.nodes()) {
            if (Math.abs(wx - n.x()) <= 78.0 && Math.abs(wy - n.y()) <= 29.0) return n;
        }
        return null;
    }

    void handleKnowledgeKeyPressed(int code) {
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_ESCAPE) { closeKnowledgeScreen(); return; }
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_ENTER || code == KeyEvent.VK_SPACE || code == KeyEvent.VK_E) { attemptKnowledgeUnlock(); return; }
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_HOME) { resetKnowledgeTreeView(); repaint(); return; }
        LinkedHashMap<String, KnowledgeTree> branches = liveKnowledgeBranches();
        ArrayList<String> ids = new ArrayList<>(branches.keySet());
        int idx = Math.max(0, ids.indexOf(activeKnowledgeBranchId));
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_LEFT || code == KeyEvent.VK_A) { activeKnowledgeBranchId = ids.get(Math.max(0, idx - 1)); selectedKnowledgeNodeId = null; resetKnowledgeTreeView(); repaint(); return; }
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_RIGHT || code == KeyEvent.VK_D) { activeKnowledgeBranchId = ids.get(Math.min(ids.size() - 1, idx + 1)); selectedKnowledgeNodeId = null; resetKnowledgeTreeView(); repaint(); return; }
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_UP || code == KeyEvent.VK_W) { knowledgeTreePanY += 24; repaint(); return; }
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_DOWN || code == KeyEvent.VK_S) { knowledgeTreePanY -= 24; repaint(); return; }
    }

    void drawKnowledgeScreen(Graphics2D g) {
        drawBackground(g);
        Rectangle modal = knowledgeModalRect();
        drawPanelBox(g, modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height, "F9187 KNOWLEDGE TREE");
        g.setFont(titleFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE));
        center(g, "CHARACTER KNOWLEDGE / PROGRESSION", modal.x + modal.width / 2, modal.y + 36);
        drawKnowledgeBranchTabs(g);
        drawKnowledgeLeftPane(g);
        drawKnowledgeCanvas(g);
        drawKnowledgeRightPane(g);
    }

    void drawKnowledgeBranchTabs(Graphics2D g) {
        Rectangle bar = knowledgeBranchBarRect();
        LinkedHashMap<String, KnowledgeTree> branches = liveKnowledgeBranches();
        int count = Math.max(1, branches.size());
        int gap = Math.max(6, Math.min(10, bar.width / 80));
        int tabW = Math.max(82, (bar.width - gap * Math.max(0, count - 1)) / count);
        int i = 0;
        for (KnowledgeTree tree : branches.values()) {
            int x = bar.x + i * (tabW + gap);
            boolean active = tree.id().equals(activeKnowledgeBranchId);
            g.setColor(active ? new Color(34, 46, 32, 232) : new Color(10, 13, 12, 220));
            g.fillRoundRect(x, bar.y, tabW, bar.height, 10, 10);
            g.setColor(active ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            g.drawRoundRect(x, bar.y, tabW, bar.height, 10, 10);
            g.setFont(smallFont);
            center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(tree.displayName(), g.getFontMetrics(), tabW - 8), x + tabW / 2, bar.y + 22);
            i++;
        }
    }

    void drawKnowledgeLeftPane(Graphics2D g) {
        Rectangle r = knowledgeLeftPaneRect();
        drawPanelBox(g, r.x, r.y, r.width, r.height, "F9188 POINTS");
        KnowledgeTree tree = activeKnowledgeTreeSnapshot();
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        g.drawString("Credits: " + knowledgeCredits, r.x + 18, r.y + 58);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        lines.add("Active branch: " + (tree == null ? "None" : tree.displayName()) + ".");
        lines.add(tree == null ? "No nodes loaded." : tree.unlockedCount() + " / " + tree.nodes().size() + " known. " + tree.availableCount() + " currently affordable and prerequisite-ready.");
        lines.add("");
        lines.add("How to earn more points: survive, work, fight, research, operate labs, complete contracts, study slates, and pass XP thresholds. This is character-owned progression inside the game, not an Infopedia purchase screen and not a separate external utility window.");
        drawWrappedPanelLines(g, lines, r.x + 18, r.y + 86, r.width - 36, r.height - 145);
    }

    void drawKnowledgeRightPane(Graphics2D g) {
        Rectangle r = knowledgeRightPaneRect();
        drawPanelBox(g, r.x, r.y, r.width, r.height, "F9189 INSPECTOR");
        KnowledgeTree tree = activeKnowledgeTreeSnapshot();
        KnowledgeNode node = selectedKnowledgeNode(tree);
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (node == null) {
            lines.add("Select a node in the center tree.");
            lines.add("Green is known. Yellow is unlockable. Gray is still locked by prerequisites or credits.");
        } else {
            KnowledgeTree.NodeState state = tree.stateOf(node);
            lines.add(node.name());
            lines.add("Cost: " + node.costLabel());
            lines.add("State: " + switch (state) { case UNLOCKED -> "Known / unlocked"; case AVAILABLE -> "Available to unlock"; case LOCKED -> "Locked"; });
            lines.add("");
            String detail = node.longDescription() == null || node.longDescription().isBlank() ? node.shortDescription() : node.longDescription();
            for (String raw : detail.split("\\n")) lines.add(raw);
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        drawWrappedPanelLines(g, lines, r.x + 18, r.y + 58, r.width - 36, r.height - 130);
    }

    void drawKnowledgeCanvas(Graphics2D g) {
        Rectangle canvas = knowledgeCanvasRect();
        KnowledgeTree tree = activeKnowledgeTreeSnapshot();
        g.setColor(new Color(4, 7, 6, 240));
        g.fillRect(canvas.x, canvas.y, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, canvas.x, canvas.y, canvas.width, canvas.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "knowledge-canvas", canvas.x, canvas.y, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        try {
            gg.setClip(canvas.x + 8, canvas.y + 8, canvas.width - 16, canvas.height - 16);
            gg.translate(canvas.x + knowledgeTreePanX, canvas.y + knowledgeTreePanY);
            gg.scale(knowledgeTreeScale, knowledgeTreeScale);
            drawKnowledgeTreeGrid(gg, canvas);
            if (tree != null) drawKnowledgeTreeGraph(gg, tree);
        } finally {
            gg.dispose();
            g.setClip(oldClip);
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        g.drawString("Mouse wheel zooms. Drag pans. Click a node to inspect. Enter/Space unlocks selected.", canvas.x + 18, canvas.y + canvas.height - 18);
    }

    void drawKnowledgeTreeGrid(Graphics2D g, Rectangle canvas) {
        g.setColor(new Color(18, 20, 18));
        int step = 48;
        for (int x = -500; x < 1800; x += step) g.drawLine(x, -500, x, 1600);
        for (int y = -500; y < 1600; y += step) g.drawLine(-500, y, 1800, y);
    }

    void drawKnowledgeTreeGraph(Graphics2D g, KnowledgeTree tree) {
        Map<String, KnowledgeNode> byId = tree.nodeMap();
        g.setStroke(new BasicStroke(4.0f, BasicStroke.CAP_ROUND, BasicStroke.JOIN_ROUND));
        for (KnowledgeNode node : tree.nodes()) {
            for (String preId : node.prerequisiteNodeIds()) {
                KnowledgeNode pre = byId.get(preId);
                if (pre == null) continue;
                KnowledgeTree.NodeState state = tree.stateOf(node);
                g.setColor(pre.unlocked() && node.unlocked() ? new Color(40, 150, 70) : (state == KnowledgeTree.NodeState.AVAILABLE ? new Color(194, 166, 55) : new Color(83, 83, 78)));
                g.drawLine((int)pre.x(), (int)pre.y(), (int)node.x(), (int)node.y());
            }
        }
        for (KnowledgeNode node : tree.nodes()) drawKnowledgeTreeNode(g, tree, node);
    }

    void drawKnowledgeTreeNode(Graphics2D g, KnowledgeTree tree, KnowledgeNode node) {
        KnowledgeTree.NodeState state = tree.stateOf(node);
        boolean selected = node.id().equals(selectedKnowledgeNodeId);
        int x = (int)Math.round(node.x() - 78.0);
        int y = (int)Math.round(node.y() - 29.0);
        Color fill = switch (state) { case UNLOCKED -> new Color(30, 112, 55); case AVAILABLE -> new Color(156, 130, 34); case LOCKED -> new Color(55, 56, 54); };
        Color border = selected ? new Color(230, 220, 150) : switch (state) { case UNLOCKED -> new Color(88, 218, 105); case AVAILABLE -> new Color(245, 215, 78); case LOCKED -> new Color(116, 116, 110); };
        g.setColor(fill);
        g.fillRoundRect(x, y, 156, 58, 18, 18);
        g.setStroke(new BasicStroke(selected ? 4.0f : 2.4f));
        g.setColor(border);
        g.drawRoundRect(x, y, 156, 58, 18, 18);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        String title = fitText(node.name(), fm, 138);
        String cost = state == KnowledgeTree.NodeState.UNLOCKED ? "KNOWN" : "Cost " + node.pointCost();
        g.setColor(new Color(245, 242, 205));
        g.drawString(title, x + 10, y + 25);
        g.setColor(state == KnowledgeTree.NodeState.LOCKED ? new Color(190, 188, 170) : new Color(255, 242, 156));
        g.drawString(cost, x + 10, y + 45);
    }

    static String fitText(String text, FontMetrics fm, int width) {
        if (text == null) return "";
        if (fm.stringWidth(text) <= width) return text;
        String suffix = "…";
        String t = text;
        while (!t.isEmpty() && fm.stringWidth(t + suffix) > width) t = t.substring(0, t.length() - 1);
        return t + suffix;
    }

    void drawCharacter(Graphics2D g) {
        Candidate c = candidates.get(candidateIndex);
        JobProfile jp = JobProfile.get(c.jobs.get(jobIndex));
        boolean validJob = jp.meets(c);
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.BACKGROUND));
        g.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, 20, 20, W-40, H-40, "outer");
        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(24f, Math.min(38f, H / 15f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE)); center(g, "SELECT THE UNFORTUNATE", W/2, Math.max(54, H/10));

        int margin = Math.max(24, W / 34);
        int topY = Math.max(86, H / 7);
        int bh = Math.max(28, Math.min(38, H / 17));
        int gap = Math.max(8, W / 120);
        int nameY = topY + bh + 10;
        int colTop = nameY + 86;
        int colH = Math.max(210, H - colTop - 44);
        int availW = W - margin * 2 - gap * 2;
        int rangesW = Math.max(120, Math.min(160, availW / 5));
        int dossierW = Math.max(220, Math.min(310, availW / 3));
        int statsW = Math.max(260, availW - rangesW - dossierW - gap * 2);
        int rangesX = margin;
        int statsX = rangesX + rangesW + gap;
        int dossierX = statsX + statsW + gap;
        if (dossierX + dossierW > W - margin) {
            dossierW = Math.max(210, W - margin - dossierX);
            statsW = Math.max(250, dossierX - gap - statsX);
        }

        // Compact portrait + editable name band. The portrait is intentionally scaled so it no longer steals the central screen.
        int portraitSizeW = Math.max(62, Math.min(86, H / 6));
        int portraitX = margin + 10;
        int portraitY = nameY - 4;
        Graphics2D pg = (Graphics2D)g.create();
        double ps = portraitSizeW / 150.0;
        pg.translate(portraitX, portraitY);
        pg.scale(ps, ps);
        drawPortrait(pg, 0, 0, c);
        pg.dispose();
        int nameW = Math.min(460, Math.max(250, W - portraitX - portraitSizeW - margin - 32));
        characterNameEditRect.setBounds(Math.max(portraitX + portraitSizeW + 22, W - margin - nameW - 10), nameY + 2, nameW, 34);
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(characterNameEditActive ? new Color(70, 58, 34) : new Color(28, 25, 22));
        g.fillRoundRect(characterNameEditRect.x, characterNameEditRect.y, characterNameEditRect.width, characterNameEditRect.height, 10, 10);
        g.setColor(characterNameEditActive ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        g.drawRoundRect(characterNameEditRect.x, characterNameEditRect.y, characterNameEditRect.width, characterNameEditRect.height, 10, 10);
        String nameLine = c.name + (characterNameEditActive && (frameCount / 18) % 2 == 0 ? "_" : "");
        FontMetrics nameFm = g.getFontMetrics();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(nameLine, nameFm, nameW - 20), characterNameEditRect.x + characterNameEditRect.width/2, nameY + 25);
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        int candX = portraitX + portraitSizeW + 8;
        int candY = portraitY + Math.max(20, portraitSizeW - 24);
        AgeAndWorldTimeAuthority.initializeCandidateAge(c, new Random(Objects.hash(c.name, c.portraitIndex, candidateIndex, seed)));
        String candLine = "Candidate " + (candidateIndex+1) + "/" + candidates.size() + " | " + c.ageYears + "y " + c.ageBand;
        g.setColor(new Color(18,17,15,220));
        int candW = Math.max(154, Math.min(220, characterNameEditRect.x - candX - 10));
        g.fillRoundRect(candX, candY, candW, 24, 8, 8);
        g.setColor(new Color(120,105,72));
        g.drawRoundRect(candX, candY, candW, 24, 8, 8);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(candLine, g.getFontMetrics(), candW - 10), candX + candW/2, candY + 17);

        // Left: thin roll range reference.
        drawPanelBox(g, rangesX, colTop, rangesW, colH, "ROLL RANGES");
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        int ry = colTop + 50;
        for (String key : Candidate.statKeys()) {
            if (ry > colTop + colH - 70) break;
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(key + ": " + Candidate.statRangeText(key), g.getFontMetrics(), rangesW - 24), rangesX+12, ry);
            ry += 23;
        }
        g.setColor(new Color(190,140,110));
        for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap("Jobs may require base stats. Invalid work is marked red and blocked.", Math.max(16, (rangesW-24)/8))) {
            if (ry > colTop + colH - 16) break;
            drawUiTextLine(g, line, rangesX+12, ry); ry += 16;
        }

        // Center: prioritized character sheet.
        g.setColor(new Color(20,20,20,225)); g.fillRect(statsX, colTop, statsW, colH);
        g.setColor(new Color(120,105,72)); g.drawRect(statsX, colTop, statsW, colH); stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "character-sheet-stats", statsX, colTop, statsW, colH);
        g.setFont(uiFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT)); drawUiTextLine(g, "CHARACTER SHEET", statsX+14, colTop+30);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        int sx = statsX+16, sy = colTop+76;
        boolean twoCols = statsW >= 360;
        int colW = twoCols ? Math.max(190, statsW/2-8) : statsW - 28;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "STAT", sx, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "BASE", sx+94, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "MOD", sx+134, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "TOTAL", sx+174, sy-20);
        if (twoCols) {
            int hx = sx + colW;
            drawUiTextLine(g, "STAT", hx, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "BASE", hx+94, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "MOD", hx+134, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "TOTAL", hx+174, sy-20);
        }
        int row = 0;
        int rowsPerCol = twoCols ? 7 : Math.max(7, (colH - 96) / 22);
        for (Map.Entry<String,Integer> e : c.stats.entrySet()) {
            if (!twoCols && row >= rowsPerCol) break;
            int bonus = jp.statBonuses.getOrDefault(e.getKey(), 0) + jp.statPenalties.getOrDefault(e.getKey(), 0);
            int total = e.getValue() + bonus;
            int drawX = sx + (twoCols && row >= rowsPerCol ? colW : 0);
            int drawY = sy + (row % rowsPerCol) * 22;
            if (drawY > colTop + colH - 42) break;
            g.setColor(new Color(180,178,150));
            drawUiTextLine(g, e.getKey()+":", drawX, drawY);
            drawUiTextLine(g, String.format("%2d", e.getValue()), drawX+100, drawY);
            g.setColor(bonus < 0 ? new Color(185,70,60) : (bonus > 0 ? new Color(100,175,100) : new Color(145,142,120)));
            drawUiTextLine(g, bonus == 0 ? "--" : String.format("%+d", bonus), drawX+140, drawY);
            g.setColor(total < e.getValue() ? new Color(205,95,82) : (total > e.getValue() ? new Color(135,215,135) : new Color(190,188,158)));
            drawUiTextLine(g, String.format("%2d", total), drawX+184, drawY);
            row++;
        }
        g.setColor(validJob ? new Color(150,145,118) : new Color(235,95,75));
        int ledgerY = colTop + colH - 34;
        for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap(validJob ? "Green modifiers help; red modifiers hurt. Final total after job." : "INVALID JOB: " + jp.missingText(c), Math.max(22, (statsW-34)/8))) {
            if (ledgerY > colTop + colH - 10) break;
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(line, g.getFontMetrics(), statsW-34), statsX+18, ledgerY);
            ledgerY += Math.max(14, g.getFontMetrics().getHeight());
        }

        // Right: lower-priority dossier, scrollable inside its own panel.
        g.setColor(new Color(22,21,19,232)); g.fillRect(dossierX, colTop, dossierW, colH);
        g.setColor(validJob ? new Color(145,122,78) : new Color(180,55,45)); g.drawRect(dossierX, colTop, dossierW, colH);
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT)); drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(jobDossierTab==0 ? "JOB DOSSIER: " + jp.name : "MASTER JOB LIST", g.getFontMetrics(), dossierW-28), dossierX+14, colTop+66);
        if (!validJob) {
            g.setFont(uiFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(20f, uiFont.getSize2D()+6f)));
            g.setColor(new Color(245,95,80));
            center(g, "INVALID JOB", dossierX + dossierW/2, colTop + 92);
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        ArrayList<String> dossier = new ArrayList<>();
        if (jobDossierTab == 1) {
            dossier.add("JOB | STATUS | FACTION | CLOTHING | REQUIREMENTS");
            dossier.add("Use < JOB / JOB > to select an entry; the table remains separated from the dossier text.");
            dossier.add("");
            for (int i=0; i<c.jobs.size(); i++) {
                JobProfile p = JobProfile.get(c.jobs.get(i));
                boolean ok = p.meets(c);
                dossier.add((i==jobIndex?"> ":"  ") + p.name + " | " + (ok ? "VALID" : "INVALID: " + p.missingText(c)) + " | " + p.faction.label + " | " + p.clothingName);
                dossier.add("    Req: " + p.requirementText());
                dossier.add("");
            }
        } else {
            dossier.addAll(TextSurfaceApi.wrap(jp.description, Math.max(24, (dossierW-42)/8)));
            dossier.add("");
            dossier.add("Requirements: " + jp.requirementText());
            dossier.add(validJob ? "Requirement check: PASSED" : "Requirement check: FAILED — " + jp.missingText(c));
            dossier.add("Bonuses: " + jp.bonusText());
            dossier.add("Penalties: " + jp.penaltyText());
            dossier.add("Faction affiliation: " + jp.faction.label);
            dossier.add("Starting clothes: " + jp.clothingName + " | Defense " + jp.clothingDefense + " | Disguise cover " + jp.disguiseBase + "%");
            dossier.add("");
            dossier.add("Starting inventory:");
            for (String item : jp.startingItems()) dossier.add("- " + item);
            dossier.add("");
            if (jp.faction == Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS) dossier.add("Warning: most gangers will treat this start as a walking arrest warrant.");
            else if (jp.faction == Faction.BANDIT) dossier.add("Warning: law enforcement and rival crews will not admire your career path.");
            else if (jp.faction == Faction.SCAVENGER) dossier.add("Scavenger-aligned clothing is broadly tolerated, except by bandits, and often questioned by Civic Wardens patrols.");
            else if (jp.faction == Faction.NONE) dossier.add("No faction backing. Better skills, fewer friends, and the full warmth of underhive hospitality.");
            else dossier.add("Faction-aligned start. Your clothes open some doors and paint a target on your back for enemy factions.");
            if (jp.faction != Faction.NONE) dossier.add("Affiliation rule: true members of this faction do not roll disguise checks against their own faction merely because of clothing.");
        }
        drawScrollableWrappedLines(g, dossier, dossierX+14, colTop+96, dossierW-36, colH-126, jobDossierScroll, jobDossierTab==0?"job-dossier":"job-list");
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel("Scroll with wheel/drag/arrows/PgUp/PgDn", g.getFontMetrics(), dossierW-28), dossierX+14, colTop+colH-12);
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(new Color(150,145,118));
        center(g, "Top row changes candidate/job; center sheet is primary; dossier and roll ranges remain bounded and scrollable.", W/2, H-24);
    }


    void addInfopediaButtons() {
        Rectangle modal = uiLayout().modal;
        int tabX = modal.x + 28, tabY = modal.y + 70;
        String[] tabs = infopediaTabs();
        int visibleTabs = Math.min(tabs.length, Math.max(1, (modal.width - 56) / 128));
        int tabStart = Math.max(0, Math.min(infopediaTab - visibleTabs/2, tabs.length - visibleTabs));
        for (int j=0;j<visibleTabs;j++) {
            int i = tabStart + j;
            final int idx=i;
            String label = (idx == infopediaTab ? "[" + tabs[i] + "]" : tabs[i]);
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox(label, tabX + j*128, tabY, 120, 32, "Infopedia tab: "+tabs[i], () -> { infopediaTab=idx; infopediaSelected=0; infopediaScroll=0; infopediaDetailScroll=0; repaint(); }));
        }
        java.util.List<String> entries = infopediaEntries(infopediaTab);
        int ex = modal.x + 36, ey = modal.y + 125;
        int visible = Math.min(entries.size(), Math.max(1,(modal.height-175)/32));
        for (int i=0; i<visible; i++) {
            int idx = i + infopediaScroll;
            if (idx >= entries.size()) break;
            final int sel=idx;
            String label = entries.get(idx);
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox((idx==infopediaSelected?"> ":"") + label, ex, ey + i*34, 260, 29, "Open infopedia entry: "+label, () -> { infopediaSelected=sel; infopediaDetailScroll=0; repaint(); }));
        }
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("◀ TYPE", modal.x+24, modal.y+22, 112, 30, "Previous Infopedia category/type.", () -> { cycleInfopediaTab(-1); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("TYPE ▶", modal.x+modal.width-136, modal.y+22, 112, 30, "Next Infopedia category/type.", () -> { cycleInfopediaTab(1); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("ENTRY ↑", ex, modal.y+modal.height-48, 120, 30, "Scroll/select previous infopedia entry.", () -> { moveInfopediaSelection(-1); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("ENTRY ↓", ex+140, modal.y+modal.height-48, 120, 30, "Scroll/select next infopedia entry.", () -> { moveInfopediaSelection(1); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("LIST", modal.x+modal.width-456, modal.y+modal.height-48, 78, 30, "Use wheel/drag/key scroll on the Infopedia entry list.", () -> { activeScrollTag = "infopedia-list"; repaint(); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("DETAIL", modal.x+modal.width-370, modal.y+modal.height-48, 94, 30, "Use wheel/drag/key scroll on the Infopedia detail pane.", () -> { activeScrollTag = "infopedia-detail"; repaint(); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("DETAIL ↑", modal.x+modal.width-268, modal.y+modal.height-48, 96, 30, "Scroll selected Infopedia detail upward.", () -> { scrollInfopediaDetail(-1, false); }));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("DETAIL ↓", modal.x+modal.width-164, modal.y+modal.height-48, 96, 30, "Scroll selected Infopedia detail downward.", () -> { scrollInfopediaDetail(1, false); }));
        if ("KNOWLEDGE".equals(tabs[Math.max(0, Math.min(infopediaTab, tabs.length-1))])) {
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("OPEN TREE", modal.x+modal.width-326, modal.y+modal.height-86, 220, 30, "Open the character-owned Knowledge Tree. Purchases no longer occur inside the Infopedia.", this::openKnowledgeMenu));
        }
        if (isAssetInfopediaTab(infopediaTab)) {
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("ASSET TYPE ◀", modal.x+154, modal.y+22, 130, 30, "Previous semantic asset purpose/type for the Infopedia asset index.", () -> { cycleInfopediaAssetType(-1); }));
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("ASSET TYPE ▶", modal.x+292, modal.y+22, 130, 30, "Next semantic asset purpose/type for the Infopedia asset index.", () -> { cycleInfopediaAssetType(1); }));
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("FILTER", modal.x+430, modal.y+22, 92, 30, "Focus the semantic asset text filter. Type to search IDs, names, paths, and descriptions.", () -> { activeScrollTag = "infopedia-asset-filter"; repaint(); }));
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("CLEAR", modal.x+530, modal.y+22, 82, 30, "Clear the semantic asset filter.", () -> { infopediaAssetFilter = ""; infopediaSelected = 0; infopediaScroll = 0; activeScrollTag = "infopedia-list"; repaint(); }));
        }
        addInfopediaRelatedEntryButtons(modal, entries);
    }

    void cycleInfopediaTab(int delta) {
        String[] tabs = infopediaTabs();
        infopediaTab = Math.max(0, Math.min(tabs.length-1, infopediaTab + delta));
        infopediaSelected = 0;
        infopediaScroll = 0;
        infopediaDetailScroll = 0;
        activeScrollTag = "infopedia-list";
        repaint();
    }

    boolean isAssetInfopediaTab(int tab) {
        String[] tabs = infopediaTabs();
        return tab >= 0 && tab < tabs.length && "ASSETS".equals(tabs[tab]);
    }

    AssetType selectedInfopediaAssetType() {
        AssetType[] types = SemanticAssetInfopediaAuthority.browseTypes();
        if (infopediaAssetTypeIndex < 0 || infopediaAssetTypeIndex >= types.length) return null;
        return types[infopediaAssetTypeIndex];
    }

    void cycleInfopediaAssetType(int delta) {
        AssetType[] types = SemanticAssetInfopediaAuthority.browseTypes();
        int slots = types.length + 1; // All + explicit types.
        int raw = infopediaAssetTypeIndex + 1;
        raw = Math.floorMod(raw + delta, slots);
        infopediaAssetTypeIndex = raw - 1;
        infopediaSelected = 0;
        infopediaScroll = 0;
        infopediaDetailScroll = 0;
        activeScrollTag = "infopedia-list";
        repaint();
    }

    void appendInfopediaAssetFilter(char ch) {
        if (Character.isISOControl(ch)) return;
        if (infopediaAssetFilter.length() >= 48) return;
        infopediaAssetFilter = (infopediaAssetFilter + ch).trim().replaceAll("\\s+", " ");
        infopediaSelected = 0;
        infopediaScroll = 0;
        infopediaDetailScroll = 0;
        repaint();
    }

    void backspaceInfopediaAssetFilter() {
        if (!infopediaAssetFilter.isEmpty()) {
            infopediaAssetFilter = infopediaAssetFilter.substring(0, infopediaAssetFilter.length() - 1);
            infopediaSelected = 0;
            infopediaScroll = 0;
            infopediaDetailScroll = 0;
            repaint();
        }
    }

    void moveInfopediaSelection(int delta) {
        java.util.List<String> entries = infopediaEntries(infopediaTab);
        if (entries.isEmpty()) { infopediaSelected = 0; return; }
        infopediaSelected = Math.max(0, Math.min(entries.size()-1, infopediaSelected + delta));
        int visible = Math.max(1, (uiLayout().modal.height-228)/32);
        if (infopediaSelected < infopediaScroll) infopediaScroll = infopediaSelected;
        if (infopediaSelected >= infopediaScroll + visible) infopediaScroll = infopediaSelected - visible + 1;
        infopediaDetailScroll = 0;
        activeScrollTag = "infopedia-list";
        repaint();
    }

    void scrollInfopediaDetail(int delta, boolean page) {
        int step = page ? 8 : 3;
        infopediaDetailScroll = Math.max(0, infopediaDetailScroll + Integer.compare(delta, 0) * step);
        activeScrollTag = "infopedia-detail";
        repaint();
    }

    void openInfopediaEntry(String target) {
        if (target == null || target.isBlank()) return;
        for (int t=0; t<infopediaTabs().length; t++) {
            java.util.List<String> entries = infopediaEntries(t);
            for (int i=0; i<entries.size(); i++) {
                if (entries.get(i).equalsIgnoreCase(target) || ItemQuality.namesMatch(entries.get(i), target)) {
                    infopediaTab = t;
                    infopediaSelected = i;
                    int visible = Math.max(1, (uiLayout().modal.height-228)/32);
                    infopediaScroll = Math.max(0, i - visible / 2);
                    infopediaDetailScroll = 0;
                    activeScrollTag = "infopedia-detail";
                    logEvent("INFOPEDIA LINK: opened " + entries.get(i) + ".");
                    repaint();
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
        logEvent("INFOPEDIA LINK: no entry found for " + target + ".");
    }

    ArrayList<String> infopediaRelatedEntries(int tab, String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> raw = new ArrayList<>();
        if (entry == null) return raw;
        String low = entry.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (tab == 0) Collections.addAll(raw, entry + " Rooms", "Heat and Suspicion Overview", "Vendor & Shop Stock Rules");
        else if (tab == 1) Collections.addAll(raw, "Scavenge XP", "Vendor & Shop Stock Rules", "Actor Access / Permission Ledger");
        else if (tab == 2 || tab == 3) Collections.addAll(raw, "Item Quality Ladder", "Vendor & Shop Stock Rules", "Contraband and Law Status Ledger");
        else if (tab == 4) Collections.addAll(raw, "Look and Examine", "Movement Planning", "Inventory and Transfer", "Medical Overview", "Body Overview", "Food and Water", "Sleep and Exhaustion");
        else if (tab == 5) Collections.addAll(raw, "Body Injuries and Incapacitation", "Damage and Armor", "Targeted Attacks", "Medical Overview");
        else if (tab == 6) Collections.addAll(raw, "Medical Overview", "Bandages and Field Dressings", "Splints", "Incapacitation");
        else if (tab == 7) Collections.addAll(raw, "Body Overview", "Bleeding", "Infection Risk", "Doctors and Clinics");
        else if (tab == 8) Collections.addAll(raw, "Hourly Decay", "Heat Sources", "Suspicion Sources", "Avoiding Attention");
        else if (tab == 9) Collections.addAll(raw, "Task XP", "Combat XP", "Trade XP", "Construction XP");
        else if (tab == 10) Collections.addAll(raw, "Knowledge Tree Authority", "Purchasing Knowledge", "Training Sources", "Crafting Overview");
        else if (tab == 11) Collections.addAll(raw, "Recipe Requirements", "Machine Quality Ceilings", "Production Ledger Overview", "Item Quality Ladder");
        else if (tab == 12 || tab == 13) Collections.addAll(raw, "Audit Overview", "Examine and Infopedia Link Audit", "Menu Definition Audit", "Movement Planning Audit", "Production Ledger Overview", "Actor Access / Permission Ledger", "Unified Input Registry / Gamepad Bridge");
        else if (tab == 14) Collections.addAll(raw, "Passive Defense Effects", "Defense Semantic Audit", "Heat and Suspicion Overview", "Construction XP");
        else if (tab == 15) Collections.addAll(raw, "Faction Variant Production Rules", "Hostile Intent Barks", "Heat and Suspicion Overview", "Vendor & Shop Stock Rules");
        else if (tab == 16) Collections.addAll(raw, "Faction Variant Production Rules", "Heat and Suspicion Overview", "Vendor & Shop Stock Rules");
        else if (tab == 17) Collections.addAll(raw, "Actor Access / Permission Ledger", "Heat and Suspicion Overview", "Look and Examine", "Movement Planning");
        else if (tab == 18) Collections.addAll(raw, "Construction Validation Inspection", "Audit Overview", "Tile Asset Mapping");
        if (low.contains("medical") || low.contains("bleeding") || low.contains("infection") || low.contains("pain")) raw.add("Medical Overview");
        if (low.contains("heat") || low.contains("suspicion") || low.contains("permit")) raw.add("Heat and Suspicion Overview");
        if (low.contains("trade") || low.contains("vendor") || low.contains("market")) raw.add("Vendor & Shop Stock Rules");
        if (low.contains("recipe") || low.contains("production") || low.contains("machine")) raw.add("Production Ledger Overview");
        return existingInfopediaRelatedEntries(raw, entry);
    }

    ArrayList<String> existingInfopediaRelatedEntries(java.util.List<String> candidates, String currentEntry) {
        ArrayList<String> out = new ArrayList<>();
        if (candidates == null) return out;
        HashSet<String> seen = new HashSet<>();
        for (String candidate : candidates) {
            String found = findInfopediaEntryLabel(candidate);
            if (found == null || found.equalsIgnoreCase(currentEntry)) continue;
            String key = found.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
            if (seen.add(key)) out.add(found);
            if (out.size() >= 6) break;
        }
        return out;
    }

    String findInfopediaEntryLabel(String target) {
        if (target == null || target.isBlank()) return null;
        for (int t=0; t<infopediaTabs().length; t++) {
            for (String entry : infopediaEntries(t)) {
                if (entry.equalsIgnoreCase(target) || ItemQuality.namesMatch(entry, target)) return entry;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    String[] infopediaTabs() { return new String[]{"ZONES", "ROOMS", "ITEMS", "WEAPONS", "SURVIVAL", "COMBAT", "BODY", "MEDICAL", "HEAT", "XP", "KNOWLEDGE", "CRAFTING", "PRODUCTION", "AUDITS", "DEFENSES", "NPCS", "FACTIONS", "TILES", "ASSETS"}; }

    java.util.List<String> infopediaEntries(int tab) {
        ArrayList<String> out = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(tab) {
            case 0:
                for (ZoneType z : ZoneType.values()) out.add(z.label);
                break;
            case 1:
                for (ZoneType z : ZoneType.values()) {
                    out.add(z.label + " Rooms");
                    out.add(z.label + " Generic: " + RoomProfile.forZone(z, new Random(77)).name);
                    out.add(z.label + " Special: " + RoomProfile.forZone(z, new Random(88)).asSpecial(z, new Random(99)).name);
                }
                break;
            case 2:
                out.add("Item Quality Ladder");
                out.add("Vendor & Shop Stock Rules");
                out.add("Faction Variant Production Rules");
                out.add("Production Quality Ceilings");
                out.add("Quality Authority Layer");
                out.add("Knowledge Tree Authority");
                out.add("Machine Tier Authority");
                out.addAll(ItemCatalog.names(false));
                break;
            case 3:
                out.addAll(ItemCatalog.names(true));
                break;
            case 4:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Calendar and Time", "Food and Water", "Sleep and Exhaustion", "Stimulants and Recovery", "Survival Failure States");
                Collections.addAll(out, "Look and Examine", "Movement Planning", "Interaction Approach Planning", "Inventory and Transfer", "Base Storage", "Pet Care", "Context Prompts");
                break;
            case 5:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Combat Command", "Hit Chance and Defense", "Damage and Armor", "Targeted Attacks", "Body Injuries and Incapacitation", "Hostile Intent Barks");
                break;
            case 6:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Body Overview", "Crippled Legs", "Crippled Arms and Hands", "Bleeding", "Pain", "Infection Risk", "Incapacitation");
                break;
            case 7:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Medical Overview", "Bandages and Field Dressings", "Medkits and Medicae Supplies", "Antiseptic", "Splints", "Injectors", "Doctors and Clinics", "Prosthetics Roadmap");
                break;
            case 8:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Heat and Suspicion Overview", "Hourly Decay", "Heat Sources", "Suspicion Sources", "Avoiding Attention");
                break;
            case 9:
                Collections.addAll(out, "XP Overview", "Task XP", "Combat XP", "Scavenge XP", "Trade XP", "Construction XP");
                break;
            case 10:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Knowledge Overview", "Known Knowledge", "Purchasing Knowledge", "Training Sources", "Knowledge Roadmap", "Profile Special Unlocks");
                for (String k : unlockedKnowledges) if (k != null && k.startsWith("Profile Dossier:")) out.add(k);
                out.addAll(KnowledgeDef.names());
                break;
            case 11:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Crafting Overview", "Recipe Requirements", "Machine Quality Ceilings", "Ingredient Consumption", "Faction Output Variants");
                for (CraftingRecipe r : CraftingRecipe.all()) out.add(r.name);
                break;
            case 12:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Production Ledger Overview", "Draft Recipe Graph", "Faction Variant Ledger", "Chemical Equipment Ledger", "Live Placement Ledger", "Facility Output Modifier Ledger", "Build Requirement Cost Ledger", "Production Container Ledger", "Persistent Stock Container Ledger", "Persistent Stock Pickup UX Ledger", "Actor Access / Permission Ledger", "Quality / Knowledge / Machine Authority Ledger", "Contraband and Law Status Ledger", "Recipe Ancestry Samples", "Laboratory Process Samples", "Base Production Ledger", "Economic Topology Framework", "Economic Generation Bias", "Local Topology Metadata Surface", "Economic Topology Preview Consumers", "Economic Topology Reporting Overlay", "Economic Topology Map Intel Bridge", "Retarget Readiness Endpoint", "Runtime Separation Plan", "Launcher / Client / Server Runtime", "Launcher Shell State", "User Profile Surface", "Render Scaling / CRT Surface", "Unified Input Registry / Gamepad Bridge", "Staffing Labor Bridge", "Manual Staffing Assignment Bridge", "Logistics Reservation Scaffold", "Logistics Delivery Intent Bridge", "Logistics Route Readiness Preview", "Logistics Manual Haul Contract", "Logistics Haul Fulfillment Preflight");
                int shownRecipes = 0;
                for (DraftIndustrialRecipe r : RecipeDecompositionApi.generatedDraftRecipes()) {
                    out.add("Recipe: " + r.outputBaseItem);
                    if (++shownRecipes >= 90) break;
                }
                int shownVariants = 0;
                for (FactionRecipeVariant v : FactionRecipeVariantApi.generatedFactionVariants()) {
                    out.add("Variant: " + v.outputName);
                    if (++shownVariants >= 50) break;
                }
                break;
            case 13:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Audit Overview", "Examine and Infopedia Link Audit", "Menu Definition Audit", "Movement Planning Audit", "Industrial Itemization Audit", "Faction Variant Audit", "Chemical Equipment Audit", "Live Placement Audit", "Facility Output Modifier Audit", "Build Requirement Cost Audit", "Production Container Authority Audit", "Persistent Stock Container Audit", "Persistent Stock Pickup UX Audit", "Actor Access Permission Audit", "Authority Alignment Audit", "Production Ledger Display Audit", "Economic Topology Audit", "Economic Generation Bias Audit", "Local Topology Metadata Audit", "Economic Topology Preview Audit", "Economic Topology Reporting Overlay Audit", "Economic Topology Map Intel Bridge Audit", "Retarget Readiness Audit", "Runtime Separation Audit", "Launcher / Client / Server Runtime Audit", "Launcher Shell State Audit", "User Profile Audit", "Render Scaling / CRT Audit", "Unified Input Registry Audit", "Construction Validation Inspection", "Progressive Construction Audit", "Staffing Labor Bridge", "Manual Staffing Assignment Bridge", "Logistics Reservation Scaffold", "Logistics Delivery Intent Bridge", "Logistics Route Readiness Preview", "Logistics Manual Haul Contract", "Logistics Haul Fulfillment Preflight");
                break;
            case 14:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Defense Build Surface", "Defense Semantic Audit", "Passive Defense Effects");
                out.addAll(DefenseSemanticIntegration.labels());
                break;
            case 15:
                Collections.addAll(out, "Civilian", "Trader", "Hiver", "Scavenger", "Ganger", "Civic Wardens", "Concord Guard", "Mechanist Collegia Adept", "Mutant", "Cultist", "Outcast", "Passive: Vending Machine", "Passive: Concord Shrine", "Passive: Heretical Shrine");
                break;
            case 16:
                for (Faction f : Faction.visibleFactions()) out.add(f.label);
                break;
            case 17:
                out.addAll(TileInfopediaAuthority.entryLabels());
                break;
            case 18:
                out.addAll(SemanticAssetInfopediaAuthority.entries(AssetManager.registry(), selectedInfopediaAssetType(), infopediaAssetFilter));
                break;
            default:
                for (Faction f : Faction.visibleFactions()) out.add(f.label);
                break;
        }
        return out;
    }

    java.util.List<String> infopediaDetailLines(int tab, String entry) {
        if (isAssetInfopediaTab(tab)) {
            return SemanticAssetInfopediaAuthority.detailLines(AssetManager.registry(), entry, selectedInfopediaAssetType(), infopediaAssetFilter);
        }
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        lines.add(entry);
        lines.add("Reference ID: " + tab + ":" + Math.abs(entry.hashCode()));
        lines.add("");
        if (tab == 0) {
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(entry);
            lines.add("Zone profile");
            lines.add("Description: " + (z==null?"Unknown zone.":z.descriptor));
            if (z != null) {
                int[] minmax = z.roomSize(new Random(3));
                lines.add("Generation role: " + zoneGenerationRole(z));
                lines.add("Room pattern: 20-30 rooms per slice; larger centered zone footprint; biased room dimensions around " + minmax[0] + "x" + minmax[1] + "; specials selected from zone-specific pools.");
                lines.add("Likely NPCs: " + likelyNpcText(z));
                lines.add("Likely fixtures: " + new String(world==null?new char[]{'o','u','t'}:samplePropsForZone(z)) + " — " + zoneFixtureMeaning(z));
                lines.add("Player warning: " + zonePlayerWarning(z));
                lines.addAll(EconomicTopologyFramework.zonePurposeLines(z));
            }
        } else if (tab == 1) {
            lines.addAll(roomInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 2 || tab == 3) {
            if (entry.equals("Item Quality Ladder")) {
                lines.add("Quality and value reference");
                lines.add("Every cataloged item can be described through the same eight-tier quality ladder. This entry is about tier meaning, not one specific object.");
                lines.addAll(ItemQuality.detailLines());
                lines.add("Gameplay use: quality modifies value, charges/usefulness, reliability, and social/economic weight. It also feeds production ceilings and provenance labels.");
            } else if (entry.equals("Quality Authority Layer")) {
                lines.addAll(QualityAuthorityApi.detailLines());
            } else if (entry.equals("Knowledge Tree Authority")) {
                lines.addAll(KnowledgeTreeApi.detailLines());
            } else if (entry.equals("Machine Tier Authority")) {
                lines.addAll(MachineTierAuthority.detailLines());
            } else if (entry.equals("Vendor & Shop Stock Rules")) {
                lines.add("Vendor and shop stock reference");
                lines.add("Scope: explains how trade offers are assembled and priced, not what any one item does.");
                lines.add("Traders draw visible stock from cataloged items and may bias stock by faction, zone, room, and trader role.");
                lines.add("Offer labels may carry quality prefixes: Junk, Shoddy, Common, Serviceable, Fine, Masterwork, Noble, or Archeotech.");
                lines.add("Buy prices derive from catalog base price, item quality, trader markup, and haggle discount. Sell prices use catalog value, then apply trader pressure.");
                lines.add("Current operational rule: purchased offers are materialized on a trader shelf container, then transferred into player inventory with provenance preserved.");
            } else if (entry.equals("Faction Variant Production Rules")) {
                lines.add("Faction manufacturing identity reference");
                lines.add("Scope: explains why two goods with the same base item may differ by maker, doctrine, quality, social meaning, lawful status, and production inputs.");
                lines.add("Formula: base draft recipe + faction manufacturing identity + quality authority + knowledge category + machine tier = generated faction recipe variant.");
                lines.add("Generated faction variants remain draft/provenance-facing for now; they are not wholesale-injected into the player workbench list.");
                lines.add("Civilian goods favor availability; military goods favor rugged durability; noble goods favor comfort/status; Mechanist Collegia goods favor throughput/efficiency with higher power and maintenance demands; scavver goods favor repairability with serious defect risk.");
                lines.add("Recipe knowledge is quality-bound. Machines cannot exceed their own quality ceiling even when the actor knows a better pattern.");
                lines.addAll(FactionManufacturingProfile.summaryLines());
                lines.add("Example generated faction variants:");
                lines.addAll(FactionRecipeVariantApi.sampleLines(8));
            } else if (entry.equals("Production Quality Ceilings")) {
                lines.add("Production ceiling reference");
                lines.add("Scope: explains the cap that keeps production honest instead of letting every recipe produce top-tier goods.");
                lines.add("Output quality is capped by the lowest relevant authority: recipe knowledge tier, machine tier, input material tier, facility tier, and worker/recruit competence.");
                lines.add("Example: a Junk Micro Assembler can only make Junk outputs even if the player owns better knowledge. The pamphlet may be holy; the machine remains a coughing brick.");
                lines.add("Example generated recipe previews:");
                lines.addAll(ProductionRecipe.sampleLines());
                lines.add("Current status: faction variants use these quality, knowledge, and machine authorities; input-material, facility, and worker ceilings remain explicit hooks that stay permissive until those ledgers carry quality tiers.");
            } else {
                ItemDef def = ItemCatalog.get(entry);
                if (def == null) {
                    lines.add(tab==2?"Item catalog gap":"Weapon catalog gap");
                    lines.add("This entry exists in the menu but is not cataloged. It needs a proper entry before expansion continues.");
                } else {
                    lines.addAll(def.detailLines());
                }
            }
        } else if (tab == 4) {
            lines.addAll(survivalInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 5) {
            lines.addAll(combatInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 6) {
            lines.addAll(bodyInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 7) {
            lines.addAll(medicalInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 8) {
            lines.addAll(heatInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 9) {
            lines.addAll(xpInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 10) {
            if ("Profile Special Unlocks".equals(entry)) {
                lines.add("Name-locked profile unlocks");
                lines.add("These entries are separate from random character generation. They require both the active operator profile and the finalized character name to resolve to the same registered profile.");
                lines.add("Unlocks grant profile dossier items, a knowledge entry, and a portrait source that is kept out of the ordinary portrait pool.");
                lines.add("Rare world seeding: inactive registered profiles may appear as visiting nobles in noble districts. The active profile key is excluded so the player does not meet a duplicate of themselves.");
                lines.add("");
                lines.add("Registered profiles: " + NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.entries().size());
                for (NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry e : NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.entries()) lines.add("- " + e.displayName + " // " + e.title + " // " + (hasKnowledge("Profile Dossier: " + e.displayName) ? "known" : "locked"));
            } else if (entry != null && entry.startsWith("Profile Dossier:")) {
                String name = entry.substring("Profile Dossier:".length()).trim();
                NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry e = NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.match(name).orElse(null);
                lines.addAll(NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.infopediaLines(e, e != null && hasKnowledge("Profile Dossier: " + e.displayName)));
            } else {
            KnowledgeDef def = KnowledgeDef.get(entry);
            if (def != null) {
                lines.addAll(def.detailLines());
                lines.add("Status: " + (hasKnowledge(def.name) ? "KNOWN" : "LOCKED") + ". Spendable knowledge credits: " + knowledgeCredits + ".");
                lines.add("Unlock UI: open the Character Dossier Knowledge Tree. The Infopedia is now reference/audit only for doctrine entries.");
            } else {
                lines.addAll(knowledgeReferenceLines(entry));
            }
            }
        } else if (tab == 11) {
            CraftingRecipe cr = CraftingRecipe.byName(entry);
            if (cr != null) {
                lines.addAll(cr.detailLines());
                lines.add("Current status: " + cr.shortStatus(this));
            } else {
                lines.addAll(craftingReferenceLines(entry));
            }
        } else if (tab == 12) {
            lines.addAll(productionInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 13) {
            lines.addAll(auditInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 14) {
            if ("Defense Build Surface".equals(entry)) lines.addAll(DefenseBuildSelectionAuthority.buildSurfaceLines());
            else if ("Defense Semantic Audit".equals(entry)) lines.addAll(DefenseSemanticIntegration.infopediaLines());
            else if ("Passive Defense Effects".equals(entry)) lines.addAll(PassiveDefenseEffectsAuthority.infopediaLines());
            else lines.addAll(DefenseSemanticIntegration.detailLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 15) {
            lines.addAll(npcInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 16) {
            Faction f = factionByLabel(entry);
            lines.addAll(factionInfopediaLines(f, entry));
        } else if (tab == 17) {
            if (TileInfopediaAuthority.isHeader(entry)) {
                lines.add("Tile category");
                lines.add(entry.replace("--", "").trim());
                lines.add("Select a tile entry below this header to audit its glyph, descriptor, icon source, and allowed variants.");
            } else {
                lines.addAll(TileInfopediaAuthority.detailLines(entry, images == null ? null : images.tileArt));
            }
        } else {
            Faction f = factionByLabel(entry);
            lines.addAll(factionInfopediaLines(f, entry));
        }
        return lines;
    }

    java.util.List<String> infopediaDetailLinesWithRelated(int tab, String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>(infopediaDetailLines(tab, entry));
        ArrayList<String> related = infopediaRelatedEntries(tab, entry);
        if (!related.isEmpty()) {
            lines.add("");
            lines.add("Related entries:");
            for (String r : related) lines.add("  LINK: " + r);
            lines.add("Use the LINK buttons below the detail pane to jump directly to the first related entries.");
        }
        return lines;
    }
