    java.util.List<String> roomInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (entry.endsWith(" Rooms")) {
            String zoneName = entry.substring(0, entry.length() - " Rooms".length());
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(zoneName);
            lines.add("Zone room set");
            lines.add("Scope: describes the room pool for " + zoneName + ", not the whole zone and not a specific room instance.");
            lines.add("Layout rule: rooms are enclosed first, doors are placed on valid room walls, and corridors attach outward from door points.");
            lines.add("Room bias: " + (z==null?"generic underhive rooms":zoneGenerationRole(z)));
            lines.add("Inspectable texture: " + (z==null?InspectableFeatureTable.sampleLine():InspectableFeatureTable.combinedFor(z, new Random(31), "sample").replace("sample; inspectable features: ", "")) + ".");
            lines.add("Special hooks: traders, locked caches, faction access, machinery, shrines, vending machines, or encounter logic are selected from this zone's room pool.");
        } else if (entry.contains(" Generic: ")) {
            String zoneName = entry.substring(0, entry.indexOf(" Generic: ")).trim();
            String name = entry.substring(entry.indexOf(" Generic: ") + " Generic: ".length()).trim();
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(zoneName);
            lines.add("Generic room sample");
            lines.add("Zone context: " + zoneName + " — " + (z==null?"generic room pool":zoneGenerationRole(z)) + ".");
            lines.add("Sample name: " + name + ".");
            lines.add("Generation rule: common rooms use this zone's size bias, faction bias, loot list, content symbols, and inspectable feature table.");
            lines.add("Purpose: fills " + zoneName + " with believable functional clutter while keeping special rooms rarer and more meaningful.");
        } else if (entry.contains(" Special: ")) {
            String zoneName = entry.substring(0, entry.indexOf(" Special: ")).trim();
            String name = entry.substring(entry.indexOf(" Special: ") + " Special: ".length()).trim();
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(zoneName);
            lines.add("Special room sample");
            lines.add("Zone context: " + zoneName + " — " + (z==null?"generic special-room pool":zoneGenerationRole(z)) + ".");
            lines.add("Sample name: " + name + ".");
            lines.add("Generation rule: special rooms are inserted after ordinary room selection and can override contents with themed fixtures or actors.");
            lines.add("Player use: inspect before interacting; " + zoneName + " specials are where services, story hooks, danger, and operational surfaces appear.");
        } else {
            lines.add("Room reference");
            lines.add("This entry identifies a generated room concept. The current generator gives each room walls, doors, floor area, inspectable texture, and a zone/faction context.");
        }
        return lines;
    }

    java.util.List<String> survivalInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(entry) {
            case "Calendar and Time":
                lines.add("Calendar and action-time reference");
                lines.add("Rule: 100 action turns equal one local hour; 26 hours make one day; 28 days make one month.");
                lines.add("Current time: " + timeText() + ". The absolute turn counter remains the save/log authority while the visible clock translates it into survival time.");
                break;
            case "Food and Water":
                lines.add("Food and water pressure reference");
                lines.add("Current reserves: food " + food + "/15, water " + water + "/15.");
                lines.add("One reserve is consumed every eight awake hours. Starvation/dehydration damage checks happen hourly only after a reserve reaches zero.");
                lines.add("Food and water items restore reserves through inventory use and are now intended to preserve item provenance until consumption.");
                break;
            case "Sleep and Exhaustion":
                lines.add("Sleep debt reference");
                lines.add("Current sleep debt: " + (sleepNeed / TURNS_PER_HOUR) + " hour(s) of 26 before collapse risk.");
                lines.add("Sleep debt grows by one hour per awake hour. Reaching 26 hours can cause exhaustion collapse and carried item loss.");
                lines.add("Cots allow 1-8 hour sleep chunks; sleeping costs food/water by the sleep-cost rule and may reduce fatigue or wounds.");
                break;
            case "Stimulants and Recovery":
                lines.add("Stimulant and short recovery reference");
                lines.add("Coffee and stim items reduce immediate sleep debt or fatigue pressure, but repeated abuse creates stimulant strain and later backlash.");
                lines.add("Current fatigue: " + fatigue + "; stimulant strain: " + stimulantStrain + ".");
                lines.add("Design rule: stimulants buy time; they do not replace food, water, sleep, or actual medical work.");
                break;
            case "Look and Examine":
                lines.add("Look and Examine reference");
                lines.add("Look gives immediate visible context for the selected tile: tile identity, ownership, light/noise, stacked contents, obvious NPC or object detail, and whether deeper examination is useful.");
                lines.add("Examine spends time to read the selected visible target more carefully. Repeating Examine on the same target within a few turns can reveal deeper threat, senses, condition, evidence, and interaction context.");
                lines.add("Boundary: Examine reports known or observable reads. It should not reveal hidden identities, private contract state, or internal records unless the world has exposed them.");
                break;
            case "Movement Planning":
                lines.add("Movement planning reference");
                lines.add("PLAN MOVE lets the player choose a movement endpoint, preview the route, see hazards, and confirm instead of relying only on directional movement.");
                lines.add("Movement mode changes range, time cost, noise, fatigue, and observation. The preview divides long routes into action chunks based on the current movement mode.");
                lines.add("Current movement: " + movementModeLabel() + ", range " + movementModeRange() + ", cost " + movementTurnCost() + " turn(s) per tile.");
                break;
            case "Interaction Approach Planning":
                lines.add("Interaction approach planning reference");
                lines.add("When a selected interaction target is too far away, the interaction preflight can nominate a reachable adjacent approach tile.");
                lines.add("Starting PLAN MOVE from that context prefers the approach tile and labels the preview as an approach path, helping with doors, NPCs, pets, containers, machines, vendors, and other exact-range targets.");
                lines.add("If no approach tile is shown, the target may already be adjacent, blocked, unreachable, or not an interaction target.");
                break;
            case "Inventory and Transfer":
                lines.add("Inventory and transfer reference");
                lines.add("Item movement uses a shared preflight grammar: source, target, quantity, capacity, permission/access, quest/evidence protection, risk, and whether the move is reversible.");
                lines.add("Carried load currently reads " + carryStatusText() + ". Overflow blocks purchase and recovery actions before the item moves.");
                lines.add("Quest and evidence items are protected from ordinary sale so proof, delivery goods, journals, and active turn-in objects do not vanish through routine commerce.");
                break;
            case "Base Storage":
                lines.add("Base storage reference");
                lines.add("Claimed-base storage lets the player STASH the newest carried item and TAKE the newest stored item while standing inside the claimed room.");
                lines.add("Storage reports access, capacity, quest protection, and risk categories such as weapons, suspicious tools, commerce goods, survival reserves, and medical reserves.");
                lines.add("Current storage: " + baseStorage.size() + "/" + baseStorageCapacity() + " item(s). " + baseStorageRiskSummaryLine());
                break;
            case "Pet Care":
                lines.add("Pet care reference");
                lines.add("Companion animals expose ownership, adoption/sale context, hunger, thirst, rest, shelter, temperament, accessibility, and petting permission through Look and Examine.");
                lines.add("Petting requires a companion animal, safe temperament, visibility, and adjacency. Non-pet animals explain why contact is blocked instead of pretending to be inert scenery.");
                lines.add("Pet systems should feel like visible living systems, not hidden timers.");
                break;
            case "Context Prompts":
                lines.add("Context prompt reference");
                lines.add("Major panels show prompt lines using the current input binding label and the current context: ready actions are named, and blocked actions explain what is missing.");
                lines.add("Examples include moving adjacent before confirming Interact, selecting an item before inventory actions, choosing a build tile before construction confirmation, and needing an active trader before trade confirmation.");
                lines.add("Keyboard and controller prompts share abstract action names so rebinding and profile work can update prompts without rewriting every panel.");
                break;
            default:
                lines.add("Survival failure-state reference");
                lines.add("Failure comes from accumulated pressure: no food, no water, exhaustion, untreated wounds, bleeding, infection, or reckless stimulant use.");
                lines.add("Current pressure summary: wounds " + wounds + ", fatigue " + fatigue + ", bleeding " + bleeding + ", infection risk " + infectionRisk + ", pain " + pain + ".");
                lines.add("Design intent: survival should pressure long routes and bad decisions, not interrupt every few steps with petty meter chores.");
                break;
        }
        return lines;
    }

    java.util.List<String> combatInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(entry) {
            case "Combat Command":
                lines.add("Attack command reference");
                lines.add("Use the COMBAT button or F hotkey to attack an adjacent hostile using carried/equipped weapon logic or bare hands.");
                lines.add("Each attack spends action time and reports hit, miss, armor soak, wounds, and incapacitation through RECENT ACTIONS.");
                break;
            case "Hit Chance and Defense":
                lines.add("Accuracy and defense reference");
                lines.add("Hit chance compares attack skill, weapon suitability, target defense/agility, and situational cover logic.");
                lines.add("Failed attacks still produce explicit feedback so the player knows whether the problem was range, target state, weapon, or chance.");
                break;
            case "Damage and Armor":
                lines.add("Damage resolution reference");
                lines.add("Weapon or base attack damage is reduced by armor before body damage is applied to a rolled location.");
                lines.add("Armor therefore changes expected injury, not just whether an enemy is allowed to exist after being clicked.");
                break;
            case "Targeted Attacks":
                lines.add("Targeting system reference");
                lines.add("Reserved targeting should trade hit chance for tactical reward: disarming arms, slowing legs, stunning heads, or damaging torso stability.");
                lines.add("This entry is intentionally distinct from default attacks, which currently roll a random body location for speed and danger.");
                break;
            case "Body Injuries and Incapacitation":
                lines.add("Combat injury reference");
                lines.add("Damaged legs slow movement, damaged arms and hands penalize weapon/tool use, and severe body or head damage risks incapacitation.");
                lines.add("Current body pressure: crippled legs " + crippledLegCount() + ", crippled arms/hands " + crippledArmCount() + ", wounds " + wounds + ".");
                break;
            default:
                lines.add("Hostile intent bark reference");
                lines.add("Enemies that see or hear the player can announce intent in the action feed before or as combat begins.");
                lines.add("Purpose: make danger readable without granting perfect tactical information through the map display.");
                break;
        }
        return lines;
    }

                break;
            case "Bleeding":

                break;
            case "Pain":

                break;

                lines.add("Incapacitation reference");
                lines.add("Severe accumulated damage, body/head trauma, and exhaustion can push the character out of useful action.");
                lines.add("Purpose: body systems make injury a continuing operational problem, not a single red number.");
                break;
        }
        return lines;
    }

    java.util.List<String> medicalInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(entry) {
            case "Medical Overview":
                lines.add("Medical treatment overview");
                lines.add("Medical play is divided between carried supplies, field stabilization, paid doctors/clinics, and later prosthetic or augmentic repair.");
                lines.add("Current state: wounds " + wounds + ", bleeding " + bleeding + ", infection risk " + infectionRisk + ", fatigue " + fatigue + ", pain " + pain + ".");
                break;
            case "Bandages and Field Dressings":
                lines.add("Bleeding-control reference");
                lines.add("Bandages and field dressings reduce bleeding and one wound. They are the best first response after knives, claws, bullets, and poor decisions.");
                break;
            case "Medkits and Medicae Supplies":
                lines.add("General medicae item reference");
                lines.add("Medkits and medicae supplies provide stronger treatment: bleeding, wounds, infection risk, fatigue, pain, and the worst body part can all improve slightly.");
                break;
            case "Antiseptic":
                lines.add("Infection-control reference");
                lines.add("Antiseptic reduces infection risk without pretending to fix structural damage. Use it after dirty wounds, sewer work, or mutant unpleasantness.");
                break;
            case "Splints":
                lines.add("Limb-stabilization reference");
                lines.add("Splints stabilize the worst limb enough to reduce mobility/tool collapse, especially after leg or arm trauma.");
                break;
            case "Injectors":
                lines.add("Injector reference");
                lines.add("Injectors reduce fatigue and pain with minor wound relief. Useful, portable, and absolutely not a license to sprint through a gunfight twice.");
                break;
            case "Doctors and Clinics":
                lines.add("Paid treatment reference");
                lines.add("Doctors and clinics are the intended vendor/service path for deeper repair, prosthetics, augmentics, and high-quality medical work.");
                break;
            default:
                lines.add("Prosthetics system reference");
                lines.add("Reserved prosthetics should replace or augment damaged limbs through clinics, Mechanist Collegia service, rare parts, faction access, and cost.");
                break;
        }
        return lines;
    }

    java.util.List<String> heatInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(entry) {
            case "Heat and Suspicion Overview":
                lines.add("Attention pressure overview");

                break;
            case "Hourly Decay":
                lines.add("Attention decay reference");
                lines.add("Once each 100-turn hour, heat and suspicion decay by 1 while awake. Sleeping counts as laying low and decays each by 2 per hour.");
                lines.add("If no base is claimed, suspicion receives one extra hourly decay point because the character is not leaving a stable property trail yet.");
                break;
            case "Heat Sources":
                lines.add("Gang heat source reference");

                break;
            case "Suspicion Sources":

    java.util.List<String> npcInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        lines.add("NPC/actor reference");
        switch(entry) {
            case "Civilian": lines.add("Role: noncombat local population, service customers, witnesses, and ambient underhive pressure."); lines.add("Behavior: usually wanders, idles, flees danger, or seeks needs providers rather than picking fights."); break;
            case "Trader": lines.add("Role: opens trade sessions and supplies catalog-backed stock with prices, markups, haggle, and provenance handoff."); lines.add("Operational note: trader shelves now have generated containers for bought/sold item movement."); break;
            case "Hiver": lines.add("Role: ordinary arcology resident; baseline faction texture for habs, markets, work floors, and neutral civilian spaces."); lines.add("Gameplay use: social camouflage and crowd density rather than specialized services."); break;
            case "Scavenger": lines.add("Role: marginal salvage actor tied to trash warrens, sewer edges, and low-trust trading."); lines.add("Expected goods: cheap tools, bad food, improvised water, lock tools, and scrap."); break;
            case "Ganger": lines.add("Role: hostile or coercive local criminal power; raises heat and controls gang rooms."); lines.add("Behavior: can threaten, patrol, attack, or trade through fences depending on context."); break;
            case "Civic Wardens": lines.add("Role: law enforcement pressure and procedural brutality rather than civic comfort."); lines.add("Behavior: interrogations, checkpoints, suspicion reactions, restricted stock, and faction-only spaces."); break;
            case "Concord Guard": lines.add("Role: military presence around billets, depots, and field logistics."); lines.add("Expected goods: rations, water, armor, weapons, and rugged tools."); break;
            case "Mechanist Collegia Adept": lines.add("Role: machine-cult worker, trader, tutor, or gatekeeper around forge cloisters and relic ducts."); lines.add("Expected goods: machine parts, sacred wire, tool rolls, data spikes, and machine doctrine."); break;
            case "Mutant": lines.add("Role: hostile or semi-feral sewer/warren threat with its own camps and warning signs."); lines.add("Behavior: generally attacks on sight in mutant layers."); break;
            case "Cultist": lines.add("Role: heretical sewer-camp threat tied to illegal shrines, ritual objects, and hidden danger."); lines.add("Behavior: generally hostile when discovered in cult spaces."); break;
            case "Outcast": lines.add("Role: disconnected survivor used for marginal spaces, barter, rumor, or faction ambiguity."); lines.add("Behavior: should not automatically share civilian trust or ganger hostility."); break;
            case "Passive: Vending Machine": lines.add("Role: passive service object pretending to be an NPC entry for inspection/trade convenience."); lines.add("Use: sells ration/water/supply goods from map-object state and logs stock/cooldown changes."); break;
            case "Passive: Concord Shrine": lines.add("Role: passive loyal shrine fixture for interaction, attention, and faith/social consequences."); lines.add("Use: should support lawful/Concord flavor without duplicating heretical shrine risk."); break;
            default: lines.add("Role: passive illegal shrine fixture with cult risk, suspicion/heat consequences, and forbidden-service hooks."); lines.add("Use: distinct from Concord shrines because interacting with it should be socially and legally dangerous."); break;
        }
        lines.add("Actor standard: every active NPC now has a stable numeric identifier and string ID for logging/save tracking.");
        return lines;
    }

    java.util.List<String> factionInfopediaLines(Faction f, String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        lines.add("Faction reference");
        lines.add("Standing: " + (f==null?0:factionStanding.getOrDefault(f,0)) + "   Hostility timer: " + (f==null?0:temporaryHostileTurns.getOrDefault(f,0)));
        lines.add("Specific designation: " + entry + ".");
        lines.add("Role: " + factionRoleText(f));
        lines.add("Typical presence: " + factionPresenceText(f));
        lines.add("Trade/production bias: " + factionTradeBiasText(f));
        lines.add("Local distinction: " + factionSpecificNote(f, entry));
        lines.addAll(EconomicTopologyFramework.factionDoctrineLines(f));
        lines.add("Disguise note: true affiliation bypasses checks against that same faction; clothing still matters with outsiders.");
        return lines;
    }

    String zoneGenerationRole(ZoneType z) {
        if (z==ZoneType.SEWER_CONDUIT) return "utility corridors, water machinery, pipe access, and low-visibility traversal";
        if (z==ZoneType.MUTANT_SEWER_CAMP || z==ZoneType.CULTIST_SEWER_CAMP) return "dangerous sewer camp insertion with hostile inhabitants and ritual/survival clutter";
        if (z==ZoneType.MECHANICUS_FORGE_CLOISTER || z==ZoneType.MECHANICUS_RELIC_DUCT) return "machine rooms, forge service paths, relic hardware, and technical loot";
        if (z==ZoneType.ADMINISTRATUM_ARCHIVE) return "records, permits, queues, filing cages, and bureaucratic choke points";
        if (z==ZoneType.ARBITES_PRECINCT_EDGE) return "law checkpoints, evidence spaces, holding edges, and suspicion pressure";
        if (z==ZoneType.IMPERIAL_GUARD_BILLET) return "bunks, ration lockers, field stores, and military logistics";
        if (z==ZoneType.GANGER_TURF) return "territorial rooms, fences, stash points, ambush spaces, and heat pressure";
        if (z==ZoneType.SUMP_MARKET || z==ZoneType.NEUTRAL_RAIL_DEPOT) return "trade counters, public services, barter space, and mixed civilian traffic";
        if (z==ZoneType.NOBLE_SERVICE_SPINE) return "cleaner service corridors, servant infrastructure, restricted access, and high-value scraps";
        if (z==ZoneType.TRAIN_SERVICE_YARD) return "freight handling, tickets, cargo chains, and transit machinery";
        if (z==ZoneType.TRASH_WARREN || z==ZoneType.MUTANT_WARRENS) return "dense salvage, cramped danger, low-trust loot, and organic filth";
        return "habitation, basic services, local clutter, and civilian movement";
    }

    String zoneFixtureMeaning(ZoneType z) {
        if (z==ZoneType.MECHANICUS_FORGE_CLOISTER || z==ZoneType.MECHANICUS_RELIC_DUCT) return "machinery and technical inspection targets are more common here";
        if (z==ZoneType.SUMP_MARKET || z==ZoneType.NEUTRAL_RAIL_DEPOT) return "trade and service fixtures are more common here";
        if (z==ZoneType.GANGER_TURF) return "stash, threat, and gang-sign fixtures are more common here";
        if (z==ZoneType.SEWER_CONDUIT || z==ZoneType.MUTANT_SEWER_CAMP || z==ZoneType.CULTIST_SEWER_CAMP) return "pipes, water hazards, camps, and survival fixtures dominate";
        return "ordinary local fixtures, beds, lockers, refuse, benches, and room-specific objects";
    }

    String zonePlayerWarning(ZoneType z) {
        if (z==ZoneType.MUTANT_SEWER_CAMP || z==ZoneType.MUTANT_WARRENS) return "expect hostile mutants and poor escape conditions";
        if (z==ZoneType.CULTIST_SEWER_CAMP) return "expect illegal ritual danger and hostile cultists";
        if (z==ZoneType.ARBITES_PRECINCT_EDGE) return "misbehavior raises suspicion faster here";
        if (z==ZoneType.GANGER_TURF) return "violence and theft raise gang heat quickly here";
        if (z==ZoneType.MECHANICUS_RELIC_DUCT) return "rare machine objects may be valuable, restricted, or dangerous";
        if (z==ZoneType.NOBLE_SERVICE_SPINE) return "high-value scraps come with access and attention risks";
        return "inspect rooms before assuming public access or safe loot";
    }


    String factionSpecificNote(Faction f, String entry) {
        if (f==null) return "entry exists in the menu without a current faction enum binding";
        String n=f.name();
        if (f==Faction.NONE) return "used when ownership should be deliberately absent, not merely unknown";
        if (n.contains("CLOISTER_RED")) return "red-robed forge alignment; favor orthodox machine service and visible Mechanist Collegia authority";
        if (n.contains("CLOISTER_RUST")) return "rust-cloister alignment; favor maintenance, salvage, and worn machine infrastructure";
        if (n.contains("CLOISTER_VOID")) return "void-cloister alignment; favor sealed systems, space-adjacent hardware, and stranger machine rites";
        if (n.contains("BLOCK_AUREL")) return "hiver block identity for local civilian loyalty, grudges, and housing politics";
        if (n.contains("BLOCK_MARROW")) return "hiver block identity with poorer marrow-hab survival texture and local obligations";
        if (n.contains("BLOCK_SUMPLEDGER")) return "hiver block identity tied to accounting, debts, sump trade, and civic ledgers";
        if (n.contains("IRON_RATS")) return "gang variant leaning toward scrap, tunnels, ambush, and cheap intimidation";
        if (n.contains("BLACK_SUMP")) return "gang variant leaning toward knives, sewer routes, and black-water extortion";
        if (n.contains("CANDLE_JACKS")) return "gang variant leaning toward shrine-like menace, candles, and debt violence";
        if (n.contains("RED_GRIN")) return "gang variant leaning toward open brutality, intimidation theater, and visible heat";
        if (n.contains("CHAIN_SAINTS")) return "gang variant leaning toward chain weapons, false piety, and ritualized street control";
        if (n.contains("ASH_MARKET")) return "gang variant leaning toward market rackets, teeth-debt markers, and trade coercion";
        if (n.contains("WIRE_WOLVES")) return "gang variant leaning toward electrical theft, sabotage, and wire-running turf";
        if (n.contains("DROWNED_9TH")) return "gang variant leaning toward sewer survivorship, drowned routes, and hidden water access";
        if (n.contains("HOUSE_VARN")) return "noble house variant for contracts, permits, status games, and clean-paper cruelty";
        if (n.contains("HOUSE_KASTOR")) return "noble house variant for guarded logistics, household service, and controlled access";
        if (n.contains("HOUSE_MORVAIN")) return "noble house variant for old money, quiet hostility, and polished neglect";
        if (n.contains("HOUSE_CYRA")) return "noble house variant for commerce, favor trading, and cosmetic legality";
        if (n.contains("HOUSE_DRAKE")) return "noble house variant for militarized wealth, security contracts, and hard retaliation";
        if (n.contains("HOUSE_TOLL")) return "noble house variant for fees, transit gates, licenses, and extraction by paperwork";
        if (n.contains("HOUSE_OSSUARY")) return "noble house variant for funereal status, relic claims, and tasteful horror";
        if (f==Faction.MUTANT) return "hostile biological underclass pressure; not the same as cult or machine danger";
        if (f==Faction.CULTIST) return "illegal ritual cell pressure; socially and legally distinct from ordinary crime";
        if (f==Faction.ROGUE_MACHINE) return "machine threat category; should key off failed automation and hostile mechanisms";
        if (f==Faction.HERETIC) return "broad treasonous alignment for forbidden services, contraband doctrine, and high-risk contacts";
        return "base faction entry; subfactions inherit this role but add local grudges, stock bias, and encounter flavor";
    }

    String factionRoleText(Faction f) {
        if (f==null) return "unresolved faction label";
        String n=f.name();
        if (f==Faction.NONE) return "neutral/no-faction marker for generic objects and unowned systems";
        if (n.contains("MECHANIST COLLEGIA")) return "machine authority, technical services, machine goods, and doctrine gates";
        if (n.contains("GANGER") || f==Faction.BANDIT) return "local criminal power, heat pressure, fences, and violent control of turf";
        if (n.contains("HIVER") || f==Faction.HIVER) return "civilian labor/population bloc for habs, markets, and ordinary survival";
        if (n.contains("NOBLE") || f==Faction.NOBLE) return "upper-spire property, permits, luxury goods, servants, and status pressure";
        if (f==Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS) return "law enforcement, suspicion pressure, paperwork, and coercive order";
        if (f==Faction.IMPERIAL_GUARD) return "military logistics, rations, armor, weapons, and depot discipline";
        if (f==Faction.CIVIC_LEDGER_OFFICE) return "records, permits, forms, and bureaucratic access";
        if (f==Faction.SCAVENGER) return "salvage economy, low-trust goods, trash routes, and survival barter";
        return "specialized local faction with its own standing, hostility, and production bias";
    }

    }

    void showTimedAlert(String title, String body, int millis) {
        alertTitle = title == null ? "" : title;
        alertBody = body == null ? "" : body;
        alertUntilMillis = System.currentTimeMillis() + Math.max(750, millis);
        DebugLog.audit("UI_ALERT", alertTitle + " :: " + alertBody);
    }

    void drawEulaOverlay(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int panelW = Math.min(980, Math.max(560, W - 80));
        int panelH = Math.min(720, Math.max(420, H - 80));
        int x = (W - panelW) / 2;
        int y = (H - panelH) / 2;
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,220));
        g.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
        g.setColor(new Color(5,6,6,248));
        g.fillRoundRect(x, y, panelW, panelH, 18, 18);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, x, y, panelW, panelH, "outer");
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, "MANDATORY EULA NOTICE", x + panelW / 2, y + 36);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        int contentX = x + 38;
        int contentY = y + 70;
        int contentW = panelW - 76;
        int contentH = panelH - 154;
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        FontMetrics eulaFm = g.getFontMetrics();
        java.util.List<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        for (String paragraph : EulaConsentAuthority.eulaText()) {
            java.util.List<String> wrapped = GuiLayoutApi.wrapText(paragraph, eulaFm, contentW - 10);
            if (wrapped.isEmpty()) lines.add(""); else lines.addAll(wrapped);
            lines.add("");
        }
        int lineH = Math.max(16, eulaFm.getHeight() + 2);
        int visibleLines = Math.max(1, contentH / lineH);
        eulaMaxScroll = Math.max(0, lines.size() - visibleLines);
        eulaScroll = Math.max(0, Math.min(eulaScroll, eulaMaxScroll));
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(contentX - 4, contentY - 4, contentW + 8, contentH + 8);
        int yy = contentY;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        for (int i = eulaScroll; i < lines.size() && yy <= contentY + contentH; i++) {
            String line = lines.get(i);
            if (line == null || line.isEmpty()) {
                yy += Math.max(6, lineH / 2);
                continue;
            }
            boolean header = line.equals("THE MECHANIST END USER LICENSE AND CONSENT NOTICE") || line.equals("INTELLECTUAL PROPERTY DISCLAIMER & FAN PROJECT ACKNOWLEDGMENT") || line.equals("IMPORTANT NOTICE: UNOFFICIAL FAN-MADE CONTENT");
            g.setColor(header ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            g.drawString(line, contentX, yy);
            yy += lineH;
        }
        g.setClip(oldClip);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        String scrollText = "Scroll wheel / Up / Down / PgUp / PgDn to read. Lines " + Math.min(lines.size(), eulaScroll + 1) + "-" + Math.min(lines.size(), eulaScroll + visibleLines) + " of " + lines.size() + ".";
        g.drawString(GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(scrollText, g.getFontMetrics(), contentW), contentX, y + panelH - 84);
        g.drawString("Keyboard: Enter/A accepts. Escape/Q/X exits.", contentX, y + panelH - 30);
    }

    void scrollEulaGate(int direction, boolean page) {
        int d = Integer.compare(direction, 0);
        if (d == 0) return;
        int step = page ? 8 : 3;
        eulaScroll = Math.max(0, Math.min(Math.max(0, eulaMaxScroll), eulaScroll + d * step));
        repaint();
    }

    void drawTimedAlert(Graphics2D g) {
        if (alertUntilMillis <= System.currentTimeMillis() || alertTitle == null || alertTitle.isEmpty()) return;
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int w = Math.min(620, Math.max(360, W - 160));
        int h = 150;
        int x = (W - w) / 2;
        int y = Math.max(90, H / 2 - h / 2);
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,168));
        g.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        g.setColor(new Color(4,5,4,244));
        g.fillRoundRect(x,y,w,h,16,16);
        drawSlicedFrame(g,x,y,w,h,"inner");
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, alertTitle, x + w/2, y + 38);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        int yy = y + 70;
        for(String line: TextSurfaceApi.wrap(alertBody, Math.max(34,(w-56)/8))) {
            center(g, line, x + w/2, yy);
            yy += 18;
            if (yy > y + h - 18) break;
        }
    }

    void drawInfopediaPanel(Graphics2D g) {
        Rectangle modal = uiLayout().modal;
        g.setColor(new Color(3,4,4,248)); g.fillRect(modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height, "inner");
        g.setFont(titleFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT)); center(g,"INFOPEDIA // UNDERHIVE LOGIC ENGINE", modal.x+modal.width/2, modal.y+45);
        String[] tabs = infopediaTabs();
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        String subtitle = isAssetInfopediaTab(infopediaTab)
                ? "Semantic Asset Index: image previews, asset codes, type/purpose, and in-universe descriptions. Type filter: " + SemanticAssetInfopediaAuthority.typeLabel(selectedInfopediaAssetType()) + " | Search: " + (infopediaAssetFilter.isBlank() ? "<none>" : infopediaAssetFilter) + ("infopedia-asset-filter".equals(activeScrollTag) ? " _" : "")
                : "Zones, rooms, items, weapons, NPC types, and factions. Entries summarize implemented reference rules and intended doctrine.";
        center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(subtitle, g.getFontMetrics(), modal.width-70), modal.x+modal.width/2, modal.y+102);
        int listX=modal.x+28, listY=modal.y+120, listW=285, listH=modal.height-180;
        drawSlicedFrame(g,listX,listY,listW,listH,"inner");
        java.util.List<String> entries = infopediaEntries(infopediaTab);
        g.setFont(uiFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT)); center(g,tabs[infopediaTab]+" INDEX",listX+listW/2,listY+32);
        drawInfopediaEntryList(g, entries, listX+14, listY+62, listW-34, listH-108);
        int detailX=listX+listW+24, detailY=listY, detailW=modal.x+modal.width-detailX-30, detailH=listH;
        drawSlicedFrame(g,detailX,detailY,detailW,detailH,"inner");
        String entry = entries.isEmpty()?"No entry":entries.get(Math.max(0,Math.min(infopediaSelected,entries.size()-1)));
        drawInfopediaIcon(g, detailX+24, detailY+52, 128, 128, infopediaTab, entry);
        java.util.List<String> details = infopediaDetailLinesWithRelated(infopediaTab, entry);
        drawScrollableWrappedLines(g, details, detailX+178, detailY+58, detailW-210, detailH-96, infopediaDetailScroll, "infopedia-detail");
    }

    void drawInfopediaEntryList(Graphics2D g, java.util.List<String> entries, int x, int y, int w, int h) {
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineH = Math.max(20, fm.getHeight()+4);
        int visible = Math.max(1, h / lineH);
        int maxScroll = Math.max(0, entries.size() - visible);
        infopediaScroll = Math.max(0, Math.min(infopediaScroll, maxScroll));
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(x-4,y-4,w+8,h+8);
        int yy = y + lineH;
        for(int row=0; row<visible; row++) {
            int idx = infopediaScroll + row;
            if (idx >= entries.size()) break;
            boolean sel = idx == infopediaSelected;
            if (sel) {
                g.setColor(new Color(80,65,30,220));
                g.fillRoundRect(x-6, yy-lineH+3, w+4, lineH, 8, 8);
            }
            g.setColor(sel ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            String label = (sel ? "> " : "  ") + entries.get(idx);
            g.drawString(label, x, yy);
            yy += lineH;
        }
        g.setClip(old);
        int sbX=x+w+10, sbY=y, sbW=14, sbH=h;
        g.setColor(new Color(20,18,14,235)); g.fillRect(sbX,sbY,sbW,sbH);
        g.setColor(new Color(108,92,58)); g.drawRect(sbX,sbY,sbW,sbH);
        int th=maxScroll<=0?h:Math.max(28,h*visible/Math.max(visible,entries.size())); int ty=maxScroll<=0?y:y+(h-th)*infopediaScroll/maxScroll;
        g.setColor("infopedia-list".equals(activeScrollTag)?optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT):new Color(220,190,105));
        g.fillRect(sbX+2,ty+2,sbW-3,Math.max(6,th-3));
        scrollRegions.add(new ScrollRegion("infopedia-list", new Rectangle(sbX, sbY, sbW, sbH), new Rectangle(sbX+2,ty+2,sbW-3,Math.max(6,th-3)), maxScroll, visible, infopediaScroll));
    }

    void drawInfopediaIcon(Graphics2D g, int x, int y, int w, int h, int tab, String entry) {
        drawSlicedFrame(g,x,y,w,h,"inner");
        g.setColor(new Color(12,16,14)); g.fillRect(x+10,y+10,w-20,h-20);
        if (isAssetInfopediaTab(tab)) {
            drawSemanticAssetInfopediaIcon(g, x, y, w, h, entry);
            return;
        }
        if (tab == 17) {
            drawTileInfopediaIcon(g, x, y, w, h, entry);
            return;
        }
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT)); g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(34f));
        String glyph = "?";
        if(tab==0) glyph="Z"; else if(tab==1) glyph="R"; else if(tab==2) glyph="I"; else if(tab==3) glyph="W"; else if(tab==4) glyph="S"; else if(tab==5) glyph="C"; else if(tab==6) glyph="B"; else if(tab==7) glyph="M"; else if(tab==8) glyph="N"; else glyph="F";
        center(g,glyph,x+w/2,y+h/2+10);
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM)); center(g,"reference icon",x+w/2,y+h-18);
    }

    void drawSemanticAssetInfopediaIcon(Graphics2D g, int x, int y, int w, int h, String entry) {
        java.util.Optional<AssetMetadata> meta = SemanticAssetInfopediaAuthority.metadataForEntry(AssetManager.registry(), entry);
        if (meta.isEmpty()) {
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            g.setFont(smallFont);
            center(g, "asset index", x + w/2, y + h/2 - 8);
            center(g, "select an asset ID", x + w/2, y + h/2 + 12);
            return;
        }
        ImageIcon icon = AssetManager.getAsset(meta.get().id());
        Image image = icon == null ? null : icon.getImage();
        int ix = x + 14, iy = y + 14, iw = w - 28, ih = h - 44;
        g.setColor(new Color(4,5,5,245));
        g.fillRect(ix, iy, iw, ih);
        g.setColor(new Color(115,96,58));
        g.drawRect(ix, iy, iw, ih);
        if (image != null) {
            int srcW = Math.max(1, icon.getIconWidth());
            int srcH = Math.max(1, icon.getIconHeight());
            double scale = Math.min((double)(iw - 8) / srcW, (double)(ih - 8) / srcH);
            int dw = Math.max(1, (int)Math.round(srcW * scale));
            int dh = Math.max(1, (int)Math.round(srcH * scale));
            int dx = ix + (iw - dw) / 2;
            int dy = iy + (ih - dh) / 2;
            g.drawImage(image, dx, dy, dw, dh, null);
        } else {
            g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(28f));
            g.setColor(new Color(205,80,70));
            center(g, "?", x + w/2, y + h/2);
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, meta.get().id(), x + w/2, y + h - 18);
    }

    void drawTileInfopediaIcon(Graphics2D g, int x, int y, int w, int h, String entry) {
        TileInfopediaAuthority.Entry e = TileInfopediaAuthority.find(entry);
        if (e == null || TileInfopediaAuthority.isHeader(entry)) {
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            g.setFont(smallFont);
            center(g, "tile family", x + w/2, y + h/2);
            return;
        }
        int cells = Math.max(1, Math.min(5, e.aliases.length));
        int pad = 14;
        int cell = Math.max(22, Math.min((w - pad*2 - (cells-1)*5) / cells, h - 48));
        int totalW = cells * cell + (cells-1)*5;
        int xx = x + (w - totalW) / 2;
        int yy = y + 22;
        for (int i=0; i<cells; i++) {
            BufferedImage img = images == null ? null : images.getTile(e.aliases[i], e.glyph == null ? '?' : e.glyph.charValue());
            g.setColor(new Color(4,5,5,240));
            g.fillRect(xx + i*(cell+5), yy, cell, cell);
            g.setColor(new Color(115,96,58));
            g.drawRect(xx + i*(cell+5), yy, cell, cell);
            if (img != null) {
                g.drawImage(img, xx + i*(cell+5)+2, yy+2, cell-4, cell-4, null);
            } else {
                g.setFont(smallFont);
                g.setColor(new Color(205,80,70));
                center(g, "?", xx + i*(cell+5)+cell/2, yy + cell/2 + 5);
            }
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        String label = e.primaryAlias() == null ? e.label : e.primaryAlias();
        center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(label, g.getFontMetrics(), w-20), x + w/2, y + h - 18);
    }


    void clampButtonsToVisibleMenuBounds() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        Rectangle screenSafe = new Rectangle(12, 12, Math.max(1, W - 24), Math.max(1, H - 24));
        Rectangle optionPanelSafe = optionPanelInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle commandSafe = commandPanelInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle inventoryActionSafe = inventoryActionInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle worldSetupActionSafe = worldSetupActionInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle saveLoadSafe = saveLoadButtonSafeRect();

        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
            Rectangle safe = screenSafe;
            if (screen == Screen.OPTIONS && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = isGraphicsDropdownButton(b) ? graphicsDropdownInnerRect() : optionPanelSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD") ? worldSetupGenerateInnerSafeRect() : worldSetupActionSafe;
            else if (isCommandSurfaceButton(b)) safe = commandSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.INVENTORY && isInventoryActionButton(b)) safe = inventoryActionSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.SAVELOAD && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = saveLoadSafe;
            fitButtonInto(b, safe);
        }

        if (screen == Screen.GAME) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> group = commandSurfaceButtons();
            flowButtonGroup(group, commandSafe, 1);
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.INVENTORY) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> group = inventoryActionButtons();
            flowButtonGroup(group, inventoryActionSafe, 1);
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.SAVELOAD) {
            flowSaveLoadButtons();
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelUsesCommandSurface()) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> group = commandSurfaceButtons();
            int cols = group.size() > 14 || panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH ? 2 : 1;
            flowButtonGroup(group, commandSafe, cols);
        } else if (screen == Screen.OPTIONS) {
            flowOptionsButtons(optionPanelSafe);
        } else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> actionGroup = new ArrayList<>();
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK") && !b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD")) actionGroup.add(b);
            flowButtonGroup(actionGroup, worldSetupActionSafe, 2);
            Rectangle genSafe = worldSetupGenerateInnerSafeRect();
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (b.label != null && b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD")) { b.r = new Rectangle(genSafe.x, genSafe.y, genSafe.width, Math.max(22, Math.min(30, genSafe.height))); }
        }

        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
            Rectangle safe = screenSafe;
            if (screen == Screen.OPTIONS && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = isGraphicsDropdownButton(b) ? graphicsDropdownInnerRect() : optionPanelSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD") ? worldSetupGenerateInnerSafeRect() : worldSetupActionSafe;
            else if (isCommandSurfaceButton(b)) safe = commandSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.INVENTORY && isInventoryActionButton(b)) safe = inventoryActionSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.SAVELOAD && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = saveLoadSafe;
            fitButtonInto(b, safe);
        }
    }


    void applySemanticButtonIcons() {
        if (buttons == null || buttons.isEmpty()) return;
        if (screen == Screen.PANEL && (panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH)) {
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
                if (b == null || b.label == null || "BACK".equals(b.label)) continue;
                if (b.label.startsWith("DEF INFO") || b.label.startsWith("VALIDATE") || b.label.startsWith("CLAIM") || b.label.startsWith("STASH") || b.label.startsWith("TAKE") || b.label.startsWith("DRINK") || b.label.startsWith("SECURITY")) continue;
                BufferedImage icon = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForAssetId(ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForName(b.label));
                if (icon != null) b.icon = icon;
                if (b.tip != null && !b.tip.contains("Semantic object asset:")) b.tip = b.tip + " " + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.semanticSummaryForName(b.label);
            }
        } else if (screen == Screen.EDITOR) {
            String category = inGameEditorPaletteCategory();
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
                if (b == null || b.label == null) continue;
                String clean = b.label.replace("▶", "").trim();
                if (clean.isBlank() || clean.equals("BACK") || clean.startsWith("NEW") || clean.equals("UNDO") || clean.equals("REDO") || clean.startsWith("HELP")) continue;
                String id = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForEditorPalette(category, clean);
                BufferedImage icon = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForAssetId(id);
                if (icon != null) b.icon = icon;
                if (b.tip != null && !b.tip.contains("assetId=")) b.tip = b.tip + " assetId=" + id + ".";
            }
        }
    }

    void assignButtonDebugIds() {
        for (int i=0; i<buttons.size(); i++) {
            ButtonBox b = buttons.get(i);
            if (b != null) b.uiDebugId = i + 1;
        }
    }

    void stampUiFrameId(Graphics2D g, String prefix, String label, int x, int y, int w, int h) {
        if (g == null || w < 28 || h < 18) return;
        String safePrefix = prefix == null ? "F" : prefix;
        int hash = Math.abs(Objects.hash(safePrefix, label, x/3, y/3, w/3, h/3, screen, panelMode)) % 10000;
        String id = safePrefix + String.format(Locale.US, "%04d", hash);
        Font oldFont = g.getFont();
        Color oldColor = g.getColor();
        g.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, 9));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int tw = fm.stringWidth(id);
        int bx = Math.max(x + 2, x + w - tw - 6);
        int by = y + 3;
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,188));
        g.fillRect(bx - 2, by, tw + 4, fm.getHeight() + 1);
        g.setColor(new Color(245,220,130));
        g.drawString(id, bx, by + fm.getAscent());
        g.setFont(oldFont);
        g.setColor(oldColor);
    }

    Rectangle worldSetupGenerateInnerSafeRect() {
        int w = getWidth(), h = getHeight();
        int margin = Math.max(34, w / 22);
        int top = Math.max(122, h / 5);
        int gap = Math.max(14, w / 55);
        int totalW = w - margin * 2;
        int infoW = Math.max(360, (int)(totalW * 0.58));
        int buttonX = margin + infoW + gap;
        int buttonW = Math.max(190, w - buttonX - margin);
        return new Rectangle(buttonX + 14, top + 40, Math.max(1, buttonW - 28), 34);
    }

    Rectangle optionPanelInnerSafeRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int panelX = Math.max(34, W/2 - Math.min(620, W/2 - 34));
        int panelY = Math.max(34, H / 22);
        int panelW = Math.min(W - panelX * 2, Math.max(980, W - 90));
        int panelH = Math.max(430, H - panelY - 64);
        return new Rectangle(panelX + 36, panelY + 36, Math.max(1, panelW - 72), Math.max(1, panelH - 84));
    }

    Rectangle optionTabSafeRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int panelX = Math.max(34, W/2 - Math.min(620, W/2 - 34));
        int panelY = Math.max(34, H / 22);
        int panelW = Math.min(W - panelX * 2, Math.max(980, W - 90));
        return new Rectangle(panelX + 44, panelY + 38, Math.max(1, panelW - 88), Math.max(22, Math.min(30, scaled(30))));
    }

    Rectangle optionControlInnerSafeRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int panelX = Math.max(34, W/2 - Math.min(620, W/2 - 34));
        int panelY = Math.max(34, H / 22);
        int panelW = Math.min(W - panelX * 2, Math.max(980, W - 90));
        int panelH = Math.max(430, H - panelY - 64);
        int controlsBoxX = panelX + 44;
        int controlsBoxY = panelY + 108;
        int controlsBoxW = panelW - 88;
        int controlsBoxH = Math.max(116, Math.min(188, panelH / 4));
        return new Rectangle(controlsBoxX + 12, controlsBoxY + 12, Math.max(1, controlsBoxW - 24), Math.max(1, controlsBoxH - 24));
    }

    Rectangle graphicsDropdownOuterRect() {
        if (screen != Screen.OPTIONS || graphicsDropdown < 0 || (optionsTab != 0 && optionsTab != 1 && optionsTab != 4)) return new Rectangle(0,0,0,0);
        int w = getWidth(), h = getHeight();
        Rectangle optionSafe = optionControlInnerSafeRect();
        int requestedCols = optionsTab == 7 ? 4 : 3;
        int colGap = Math.max(6, GuiLayoutApi.columnGap(uiScaleFactor()) - 4);
        int bw = Math.max(104, (optionSafe.width - colGap * (requestedCols - 1)) / requestedCols);
        int gap = bw + colGap;
        int y = optionSafe.y;
        int itemCount;
        int x;
        int ddY;
        int ddW;
        if (graphicsDropdown == 0) {
            itemCount = 3; x = optionSafe.x; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 1) {
            itemCount = Math.min(DisplayResolutionAuthority.choiceCount(), Math.max(8, Math.min(14, optionSafe.height / Math.max(22, scaled(26))))); x = optionSafe.x + gap; ddY = y + Math.max(24, Math.min(34, optionSafe.height / 6)); ddW = bw * 2 + colGap;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 2) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.PALETTE_NAMES.length; x = optionSafe.x + gap; ddY = optionsTab == 4 ? y + scaled(198) : y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 3) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.DOWNSCALE_LABELS.length; x = optionSafe.x; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 4) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.TARGET_FPS_LABELS.length; x = optionSafe.x + gap; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 5) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.RENDER_QUALITY_LABELS.length; x = optionSafe.x + gap*2; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else return new Rectangle(0,0,0,0);
        int rowH = Math.max(26, scaled(30));
        int ddH = Math.max(rowH + 18, 18 + itemCount * rowH + Math.max(0, itemCount - 1) * scaled(4));
        Rectangle controls = optionControlInnerSafeRect();
        int maxBottom = Math.max(controls.y + controls.height + 24, getHeight() - 76);
        if (ddY + ddH > maxBottom) ddY = Math.max(controls.y, maxBottom - ddH);
        int minX = Math.max(24, optionPanelInnerSafeRect().x);
        int maxX = Math.max(minX, optionPanelInnerSafeRect().x + optionPanelInnerSafeRect().width - ddW);
        x = Math.max(minX, Math.min(x, maxX));
        return new Rectangle(x, ddY, Math.max(120, ddW), ddH);
    }

    Rectangle graphicsDropdownInnerRect() {
        Rectangle r = graphicsDropdownOuterRect();
        return new Rectangle(r.x + 9, r.y + 9, Math.max(1, r.width - 18), Math.max(1, r.height - 18));
    }

    Rectangle commandPanelInnerSafeRect() {
        Rectangle cmd = commandPanelRect();
        return new Rectangle(cmd.x + 14, cmd.y + 52, Math.max(1, cmd.width - 28), Math.max(1, cmd.height - 66));
    }

    Rectangle worldSetupActionInnerSafeRect() {
        int w = getWidth(), h = getHeight();
        int margin = Math.max(34, w / 22);
        int top = Math.max(122, h / 5);
        int gap = Math.max(14, w / 55);
        int totalW = w - margin * 2;
        int infoW = Math.max(360, (int)(totalW * 0.58));
        int buttonX = margin + infoW + gap;
        int buttonW = Math.max(190, w - buttonX - margin);
        int panelH = Math.max(310, h - top - 92);
        int y = top + 142;
        int bottom = top + panelH - 14;
        return new Rectangle(buttonX + 14, y, Math.max(1, buttonW - 28), Math.max(1, bottom - y));
    }

    Rectangle inventoryActionInnerSafeRect() {
        int W=getWidth(), H=getHeight();
        int x=Math.max(36, W/2 - Math.min(880, W-72)/2);
        int y=Math.max(68, H/2 - Math.min(440, H-110)/2);
        int w=Math.min(880, W - x*2);
        int h=Math.min(440, H - y - 54);
        int gap=Math.max(12, scaled(12));
        int top=y+128;
        int bottomBoxH=Math.max(78, Math.min(108, h/4));
        int colH=Math.max(110, h - (top-y) - bottomBoxH - 26);
        int actionW=Math.max(150, Math.min(210, w/4));
        int invW=Math.max(180, (w - 52 - actionW - gap*2)/2);
        int targetW=Math.max(180, w - 52 - actionW - gap*2 - invW);
        int actionX=x+24+invW+gap+targetW+gap;
        return new Rectangle(actionX + 12, top + 50, Math.max(1, actionW - 24), Math.max(1, colH - 62));
    }

    boolean panelUsesCommandSurface() {
        return panelMode == PanelMode.INTERACT || panelMode == PanelMode.COMBAT || panelMode == PanelMode.SCAVENGE || panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH || panelMode == PanelMode.BASES || panelMode == PanelMode.TRADE;
    }

    boolean isCommandSurfaceButton(ButtonBox b) {
        if (b == null || b.label == null || b.label.equals("BACK")) return false;
        // Phase 4 containment rule: command-surface membership is semantic, not
        // geometric. Several older panels originally placed their buttons beside or
        // below the command tablet and then expected later code to corral them. If
        // we decide membership by rectangle intersection, those off-frame buttons
        // are never reclaimed and can spill down the screen.
        return screen == Screen.GAME || (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelUsesCommandSurface());
    }

    java.util.List<ButtonBox> commandSurfaceButtons() {
        ArrayList<ButtonBox> out = new ArrayList<>();
        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (isCommandSurfaceButton(b)) out.add(b);
        out.sort(Comparator.comparingInt((ButtonBox b) -> b.r.y).thenComparingInt(b -> b.r.x));
        return out;
    }

    boolean isInventoryActionButton(ButtonBox b) {
        if (b == null || b.label == null) return false;
        String l = b.label;
        return l.equals("USE / EQUIP") || l.equals("TAKE TARGET") || l.equals("TAKE ALL") || l.equals("DROP ONE") || l.equals("INSPECT") || l.equals("THROW LIGHT");
    }

    java.util.List<ButtonBox> inventoryActionButtons() {
        ArrayList<ButtonBox> out = new ArrayList<>();
        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (isInventoryActionButton(b)) out.add(b);
        return out;
    }

    java.util.List<ButtonBox> buttonsInside(Rectangle safe, boolean excludeBack) {
        ArrayList<ButtonBox> out = new ArrayList<>();
        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (b != null && b.r.intersects(safe) && (!excludeBack || (b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")))) out.add(b);
        out.sort(Comparator.comparingInt((ButtonBox b) -> b.r.y).thenComparingInt(b -> b.r.x));
        return out;
    }

    void fitButtonInto(ButtonBox b, Rectangle safe) {
        if (b == null || safe == null) return;
        b.r.width = Math.max(26, Math.min(b.r.width, safe.width));
        b.r.height = Math.max(16, Math.min(b.r.height, safe.height));
        if (b.r.x < safe.x) b.r.x = safe.x;
        if (b.r.y < safe.y) b.r.y = safe.y;
        if (b.r.x + b.r.width > safe.x + safe.width) b.r.x = safe.x + safe.width - b.r.width;
        if (b.r.y + b.r.height > safe.y + safe.height) b.r.y = safe.y + safe.height - b.r.height;
    }

    void flowButtonGroup(java.util.List<ButtonBox> group, Rectangle safe, int requestedCols) {
        if (group == null || group.isEmpty() || safe == null) return;
        int cols = Math.max(1, Math.min(Math.max(1, requestedCols), Math.max(1, group.size())));
        int rows = (int)Math.ceil(group.size() / (double)cols);
        int gap = Math.max(3, Math.min(6, scaled(5)));
        int colW = Math.max(34, (safe.width - gap * (cols - 1)) / cols);
        int bh = Math.max(16, Math.min(28, (safe.height - gap * Math.max(0, rows - 1)) / Math.max(1, rows)));
        for (int i=0; i<group.size(); i++) {
            ButtonBox b = group.get(i);
            int col = i % cols;
            int row = i / cols;
            b.r.x = safe.x + col * (colW + gap);
            b.r.y = safe.y + row * (bh + gap);
            b.r.width = colW;
            b.r.height = bh;
            fitButtonInto(b, safe);
        }
    }

    void flowOptionsButtons(Rectangle safe) {
        if (safe == null) return;
        ArrayList<ButtonBox> tabs = new ArrayList<>();
        ArrayList<ButtonBox> content = new ArrayList<>();
        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
            if (b.label == null || b.label.equals("BACK")) continue;
            if (b.label.equals("DISPLAY") || b.label.equals("TEXT") || b.label.equals("SOUND") || b.label.equals("CONTROLS") || b.label.equals("GRAPHICS") || b.label.equals("JVM") || b.label.equals("ACCESS") || b.label.equals("QOL")) tabs.add(b);
            else if (!isGraphicsDropdownButton(b)) content.add(b);
        }
        Rectangle tabSafe = optionTabSafeRect();
        if (!tabs.isEmpty()) flowButtonGroup(tabs, tabSafe, Math.min(8, tabs.size()));
        Rectangle contentSafe = optionControlInnerSafeRect();
        int cols = optionsTab == 7 ? 4 : (content.size() > 8 ? 3 : (content.size() > 4 ? 2 : 1));
        flowButtonGroup(content, contentSafe, cols);
        if (graphicsDropdown >= 0) {
            Rectangle ddSafe = graphicsDropdownInnerRect();
            ArrayList<ButtonBox> dd = new ArrayList<>();
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (isGraphicsDropdownButton(b)) dd.add(b);
            flowButtonGroup(dd, ddSafe, 1);
        }
    }


    static final class SaveLoadUiRects {
        final Rectangle outer, info, manual, auto;
        SaveLoadUiRects(Rectangle outer, Rectangle info, Rectangle manual, Rectangle auto) { this.outer=outer; this.info=info; this.manual=manual; this.auto=auto; }
    }

    SaveLoadUiRects saveLoadUiRects() {
        Rectangle modal = uiLayout().modal;
        int x = Math.max(36, modal.x), y = Math.max(56, modal.y - 8);
        int w = Math.min(getWidth() - x*2, modal.width), h = Math.min(getHeight() - y - 40, modal.height + 30);
        int infoH = Math.max(72, h/4);
        Rectangle info = new Rectangle(x+28, y+58, Math.max(1, w-56), infoH);
        int listsY = y + 58 + infoH + 14;
        int listsH = Math.max(100, h - (listsY - y) - 44);
        int gap = 24;
        int colW = Math.max(120, (w - 72 - gap) / 2);
        int mx = x + 28, ax = mx + colW + gap;
        return new SaveLoadUiRects(new Rectangle(x,y,w,h), info, new Rectangle(mx, listsY, colW, listsH), new Rectangle(ax, listsY, colW, listsH));
    }

    Rectangle saveLoadButtonSafeRect() {
        SaveLoadUiRects sl = saveLoadUiRects();
        return sl.outer == null ? new Rectangle(0,0,1,1) : new Rectangle(sl.outer.x + 18, sl.outer.y + 18, Math.max(1, sl.outer.width - 36), Math.max(1, sl.outer.height - 36));
    }

    void flowSaveLoadButtons() {
        SaveLoadUiRects sl = saveLoadUiRects();
        if (sl == null) return;
        int rowGap = Math.max(4, scaled(4));
        int topButtonH = Math.max(18, Math.min(24, sl.manual.height / 10));
        int topButtonW = Math.max(104, Math.min(184, sl.manual.width / 4));
        int topY = sl.manual.y + 44;
        int rowStart = sl.manual.y + 84;
        int manualAvailable = Math.max(72, sl.manual.y + sl.manual.height - 18 - rowStart);
        int rowH = Math.max(18, Math.min(26, (manualAvailable - rowGap * Math.max(0, SAVE_SLOT_COUNT - 1)) / Math.max(1, SAVE_SLOT_COUNT)));
        int loadW = Math.max(92, Math.min(160, sl.manual.width / 5));
        int saveW = Math.max(76, Math.min(130, sl.manual.width / 6));
        int saveX = sl.manual.x + sl.manual.width - 14 - saveW;
        int loadX = Math.max(sl.manual.x + 14, saveX - 8 - loadW);
        int autoAvailable = Math.max(90, sl.auto.y + sl.auto.height - 18 - rowStart);
        int autoRowH = Math.max(18, Math.min(26, (autoAvailable - rowGap * 4) / 5));
        int autoButtonW = Math.max(112, Math.min(190, sl.auto.width / 3));
        int autoButtonX = sl.auto.x + sl.auto.width - 14 - autoButtonW;
        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
            if (b == null || b.label == null) continue;
            String l = b.label;
            if (l.equals("SAVE DIAGNOSTIC")) b.r = new Rectangle(sl.manual.x + sl.manual.width - 14 - topButtonW, topY, topButtonW, topButtonH);
            else if (l.equals("LOAD MENU")) b.r = new Rectangle(sl.auto.x + sl.auto.width - 14 - topButtonW, topY, topButtonW, topButtonH);
            else if (l.startsWith("MANUAL ") && l.endsWith(" LOAD")) {
                int n = Character.isDigit(l.charAt(7)) ? Character.digit(l.charAt(7), 10) : 1;
                b.r = new Rectangle(loadX, rowStart + (Math.max(1,n)-1)*(rowH+rowGap), loadW, rowH);
            } else if (l.startsWith("SAVE ")) {
                int n = Character.isDigit(l.charAt(5)) ? Character.digit(l.charAt(5), 10) : 1;
                b.r = new Rectangle(saveX, rowStart + (Math.max(1,n)-1)*(rowH+rowGap), saveW, rowH);
            } else if (l.startsWith("AUTO ")) {
                int n = Character.isDigit(l.charAt(5)) ? Character.digit(l.charAt(5), 10) : 1;
                b.r = new Rectangle(autoButtonX, rowStart + (Math.max(1,n)-1)*(autoRowH+rowGap), autoButtonW, autoRowH);
            }
            fitButtonInto(b, saveLoadButtonSafeRect());
        }
    }

    void moveSelectedButton(int delta) {
        if (buttons.isEmpty()) return;
        selectedButton = Math.floorMod(selectedButton + delta, buttons.size());
        sounds.play("tab", options);
        DebugLog.audit("UI_BUTTON_SELECT", "selected=" + selectedButton + " label=" + buttons.get(selectedButton).label + " via keyboard | " + stateSummary());
        repaint();
    }

    void activateSelectedButtonUniversal() {
        if (buttons.isEmpty()) return;
        selectedButton = Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedButton, buttons.size()-1));
        ButtonBox b = buttons.get(selectedButton);
        if (!buttonIsModalInteractive(b)) { sounds.play("panelClose", options); return; }
        sounds.play("button", options);
        DebugLog.audit("UI_BUTTON_CONFIRM", "label=" + b.label + " via E/Enter | " + stateSummary());
        runGuarded("BUTTON", "universal confirm " + b.label, b.action);
        repaint();
    }

    void drawPanelBox(Graphics2D g, int x, int y, int w, int h, String title) {
        g.setColor(new Color(4, 7, 6, 232));
        g.fillRect(x, y, w, h);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, x, y, w, h, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", title, x, y, w, h);
        if (title != null && !title.isBlank()) {
            g.setFont(uiFont);
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE));
            g.drawString(title, x+18, y+32);
        }
    }

void drawWrappedPanelLines(Graphics2D g, java.util.List<String> lines, int x, int y, int w, int h) {
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineH = Math.max(20, fm.getHeight() + 4);
        int maxChars = Math.max(24, w / Math.max(7, fm.charWidth('M')));
        int yy = y;
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(x-4, y-lineH, w+20, h+lineH);
        for (String raw : lines) {
            Color c = new Color(220, 208, 145); // readable lighter yellow on green/black GUI
            if (raw.contains("Warning") || raw.contains("invalid") || raw.contains("FAILED") || raw.contains("Starving")) c = new Color(245, 120, 90);
            else if (raw.startsWith("  -") || raw.startsWith("  ")) c = new Color(205, 198, 155);
            else if (raw.endsWith(":")) c = new Color(235, 220, 150);
            g.setColor(c);
            for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap(raw, maxChars)) {
                if (yy > y + h) break;
                g.drawString(line, x, yy);
                yy += lineH;
            }
            if (yy > y + h) break;
        }
        g.setClip(old);
        int needed = Math.max(0, lines.size() * lineH - h);
        if (needed > 0) {
            g.setColor(new Color(55, 46, 30));
            g.fillRect(x + w + 6, y - lineH + 4, 8, h);
            g.setColor(new Color(220, 190, 105));
            g.fillRect(x + w + 6, y - lineH + 4, 8, Math.max(24, h / 4));
        }
    }

    void drawPortrait(Graphics2D g, int x, int y, Candidate c) {
        g.setColor(new Color(22,22,24)); g.fillRect(x,y,140,150);
        g.setColor(new Color(160,150,110)); g.drawRect(x,y,140,150);
        NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry locked = NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.unlockedEntry(cachedOperatorProfileName, c == null ? "" : c.name);
        BufferedImage face = null;
        String portraitLabel = "IMPORTED DOSSIER";
        if (locked != null) {
            face = images.getNameLockedProfilePortrait(locked.key);
            portraitLabel = "PROFILE DOSSIER";
            if (c != null) c.nameLockedProfileKey = locked.key;
        }
        if (face == null && c != null) face = images.getPortrait(c.portraitSheet, c.portraitIndex);
        if (face != null) {
            g.drawImage(face, x+6, y+6, 128, 128, null);
            g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(new Color(190,180,130));
            g.drawString(portraitLabel, x+10, y+145);
        } else {
            g.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, 18));
            for (int i=0;i<c.portrait.length;i++) g.drawString(c.portrait[i], x+30, y+35+i*20);
        }
    }

    boolean isGameOverlayPanel() {
        return screen == Screen.GAME || (screen == Screen.PANEL && (panelMode == PanelMode.LOOK || panelMode == PanelMode.COMBAT || panelMode == PanelMode.INTERACT || panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH));
    }

    UiLayout uiLayout() {
        if (screen == Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT) return UiLayout.computeSectorAudit(getWidth(), getHeight(), uiScaleFactor());
        return UiLayout.compute(getWidth(), getHeight(), uiScaleFactor());
    }

    UiLayout virtualUiLayout() {
        // Input events are mapped from physical Swing pixels into the fixed virtual
        // render canvas before they reach gameplay code. Mouse-to-tile conversion
        // must therefore use the same virtual layout that drawGame used, not the
        // live Swing panel bounds; otherwise zoom/letterbox scaling pulls targeting
        // toward the upper-left corner.
        if (screen == Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT) return UiLayout.computeSectorAudit(renderScaling.virtualWidth(), renderScaling.virtualHeight(), uiScaleFactor());
        return UiLayout.compute(renderScaling.virtualWidth(), renderScaling.virtualHeight(), uiScaleFactor());
    }

    static class UiLayout {
        final Rectangle root, topBar, map, command, tactical, modal, leftInfo;
        UiLayout(Rectangle root, Rectangle topBar, Rectangle map, Rectangle command, Rectangle tactical, Rectangle modal, Rectangle leftInfo) {
            this.root=root; this.topBar=topBar; this.map=map; this.command=command; this.tactical=tactical; this.modal=modal; this.leftInfo=leftInfo;
        }
        static UiLayout compute(int w, int h, double scale) {
            int margin = Math.max(12, (int)Math.round(16*scale));
            int topH = Math.max(24, (int)Math.round(30*scale));
            int bottomH = Math.max(92, Math.min(128, (int)Math.round(110*scale)));
            int actionFeedH = Math.max(66, Math.min(88, (int)Math.round(76*scale)));
            int gap = Math.max(6, (int)Math.round(8*scale));
            int commandW = Math.max(132, Math.min(184, (int)Math.round(152*scale)));
            int y = margin + topH + gap;
            int commandX = w - margin - commandW;
            int mapX = margin + 12;
            int mapW = Math.max(360, commandX - mapX - gap);
            int mapH = Math.max(230, h - y - bottomH - actionFeedH - margin - gap * 2);
            Rectangle root = new Rectangle(0,0,w,h);
            Rectangle top = new Rectangle(margin+12, margin+4, Math.max(1,w-margin*2-24), topH);
            Rectangle map = new Rectangle(mapX, y, mapW, mapH);
            Rectangle cmd = new Rectangle(commandX, y, commandW, Math.max(180, h-y-margin));
            Rectangle tactical = new Rectangle(mapX, y + mapH + actionFeedH + gap, mapW, bottomH);
            Rectangle modal = new Rectangle(margin+36, y, Math.max(420, w-(margin+36)*2), Math.max(300, h-y-margin-bottomH/3));
            Rectangle left = new Rectangle(margin+12, y, Math.max(240, Math.min(340, mapW/3)), mapH);
            return new UiLayout(root, top, map, cmd, tactical, modal, left);
        }

        static UiLayout computeSectorAudit(int w, int h, double scale) {
            int margin = Math.max(8, (int)Math.round(12*scale));
            int gap = Math.max(5, (int)Math.round(6*scale));
            int commandW = Math.max(118, Math.min(166, (int)Math.round(142*scale)));
            int bottomH = Math.max(80, Math.min(112, (int)Math.round(94*scale)));
            int y = margin + gap;
            int commandX = w - margin - commandW;
            int mapX = margin + 12;
            int mapW = Math.max(360, commandX - mapX - gap);
            int mapH = Math.max(260, h - y - bottomH - margin - gap * 2);
            Rectangle root = new Rectangle(0,0,w,h);
            Rectangle top = new Rectangle(margin+12, margin, Math.max(1,w-margin*2-24), Math.max(1, gap));
            Rectangle map = new Rectangle(mapX, y, mapW, mapH);
            Rectangle cmd = new Rectangle(commandX, y, commandW, Math.max(180, h-y-margin));
            Rectangle tactical = new Rectangle(mapX, y + mapH + gap, mapW, bottomH);
            Rectangle modal = new Rectangle(margin+36, y, Math.max(420, w-(margin+36)*2), Math.max(300, h-y-margin-bottomH/3));
            Rectangle left = new Rectangle(margin+12, y, Math.max(240, Math.min(340, mapW/3)), mapH);
            return new UiLayout(root, top, map, cmd, tactical, modal, left);
        }
    }

    Rectangle mapRect() { return uiLayout().map; }

    Rectangle inputMapRect() { return virtualUiLayout().map; }

    Rectangle tacticalSlateRect() { return uiLayout().tactical; }

    Rectangle commandPanelRect() { return uiLayout().command; }

    boolean tileIconMode() {
        return options.tileIconRendering && images.hasTileArt();
    }

    boolean sectorAuditTileIconMode() {
        // The Zone Audit surface is a visual-generation inspection tool. If packaged tile
        // art exists, it should display that art even when the normal play map is set
        // to ASCII/gradient fallback, otherwise road/floor art regressions are hidden.
        return images != null && images.hasTileArt();
    }

    int zoomedMapPixels(int basePixels) {
        return Math.max(6, (int)Math.round(basePixels * (options.worldZoomPercent() / 100.0)));
    }

    int mapCellW(Graphics2D g) {
        if (tileIconMode()) return scaled(zoomedMapPixels(options.mapTilePixelSize()));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics(asciiFont);
        return Math.max(8, scaled(zoomedMapPixels(Math.max(10, fm.charWidth('W')))));
    }

    int mapCellH(Graphics2D g) {
        if (tileIconMode()) return scaled(zoomedMapPixels(options.mapTilePixelSize()));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics(asciiFont);
        return Math.max(10, scaled(zoomedMapPixels(Math.max(14, fm.getHeight()))));
    }

    Font auditAsciiFont() {
        return asciiFont == null ? new Font("Monospaced", Font.PLAIN, 11) : asciiFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, asciiFont.getSize2D() - 3f));
    }

    int auditTileIconPixels() {
        int base = options == null ? 32 : options.mapTilePixelSize();
        return Math.max(16, Math.min(base, (int)Math.round(base * 0.78)));
    }

    int auditMapCellW(Graphics2D g) {
        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) return scaled(zoomedMapPixels(auditTileIconPixels()));
        Font use = auditAsciiFont();
        FontMetrics fm = g == null ? getFontMetrics(use) : g.getFontMetrics(use);
        return Math.max(7, scaled(zoomedMapPixels(Math.max(8, fm.charWidth('W')))));
    }

    int auditMapCellH(Graphics2D g) {
        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) return scaled(zoomedMapPixels(auditTileIconPixels()));
        Font use = auditAsciiFont();
        FontMetrics fm = g == null ? getFontMetrics(use) : g.getFontMetrics(use);
        return Math.max(9, scaled(zoomedMapPixels(Math.max(11, fm.getHeight()))));
    }

    void drawGame(Graphics2D g) {
        g.setFont(asciiFont);
        Rectangle map = mapRect();
        int cellW = mapCellW(g);
        int cellH = mapCellH(g);
        int worldW = world == null ? 0 : world.w;
        int worldH = world == null ? 0 : world.h;
        MapViewportTransformAuthority.Viewport viewport = MapViewportTransformAuthority.compute(
                map, worldW, worldH, playerX, playerY, cellW, cellH,
                10, tileIconMode() ? 10 : 10 + g.getFontMetrics(asciiFont).getAscent());
        int cols = viewport.cols;
        int rows = viewport.rows;
        int camX = viewport.camX;
        int camY = viewport.camY;
        updateSensoryModel("paint");

        // The active map is now a deliberately blank black CRT pane.  The clip prevents
        // ASCII and fog highlights from bleeding into the surrounding chrome or command panel.
        g.setColor(Color.BLACK);
        g.fillRect(map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height);
        g.setColor(new Color(92, 76, 48));
        g.drawRect(map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height);
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(map.x + 7, map.y + 7, map.width - 14, map.height - 14);
        int ox = viewport.ox;
        int oy = viewport.oy;

        if (world != null) {
            for (int sy = 0; sy < rows; sy++) {
                int y = camY + sy;
                if (y < 0 || y >= world.h) continue;
                for (int sx = 0; sx < cols; sx++) {
                    int x = camX + sx;
                    if (x < 0 || x >= world.w) continue;
                    boolean vis = isVisible(x, y);
                    boolean rem = isRemembered(x, y);
                    char ch = world.tiles[x][y];
                    if (vis) {
                        if (tileIconMode()) drawMapTileIcon(g, ch, x, y, ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH, cellW, cellH, 1.0f, true);
                        else { g.setColor(colorForTile(x, y, ch)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(ch), ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH); }
                        drawLightDarknessOverlay(g, x, y, ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH, cellW, cellH, true);
                    } else if (rem) {
                        char memory = ((ch == '#' || InterstitialInfrastructureApi.isInterstitialSolid(ch)) ? '#' : (ch == InterstitialInfrastructureApi.VOID_SPACE ? ' ' : '.'));
                        if (tileIconMode()) drawMapTileIcon(g, memory, x, y, ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH, cellW, cellH, 0.34f, false);
                        else { g.setColor(new Color(42, 42, 45)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(memory), ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH); }
                        drawLightDarknessOverlay(g, x, y, ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH, cellW, cellH, false);
                    }
                }
            }

            for (SensePing ping : sensePings) {
                if (ping.ttl > 0 && !isVisible(ping.x, ping.y) && ping.x >= camX && ping.y >= camY && ping.x < camX + cols && ping.y < camY + rows) {
                    g.setColor(new Color(210, 190, 105));
                    if (tileIconMode()) {
                        int px = ox + (ping.x - camX) * cellW, py = oy + (ping.y - camY) * cellH;
                        g.drawOval(px + cellW/4, py + cellH/4, Math.max(4, cellW/2), Math.max(4, cellH/2));
                        g.drawString("?", px + Math.max(2, cellW/3), py + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
                    } else g.drawString("?", ox + (ping.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (ping.y - camY) * cellH);
                }
            }
            if (world != null && world.mapObjects != null) {
                for (MapObjectState mo : world.mapObjects) {
                    if (mo != null && isVisible(mo.x, mo.y) && mo.x >= camX && mo.y >= camY && mo.x < camX + cols && mo.y < camY + rows && world != null && world.inBounds(mo.x, mo.y) && !isDoorTile(world.tiles[mo.x][mo.y]) && world.tiles[mo.x][mo.y] != 'D') {
                        g.setColor(new Color(170, 215, 155));
                        if (tileIconMode()) drawMapFeatureIcon(g, mo, ox + (mo.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (mo.y - camY) * cellH, cellW, cellH, new Color(100, 210, 160, 70));
                        else g.drawString(String.valueOf(mo.glyph), ox + (mo.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (mo.y - camY) * cellH);
                    }
                }
            }
            for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) {
