                if (isVisible(obj.x, obj.y) && obj.x >= camX && obj.y >= camY && obj.x < camX + cols && obj.y < camY + rows) {
                    g.setColor(new Color(170, 230, 155));
                    if (tileIconMode()) drawMapObjectIcon(g, obj, ox + (obj.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (obj.y - camY) * cellH, cellW, cellH, new Color(120, 230, 135, 80));
                    else g.drawString(String.valueOf(obj.symbol), ox + (obj.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (obj.y - camY) * cellH);
                }
            }
            drawPortableLightObjects(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawZoneLightFixtureObjects(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            visualLighting.render(this, g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawEnvironmentalHazardOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawTrapWarningOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            if (baseClaimed && isVisible(baseX, baseY) && baseX >= camX && baseY >= camY && baseX < camX + cols && baseY < camY + rows) {
                g.setColor(new Color(220, 240, 180));
                if (tileIconMode()) {
                    int px = ox + (baseX - camX) * cellW, py = oy + (baseY - camY) * cellH;
                    g.drawRect(px+2, py+2, Math.max(4,cellW-4), Math.max(4,cellH-4));
                    g.drawString("B", px + Math.max(3,cellW/3), py + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
                } else g.drawString("B", ox + (baseX - camX) * cellW, oy + (baseY - camY) * cellH);
            }
            if ((lookCursorActive || interactCursorActive) && lookX >= camX && lookY >= camY && lookX < camX + cols && lookY < camY + rows) {
                int sx = lookX - camX, sy = lookY - camY;
                g.setColor(interactCursorActive ? new Color(120, 220, 180) : new Color(235, 205, 120));
                int rx = ox + sx * cellW - 2;
                int ry = oy + sy * cellH - 2;
                g.drawRect(rx, ry, cellW + 4, cellH + 4);
            }
            if (buildPlacementActive && buildX >= camX && buildY >= camY && buildX < camX + cols && buildY < camY + rows) {
                int sx = buildX - camX, sy = buildY - camY;
                boolean ok = rawCanPlacePendingBuildAt(buildX, buildY).startsWith("OK");
                g.setColor(ok ? new Color(105, 235, 125) : new Color(235, 70, 55));
                if (tileIconMode()) {
                    g.drawRect(ox + sx * cellW - 2, oy + sy * cellH - 2, cellW + 4, cellH + 4);
                    g.drawString(ok ? "+" : "X", ox + sx * cellW + Math.max(3, cellW/3), oy + sy * cellH + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
                } else {
                    g.drawRect(ox + sx * cellW - 3, oy + sy * cellH - cellH + 2, cellW + 6, cellH + 5);
                    g.drawString(ok ? "+" : "X", ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH);
                }
            }
            drawMovementGhostPath(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawMouseMovementPreview(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawLookIntentOverlay(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawCombatTargetOverlay(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawCombatAnimations(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            drawExplosionAnimations(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            if (world != null) {
                for (NpcEntity npc : world.npcs) {
                    if (npc.x >= camX && npc.y >= camY && npc.x < camX + cols && npc.y < camY + rows && isVisible(npc.x, npc.y)) {
                        g.setColor(npcColor(npc.faction));
                        Point off = npcSlideOffsetPixels(npc, cellW, cellH);
                        if (tileIconMode()) drawNpcMapIcon(g, npc, ox + (npc.x - camX) * cellW + off.x, oy + (npc.y - camY) * cellH + off.y, cellW, cellH);
                        else g.drawString(String.valueOf(npc.symbol), ox + (npc.x - camX) * cellW + off.x, oy + (npc.y - camY) * cellH + off.y);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (playerX >= camX && playerY >= camY && playerX < camX + cols && playerY < camY + rows) {
                g.setColor(Color.WHITE);
                Point off = playerSlideOffsetPixels(cellW, cellH);
                if (tileIconMode()) drawPlayerMapIcon(g, ox + (playerX - camX) * cellW + off.x, oy + (playerY - camY) * cellH + off.y, cellW, cellH);
                else g.drawString("@", ox + (playerX - camX) * cellW + off.x, oy + (playerY - camY) * cellH + off.y);
            }
        }
        g.setClip(oldClip);

        drawRightPanelFrame(g);
        if (tacticalSlateVisible) drawCommandTablet(g, camX, camY);
        drawRecentActionFeed(g);
    }




    void drawLightDarknessOverlay(Graphics2D g, int tx, int ty, int px, int py, int cellW, int cellH, boolean visible) {
        int l = lightLevelAt(tx, ty);
        int alpha;
        if (!visible) alpha = 120;
        else if (l >= 72) alpha = 0;
        else if (l >= 52) alpha = 22;
        else if (l >= 34) alpha = 50;
        else if (l >= 18) alpha = 84;
        else if (l >= 8) alpha = 118;
        else alpha = 150;
        if (alpha <= 0) return;
        int yy = tileIconMode() ? py : py - cellH + 3;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.min(0.85f, alpha / 255f)));
        gg.setColor(Color.BLACK);
        gg.fillRect(px, yy, Math.max(1, cellW), Math.max(1, cellH));
        if (visible && l >= 55) {
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.min(0.18f, (l-50)/220f)));
            gg.setColor(new Color(245, 220, 135));
            gg.fillRect(px, yy, Math.max(1, cellW), Math.max(1, cellH));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }


    TrapRecord trapAt(int x, int y) {
        if (world == null || world.trapRecords == null) return null;
        for (TrapRecord t : world.trapRecords) if (t != null && t.x == x && t.y == y && !"disarmed".equals(t.state)) return t;
        return null;
    }

    void checkTrapAfterPlayerMove(int x, int y) {
        TrapRecord t = trapAt(x, y);
        if (t == null || !t.canTrigger()) return;
        int detection = 25 + stat("Intellect",5)*4 + (lookCursorActive ? 8 : 0);
        if (t.hidden && detection >= t.detectionDifficulty) {
            t.state = "revealed"; t.hidden = false;
            logEvent("You spot a " + t.label + " before fully committing weight to it.");
            return;
        }
        t.state = "triggered"; t.triggeredTurn = turn; t.hidden = false;
        String consequence = t.triggerText();
        lastSensesReport = "Trap noise: " + consequence;
        if (t.noiseRadius > 0) world.noiseSources.add(new ZoneNoiseSourceRecord(t.id+"-noise", t.label + " discharge", "trap", x, y, t.noiseRadius, Math.max(20,t.severity*12), true, false, 0, 1, t.id));
        logEvent(consequence);
        if (t.damage > 0) applyPlayerBodyDamage(t.damage, randomBodyHitLocation(), "triggered " + t.label, t.effect);
    }

    void drawTrapWarningOverlays(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || world.trapRecords == null || world.trapRecords.isEmpty()) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(9, Math.min(14, cellH/2))));
        for (TrapRecord t : world.trapRecords) {
            if (t == null || t.x < camX || t.y < camY || t.x >= camX + cols || t.y >= camY + rows) continue;
            boolean visibleTrap = !t.hidden || "revealed".equals(t.state) || "triggered".equals(t.state) || "disarmed".equals(t.state);
            if (!visibleTrap && !(isVisible(t.x,t.y) && stat("Intellect",5)*5 >= t.detectionDifficulty)) continue;
            int px = ox + (t.x - camX) * cellW, yy = (tileIconMode()? oy + (t.y-camY)*cellH : oy + (t.y-camY)*cellH - cellH + 3);
            float alpha = "triggered".equals(t.state) ? 0.35f : ("disarmed".equals(t.state) ? 0.25f : 0.70f);
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, alpha));
            gg.setColor(new Color(245, 165, 35));
            gg.drawRect(px+3, yy+3, Math.max(2,cellW-7), Math.max(2,cellH-7));
            gg.drawString("T", px + Math.max(3,cellW/3), yy + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    EnvironmentalHazardRecord hazardAt(int x, int y) {
        if (world == null || world.hazardWarnings == null) return null;
        for (EnvironmentalHazardRecord h : world.hazardWarnings) if (h != null && h.x == x && h.y == y) return h;
        return null;
    }

    void drawEnvironmentalHazardOverlays(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || world.hazardWarnings == null || world.hazardWarnings.isEmpty()) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        int tri = Math.max(8, Math.min(16, Math.min(cellW, cellH) / 2));
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(9, Math.min(15, tri))));
        for (EnvironmentalHazardRecord h : world.hazardWarnings) {
            if (h == null || h.x < camX || h.y < camY || h.x >= camX + cols || h.y >= camY + rows) continue;
            boolean vis = isVisible(h.x, h.y), rem = isRemembered(h.x, h.y);
            if (!vis && !rem) continue;
            int px = ox + (h.x - camX) * cellW, py = oy + (h.y - camY) * cellH;
            float alpha = vis ? 0.82f : 0.34f;
            int frame = Math.floorMod(turn + h.phase, 3);
            int yy = tileIconMode() ? py : py - cellH + 3;
            Color c = h.color();
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.min(0.42f, alpha * (0.24f + 0.08f * frame))));
            gg.setColor(c);
            if (h.family.contains("wire") || h.family.contains("electric")) {
                int y0 = yy + Math.max(3, cellH/3);
                gg.drawLine(px + 2, y0, px + cellW/3, yy + cellH - 3);
                gg.drawLine(px + cellW/3, yy + cellH - 3, px + (cellW*2)/3, yy + 4);
                gg.drawLine(px + (cellW*2)/3, yy + 4, px + cellW - 3, yy + Math.max(4, cellH/2));
            } else if (h.family.contains("sludge") || h.family.contains("runoff")) {
                gg.fillOval(px + Math.max(1, frame), yy + cellH/3, Math.max(6, cellW - 4), Math.max(4, cellH/3));
                gg.drawArc(px + 2, yy + 2, Math.max(6, cellW - 5), Math.max(6, cellH - 5), frame * 40, 180);
            } else {
                gg.drawArc(px + 2 + frame, yy + 3, Math.max(6, cellW - 5), Math.max(6, cellH/2), 20, 220);
                gg.drawArc(px + 4, yy + Math.max(4, cellH/3), Math.max(5, cellW - 8), Math.max(6, cellH/2), 210, 220);
                gg.drawString("~", px + Math.max(2, cellW/3), yy + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
            }
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, alpha));
            gg.setColor(new Color(220, 35, 28));
            gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(Math.max(1.0f, Math.min(2.0f, cellW / 18.0f))));
            gg.drawRect(px + 1, yy + 1, Math.max(1, cellW - 3), Math.max(1, cellH - 3));
            int[] xs = {px + cellW - tri - 1, px + cellW - 1, px + cellW - tri/2 - 1};
            int[] ys = {yy + 1, yy + 1, yy + tri + 1};
            gg.fillPolygon(xs, ys, 3);
            gg.setColor(Color.BLACK);
            gg.drawString("!", px + cellW - tri + Math.max(1, tri/4), yy + Math.max(10, tri));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void drawPortableLightObjects(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (portableLights.isEmpty()) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, Math.min(18, cellH/2))));
        for (PortableLightInstance l : portableLights) {
            if (l == null || l.expiresTurn <= turn || !sameWorldLocation(l.worldKey)) continue;
            if (l.x < camX || l.y < camY || l.x >= camX+cols || l.y >= camY+rows) continue;
            if (!isVisible(l.x,l.y) && !isRemembered(l.x,l.y)) continue;
            int px=ox+(l.x-camX)*cellW, py=oy+(l.y-camY)*cellH;
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.62f));
            gg.setColor(new Color(250, 230, 120));
            gg.drawOval(px+Math.max(1,cellW/5), py+Math.max(1,cellH/5), Math.max(4,cellW*3/5), Math.max(4,cellH*3/5));
            gg.drawString("*", px+Math.max(3,cellW/3), py+Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void drawZoneLightFixtureObjects(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || world.lightSources == null || world.lightSources.isEmpty()) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(9, Math.min(16, cellH/2))));
        for (ZoneLightSourceRecord l : world.lightSources) {
            if (l == null || l.x < camX || l.y < camY || l.x >= camX+cols || l.y >= camY+rows) continue;
            if (!isVisible(l.x,l.y) && !isRemembered(l.x,l.y)) continue;
            int px=ox+(l.x-camX)*cellW, py=oy+(l.y-camY)*cellH;
            float alpha = l.on && l.powered ? (l.flicker && Math.floorMod(turn + l.phase, Math.max(2,l.flickerPeriod)) == 0 ? 0.25f : 0.46f) : 0.16f;
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, alpha));
            gg.setColor(l.color());
            gg.drawOval(px+Math.max(1,cellW/4), py+Math.max(1,cellH/4), Math.max(4,cellW/2), Math.max(4,cellH/2));
            gg.drawString(l.on && l.powered ? "¤" : "·", px+Math.max(2,cellW/3), py+Math.max(11,(cellH*2)/3));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void pruneCombatAnimations(long now) {
        if (!explosionAnimations.isEmpty()) explosionAnimations.removeIf(a -> now - a.startMillis > a.durationMillis);
        if (combatAnimations.isEmpty()) return;
        combatAnimations.removeIf(a -> now - a.startMillis > a.durationMillis);
    }

    void startCombatAnimation(String weapon, int x0, int y0, int x1, int y1, boolean hit) {
        if (world == null) return;
        combatAnimations.add(new CombatAnimation(weapon == null ? "bare hands" : weapon, x0, y0, x1, y1, hit, System.currentTimeMillis()));
        while (combatAnimations.size() > 12) combatAnimations.remove(0);
    }

    String projectileGlyphForWeapon(String weapon, boolean hit, int frame) {
        String w = weapon == null ? "" : weapon.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (w.contains("flamer") || w.contains("flame") || w.contains("industrial Fuelgel") || w.contains("melta") || w.contains("inferno")) return (frame % 3 == 0) ? "=0)" : (frame % 3 == 1 ? "=o)" : "==)" );
        if (w.contains("las") || w.contains("laser")) return "~~~~";
        if (w.contains("plasma")) return "~~O~";
        if (w.contains("arc") || w.contains("shock") || w.contains("lightning")) return "~Z~";
        if (w.contains("chain") || w.contains("sword") || w.contains("knife") || w.contains("blade") || w.contains("axe") || w.contains("dagger") || w.contains("claw")) {
            String[] spin = {"//", "--", "\\\\", "||"};
            return spin[Math.floorMod(frame, spin.length)];
        }
        return hit ? "--~" : "-~.";
    }

    boolean weaponIsMeleeAnimation(String weapon) {
        String w = weapon == null ? "" : weapon.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        return !ItemCatalog.isFirearmLike(weapon) || w.contains("chain") || w.contains("sword") || w.contains("knife") || w.contains("blade") || w.contains("axe") || w.contains("dagger") || w.contains("claw") || w.contains("maul") || w.contains("hammer") || w.contains("club");
    }

    void drawCombatAnimations(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (combatAnimations.isEmpty()) return;
        long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, Math.min(18, cellH/2))));
        for (CombatAnimation a : combatAnimations) {
            double t = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, (now - a.startMillis) / (double)Math.max(1, a.durationMillis)));
            int frame = (int)Math.floor(t * 8.0);
            if (weaponIsMeleeAnimation(a.weapon)) {
                int sx = a.x0 - camX, sy = a.y0 - camY;
                if (sx >= 0 && sy >= 0 && sx < cols && sy < rows) {
                    gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, (float)(0.9 - t * 0.45)));
                    gg.setColor(a.hit ? new Color(245, 230, 190) : new Color(210, 160, 120));
                    gg.drawString(projectileGlyphForWeapon(a.weapon, a.hit, frame), ox + sx*cellW + Math.max(2, cellW/4), oy + sy*cellH + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
                }
                continue;
            }
            ArrayList<Point> pts = linePoints(a.x0, a.y0, a.x1, a.y1);
            int max = Math.max(1, pts.size()-1);
            int idx = Math.max(0, Math.min(max, (int)Math.round(t * max)));
            for (int j=Math.max(0, idx-2); j<=Math.min(max, idx+1); j++) {
                Point p = pts.get(j);
                int sx = p.x - camX, sy = p.y - camY;
                if (sx < 0 || sy < 0 || sx >= cols || sy >= rows) continue;
                float alpha = (float)Math.max(0.12, 0.88 - Math.abs(idx-j)*0.22 - t*0.25);
                gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, alpha));
                String glyph = projectileGlyphForWeapon(a.weapon, a.hit, frame + j);
                if (!a.hit && j == idx && (frame % 2 == 0)) glyph = glyph.replace('~', '.');
                gg.setColor(a.hit ? new Color(255, 205, 145) : new Color(240, 120, 80));
                gg.drawString(glyph, ox + sx*cellW + Math.max(1, cellW/8), oy + sy*cellH + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
            }
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }


    void drawExplosionAnimations(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (explosionAnimations.isEmpty()) return;
        long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, Math.min(20, cellH/2))));
        for (ExplosionAnimation a : explosionAnimations) {
            double t = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, (now - a.startMillis) / (double)Math.max(1, a.durationMillis)));
            if (a.grenadeArc) {
                int x = (int)Math.round(a.x0 + (a.x1 - a.x0) * t);
                int y = (int)Math.round(a.y0 + (a.y1 - a.y0) * t);
                if (x >= camX && y >= camY && x < camX+cols && y < camY+rows) {
                    int px=ox+(x-camX)*cellW, py=oy+(y-camY)*cellH;
                    gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.85f));
                    gg.setColor((System.currentTimeMillis()/120)%2==0 ? new Color(255,30,30) : new Color(255,190,70));
                    gg.drawString("*", px + Math.max(3,cellW/3), py + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
                }
            } else {
                int ring = Math.max(0, Math.min(a.radius, (int)Math.ceil(t * (a.radius+1))));
                for (int x=a.x1-ring; x<=a.x1+ring; x++) for (int y=a.y1-ring; y<=a.y1+ring; y++) {
                    int d = Math.max(Math.abs(x-a.x1), Math.abs(y-a.y1));
                    if (d != ring || x < camX || y < camY || x >= camX+cols || y >= camY+rows) continue;
                    int px=ox+(x-camX)*cellW, py=oy+(y-camY)*cellH;
                    gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, (float)Math.max(0.15, 0.9 - t*0.55)));
                    gg.setColor(new Color(255, 115, 40));
                    gg.drawString("O", px + Math.max(3,cellW/3), py + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
                }
            }
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void drawCombatTargetOverlay(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || !(screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.COMBAT) || !combatCursorActive) return;
        if (combatX < 0 || combatY < 0 || combatX >= world.w || combatY >= world.h) return;
        TargetingSolution ts = targetingSolutionAt(combatX, combatY);
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        Stroke old = gg.getStroke();
        gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(Math.max(1.0f, cellW/12.0f), BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 1.0f, new float[]{7.0f, 5.0f}, 0.0f));
        gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.82f));
        gg.setColor(new Color(185, 25, 30));
        int px = ox + (playerX - camX) * cellW + cellW/2;
        int py = oy + (playerY - camY) * cellH + cellH/2;
        int tx = ox + (combatX - camX) * cellW + cellW/2;
        int ty = oy + (combatY - camY) * cellH + cellH/2;
        gg.drawLine(px, py, tx, ty);
        gg.setStroke(old);
        if (combatX >= camX && combatY >= camY && combatX < camX + cols && combatY < camY + rows) {
            int sx = combatX - camX, sy = combatY - camY;
            int rx = ox + sx * cellW, ry = oy + sy * cellH;
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.92f));
            gg.setColor(new Color(255, 35, 40));
            gg.drawRect(rx - 2, ry - 2, cellW + 4, cellH + 4);
            gg.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry - 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + Math.max(2, cellH/4));
            gg.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH + 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH - Math.max(2, cellH/4));
            gg.drawLine(rx - 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
            gg.drawLine(rx + cellW + 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + cellW - Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
            gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, Math.min(16, cellH/2))));
            gg.setColor(ts.hitPercent <= 0 ? new Color(230,90,80) : new Color(255,210,170));
            gg.drawString(ts.hitPercent + "%", rx + Math.max(1, cellW/5), ry - 4);
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    Point screenPointToWorldTile(int sx, int sy) {
        if (world == null) return null;
        Rectangle map = inputMapRect();
        FontMetrics fm = getFontMetrics(asciiFont);
        int cellW = tileIconMode()
                ? scaled(zoomedMapPixels(options.mapTilePixelSize()))
                : Math.max(8, scaled(zoomedMapPixels(Math.max(10, fm.charWidth('W')))));
        int cellH = tileIconMode()
                ? scaled(zoomedMapPixels(options.mapTilePixelSize()))
                : Math.max(10, scaled(zoomedMapPixels(Math.max(14, fm.getHeight()))));
        MapViewportTransformAuthority.Viewport viewport = MapViewportTransformAuthority.compute(
                map, world.w, world.h, playerX, playerY, cellW, cellH,
                10, tileIconMode() ? 10 : 10 + fm.getAscent());
        Point out = viewport.pointToTile(sx, sy);
        if (out == null) return null;
        if (!world.inBounds(out.x, out.y)) return null;
        return out;
    }

    void clearMouseMovementPreview(String reason) {
        if (mouseMovePreviewActive) DebugLog.audit("MOUSE_MOVE_PREVIEW_CLEAR", reason + " target=" + mouseMoveTargetX + "," + mouseMoveTargetY);
        manualMovementPlanActive = false;
        mouseMovePreviewActive = false; mouseMovePreviewValid = false; mouseMoveTargetX = mouseMoveTargetY = -1; mouseMovePreviewPath.clear(); mouseMovePreviewStatus = "No mouse movement preview.";
    }

    void beginManualMovementPlan() {
        if (world == null || screen != Screen.GAME) return;
        manualMovementPlanActive = true;
        Point approach = selectedInteractionApproachTile();
        if (approach != null) {
            updateMouseMovementPreviewTo(approach.x, approach.y);
            manualMovementPlanActive = true;
            logEvent("Movement target planning: approaching " + interactionTargetLabel(lookX, lookY) + " from " + approach.x + "," + approach.y + ". Confirm with Enter/E/Space, cancel with Escape.");
            repaint();
            return;
        }
        int tx = playerX;
        int ty = playerY;
        int dx = lastMoveDx == 0 && lastMoveDy == 0 ? 1 : lastMoveDx;
        int dy = lastMoveDx == 0 && lastMoveDy == 0 ? 0 : lastMoveDy;
        for (int i = 0; i < Math.max(1, movementModeRange()); i++) {
            int nx = playerX + dx * (i + 1);
            int ny = playerY + dy * (i + 1);
            if (world.inBounds(nx, ny) && world.walkable(nx, ny)) { tx = nx; ty = ny; }
            else break;
        }
        if (tx == playerX && ty == playerY) {
            int[][] dirs = {{1,0},{0,1},{-1,0},{0,-1}};
            for (int[] d : dirs) {
                int nx = playerX + d[0], ny = playerY + d[1];
                if (world.inBounds(nx, ny) && world.walkable(nx, ny)) { tx = nx; ty = ny; break; }
            }
        }
        updateMouseMovementPreviewTo(tx, ty);
        manualMovementPlanActive = true;
        logEvent("Movement target planning: nudge with arrows or WASD, confirm with Enter/E/Space, cancel with Escape.");
        repaint();
    }

    void nudgeManualMovementPlan(int dx, int dy) {
        if (world == null || dx == 0 && dy == 0) return;
        if (!manualMovementPlanActive) beginManualMovementPlan();
        int baseX = mouseMoveTargetX >= 0 ? mouseMoveTargetX : playerX;
        int baseY = mouseMoveTargetY >= 0 ? mouseMoveTargetY : playerY;
        int tx = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.w - 1, baseX + dx));
        int ty = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.h - 1, baseY + dy));
        updateMouseMovementPreviewTo(tx, ty);
        manualMovementPlanActive = true;
        repaint();
    }

    void confirmManualMovementPlan() {
        if (!manualMovementPlanActive) return;
        executeMouseMovementPreview();
    }

    void cancelManualMovementPlan(String reason) {
        clearMouseMovementPreview(reason);
        logEvent("Movement target planning cancelled.");
        repaint();
    }

    void updateMouseMovementPreviewTo(int tx, int ty) {
        mouseMovePreviewActive = true; mouseMoveTargetX = tx; mouseMoveTargetY = ty; mouseMovePreviewLastMillis = System.currentTimeMillis(); mouseMovePreviewPath.clear();
        String directBlock = directMovementTargetBlockReason(tx, ty);
        if (directBlock != null) {
            mouseMovePreviewValid = false;
            mouseMovePreviewStatus = directBlock;
            return;
        }
        ArrayList<Point> path = findPreviewPath(playerX, playerY, tx, ty, 80);
        mouseMovePreviewPath.addAll(path);
        mouseMovePreviewValid = !path.isEmpty();
        int steps = Math.max(0, path.size());
        int range = Math.max(1, movementModeRange());
        int chunks = steps == 0 ? 0 : (int)Math.ceil(steps / (double)range);
        if (!mouseMovePreviewValid) {
            mouseMovePreviewStatus = "Cannot reach from here.";
            return;
        }
        String hazard = movementPathHazardWarning(path);
        String approach = interactionApproachStatusFor(tx, ty);
        mouseMovePreviewStatus = "Movement target ready"
                + (hazard.isEmpty() ? "" : "; " + hazard)
                + (approach.isEmpty() ? "" : "; " + approach)
                + " | steps " + steps + " | " + chunks + " action(s) at " + movementModeLabel();
    }

    Point selectedInteractionApproachTile() {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(lookX, lookY)) return null;
        if (!hasSelectedInteractionTarget(lookX, lookY)) return null;
        if (Math.abs(lookX - playerX) <= 1 && Math.abs(lookY - playerY) <= 1) return null;
        ArrayList<Point> candidates = new ArrayList<>();
        for (int dy=-1; dy<=1; dy++) for (int dx=-1; dx<=1; dx++) {
            if (dx == 0 && dy == 0) continue;
            int x = lookX + dx, y = lookY + dy;
            if (!world.inBounds(x, y) || !world.walkable(x, y)) continue;
            if (world.npcAt(x, y) != null) continue;
            if (x == playerX && y == playerY) continue;
            candidates.add(new Point(x, y));
        }
        Point best = null;
        int bestScore = Integer.MAX_VALUE;
        for (Point p : candidates) {
            ArrayList<Point> path = findPreviewPath(playerX, playerY, p.x, p.y, 80);
            if (path.isEmpty()) continue;
            int score = path.size() * 10 + Math.abs(p.x - playerX) + Math.abs(p.y - playerY);
            if (best == null || score < bestScore) { best = p; bestScore = score; }
        }
        return best;
    }

    boolean hasSelectedInteractionTarget(int tx, int ty) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(tx, ty)) return false;
        if (world.npcAt(tx, ty) != null) return true;
        if (baseObjectAt(tx, ty) != null) return true;
        if (world.mapObjectAt(tx, ty) != null) return true;
        char ch = world.tiles[tx][ty];
        return isDoorTile(ch) || isIntermapTransitTile(ch) || isVendingMachine(ch) || isShrine(ch) || isEmergencyMachine(ch) || ch == 'Q' || ch == 'T';
    }

    String interactionTargetLabel(int tx, int ty) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(tx, ty)) return "the selected target";
        NpcEntity npc = world.npcAt(tx, ty);
        if (npc != null) return npc.name;
        BaseObject obj = baseObjectAt(tx, ty);
        if (obj != null) return obj.name;
        MapObjectState mos = world.mapObjectAt(tx, ty);
        if (mos != null) return mos.label == null || mos.label.isBlank() ? "fixture" : mos.label;
        return describeTile(world.tiles[tx][ty]);
    }

    String interactionApproachStatusFor(int tx, int ty) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(tx, ty) || !world.inBounds(lookX, lookY)) return "";
        if (!hasSelectedInteractionTarget(lookX, lookY)) return "";
        if (Math.abs(tx - lookX) <= 1 && Math.abs(ty - lookY) <= 1 && !(tx == lookX && ty == lookY)) return "approach tile for " + interactionTargetLabel(lookX, lookY);
        return "";
    }

    String directMovementTargetBlockReason(int tx, int ty) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(tx, ty)) return "Movement target is outside the known map.";
        if (tx == playerX && ty == playerY) return "Movement target is your current position.";
        NpcEntity npc = world.npcAt(tx, ty);
        if (npc != null) return "Destination occupied.";
        if (!world.walkable(tx, ty)) {
            char ch = world.tiles[tx][ty];
            if (isDoorTile(ch) || ch == 'D') return "Door is closed.";
            return "Path blocked.";
        }
        return null;
    }

    String movementPathHazardWarning(java.util.List<Point> path) {
        if (path == null || path.isEmpty()) return "";
        for (Point p : path) {
            EnvironmentalHazardRecord h = hazardAt(p.x, p.y);
            if (h != null) return "hazard ahead";
        }
        return "";
    }

    ArrayList<Point> findPreviewPath(int sx, int sy, int tx, int ty, int maxNodes) {
        ArrayList<Point> empty = new ArrayList<>();
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(sx, sy) || !world.inBounds(tx, ty) || !world.walkable(tx, ty)) return empty;
        int max = Math.max(4, maxNodes);
        ArrayDeque<Point> q = new ArrayDeque<>();
        HashMap<String, Point> prev = new HashMap<>();
        Point start = new Point(sx, sy); q.add(start); prev.put(sx+","+sy, null);
        int[][] dirs = {{1,0},{-1,0},{0,1},{0,-1}}; int seen = 0;
        while(!q.isEmpty() && seen++ < max*max) {
            Point p = q.removeFirst();
            if (p.x == tx && p.y == ty) break;
            Arrays.sort(dirs, Comparator.comparingInt(d -> Math.abs((p.x + d[0]) - tx) + Math.abs((p.y + d[1]) - ty)));
            for (int[] d: dirs) {
                int nx = p.x + d[0], ny = p.y + d[1]; String key = nx + "," + ny;
                if (!world.inBounds(nx, ny) || prev.containsKey(key) || !world.walkable(nx, ny)) continue;
                if (world.npcAt(nx, ny) != null && !(nx == tx && ny == ty)) continue;
                prev.put(key, p); q.addLast(new Point(nx, ny));
            }
        }
        String target = tx + "," + ty;
        if (!prev.containsKey(target)) return empty;
        ArrayList<Point> rev = new ArrayList<>();
        Point cur = new Point(tx, ty);
        while(cur != null && !(cur.x == sx && cur.y == sy)) { rev.add(cur); cur = prev.get(cur.x + "," + cur.y); }
        Collections.reverse(rev);
        return rev;
    }

    void executeMouseMovementPreview() {
        if (!mouseMovePreviewActive || !mouseMovePreviewValid || mouseMovePreviewPath.isEmpty()) { clearMouseMovementPreview("execute-invalid"); repaint(); return; }
        int range = Math.max(1, movementModeRange());
        int steps = Math.min(range, mouseMovePreviewPath.size());
        Point dest = mouseMovePreviewPath.get(steps - 1);
        int dx = Integer.compare(dest.x, playerX);
        int dy = Integer.compare(dest.y, playerY);
        int fromX = playerX, fromY = playerY;
        playerX = dest.x; playerY = dest.y;
        beginPlayerTileSlide(fromX, fromY, playerX, playerY);
        lastMoveDx = dx; lastMoveDy = dy;
        activeMotionStateIndex = movementModeIndex;
        updateSensoryModel("mouse movement preview execution");
        checkTrapAfterPlayerMove(playerX, playerY);
        advanceTurn("moves by mouse path preview.");
        clearMouseMovementPreview("executed");
        repaint();
    }

    void drawMouseMovementPreview(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (!mouseMovePreviewActive) return;
        if (!manualMovementPlanActive && System.currentTimeMillis() - mouseMovePreviewLastMillis > 4000L) { clearMouseMovementPreview("timeout"); return; }
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        int range = Math.max(1, movementModeRange());
        for (int i=0; i<mouseMovePreviewPath.size(); i++) {
            Point p = mouseMovePreviewPath.get(i);
            if (p.x < camX || p.y < camY || p.x >= camX + cols || p.y >= camY + rows) continue;
            int px = ox + (p.x - camX) * cellW, py = oy + (p.y - camY) * cellH;
            boolean inAction = i < range;
            gg.setColor(inAction ? new Color(120, 230, 150, 170) : new Color(235, 70, 55, 170));
            gg.drawRoundRect(px+3, py+3, Math.max(2, cellW-7), Math.max(2, cellH-7), 6, 6);
            if (!inAction) { gg.drawLine(px+4, py+4, px+cellW-5, py+cellH-5); gg.drawLine(px+cellW-5, py+4, px+4, py+cellH-5); }
        }
        if (mouseMoveTargetX >= camX && mouseMoveTargetY >= camY && mouseMoveTargetX < camX + cols && mouseMoveTargetY < camY + rows) {
            int px = ox + (mouseMoveTargetX - camX) * cellW, py = oy + (mouseMoveTargetY - camY) * cellH;
            gg.setColor(mouseMovePreviewValid ? new Color(245, 220, 110) : new Color(255, 60, 45));
            gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(2f)); gg.drawRect(px, py, Math.max(1,cellW-1), Math.max(1,cellH-1));
        }
        gg.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-3f)));
        FontMetrics fm = gg.getFontMetrics();
        int bw = Math.min(380, Math.max(160, fm.stringWidth(mouseMovePreviewStatus) + 18));
        int anchorX = mouseX >= 0 ? mouseX : getWidth() / 2;
        int anchorY = mouseY >= 0 ? mouseY : Math.max(42, getHeight() / 2);
        int bx = Math.max(8, Math.min(getWidth() - bw - 8, anchorX + 18));
        int by = Math.max(8, Math.min(getHeight() - 42, anchorY + 18));
        gg.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,220)); gg.fillRoundRect(bx, by, bw, 28, 8, 8);
        gg.setColor(mouseMovePreviewValid ? new Color(120,230,150) : new Color(250,90,70)); gg.drawRoundRect(bx, by, bw, 28, 8, 8);
        drawUiTextLine(gg, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(mouseMovePreviewStatus, fm, bw-16), bx+9, by+19);
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void drawMovementGhostPath(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || screen != Screen.GAME || buildPlacementActive || movementModeRange() <= 1 || !movementGhostArmed) return;
        updateMoveGhostTarget(armedMoveDx == 0 && armedMoveDy == 0 ? lastMoveDx : armedMoveDx, armedMoveDy == 0 && armedMoveDx == 0 ? lastMoveDy : armedMoveDy);
        if (moveGhostX < 0 || moveGhostY < 0 || (moveGhostX == playerX && moveGhostY == playerY)) return;
        int dx = Integer.compare(moveGhostX, playerX);
        int dy = Integer.compare(moveGhostY, playerY);
        if (Math.abs(moveGhostX - playerX) > 0) dy = 0;
        else dx = 0;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.33f));
        gg.setColor(new Color(180, 220, 255));
        int tx = playerX, ty = playerY;
        for (int i=0; i<movementModeRange(); i++) {
            tx += dx; ty += dy;
            if (tx < 0 || ty < 0 || world == null || !world.inBounds(tx, ty) || !world.walkable(tx, ty)) break;
            if (tx >= camX && ty >= camY && tx < camX + cols && ty < camY + rows) {
                int px = ox + (tx - camX) * cellW;
                int py = oy + (ty - camY) * cellH;
                gg.drawRect(px + Math.max(1, cellW/5), py + Math.max(1, cellH/5), Math.max(3, (cellW*3)/5), Math.max(3, (cellH*3)/5));
            }
            if (tx == moveGhostX && ty == moveGhostY) break;
        }
        if (moveGhostX >= camX && moveGhostY >= camY && moveGhostX < camX + cols && moveGhostY < camY + rows) {
            int px = ox + (moveGhostX - camX) * cellW;
            int py = oy + (moveGhostY - camY) * cellH;
            BufferedImage face = activePortraitImage();
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.42f));
            if (tileIconMode() && face != null) drawCachedMapImage(gg, face, px, py, cellW, cellH);
            else { gg.setColor(new Color(180, 220, 255)); gg.drawString("@", px + Math.max(2,cellW/3), py + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3)); }
            gg.setColor(new Color(180, 220, 255));
            gg.drawRect(px+1, py+1, Math.max(3, cellW-3), Math.max(3, cellH-3));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    NpcEntity selectedLookNpc() {
        if (world == null || !lookCursorActive || !world.inBounds(lookX, lookY) || !isVisible(lookX, lookY)) return null;
        return world.npcAt(lookX, lookY);
    }

    IntentReadResult intentReadFor(NpcEntity npc) {
        IntentReadResult r = new IntentReadResult();
        if (npc == null || active == null) { r.available = false; r.summary = "No readable entity selected."; return r; }
        r.available = true;
        r.intent = npcIntentLabel(npc);
        r.visionRange = npcVisionRange(npc);
        r.hearingRange = npcHearingRange(npc);
        int playerScore = stat("Intellect", 5) * 3 + stat("Vision", 5) * 2 + stat("Hearing", 5) + stat("Nerve", 5);
        playerScore -= detectionLightPenalty(playerX, playerY, npc.x, npc.y) / 2;
        if (activeMotionStateIndex == MOTION_STATIONARY) playerScore += 10;
        else if (activeMotionStateIndex == MOTION_WALK) playerScore += 5;
        else if (activeMotionStateIndex == MOTION_SNEAK) playerScore += 2;
        else if (activeMotionStateIndex == MOTION_RUN) playerScore -= 8;
        else if (activeMotionStateIndex == MOTION_SPRINT) playerScore -= 14;
        int targetScore = 18 + Math.max(0, npc.idleBias) * 3 + factionIntentMasking(npc.faction);
        if ("Hostile".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) targetScore += 5;
        int deterministic = Math.floorMod(Objects.hash(npc.id, turn / 2, playerX, playerY, active == null ? "" : active.name), 21) - 10;
        r.margin = playerScore + deterministic - targetScore;
        r.degree = r.margin >= 22 ? 4 : (r.margin >= 12 ? 3 : (r.margin >= 3 ? 2 : (r.margin >= -6 ? 1 : 0)));
        Point step = npcProjectedStep(npc);
        r.projectedX = step == null ? npc.x : step.x;
        r.projectedY = step == null ? npc.y : step.y;
        r.facingDx = npcFacingDx(npc);
        r.facingDy = npcFacingDy(npc);
        int dist = Math.abs(npc.x - playerX) + Math.abs(npc.y - playerY);
        r.attackLine = isHostileNpc(npc) && dist <= Math.max(1, r.visionRange) && hasLineOfSight(npc.x, npc.y, playerX, playerY);
        if (r.degree <= 0) r.summary = "Intent read failed: you cannot get past posture, faction tells, and underhive noise.";
        else if (r.degree == 1) r.summary = "Intent read partial: " + npc.name + " seems " + r.intent.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT) + ".";
        else if (r.degree == 2) r.summary = "Intent read: " + npc.name + " appears " + r.intent.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT) + "; likely next step " + r.projectedX + "," + r.projectedY + ".";
        else if (r.degree == 3) r.summary = "Intent read strong: " + r.intent + "; motion " + npc.activeMotionLabel() + "; vision/hearing estimates available; likely step " + r.projectedX + "," + r.projectedY + ".";
        else r.summary = "Intent read exacting: " + r.intent + "; motion " + npc.activeMotionLabel() + "; vision cone, hearing radius, projected movement, obstruction, and attack line are revealed.";
        return r;
    }

    int factionIntentMasking(Faction f) {
        if (f == null) return 0;
        switch(f) {
            case CIVIC_WARDENS: case IMPERIAL_GUARD: case SORORITAS: return 8;
            case NOBLE: case NOBLE_HOUSE_VARN: case NOBLE_HOUSE_KASTOR: case NOBLE_HOUSE_MORVAIN: case NOBLE_HOUSE_CYRA: case NOBLE_HOUSE_DRAKE: case NOBLE_HOUSE_TOLL: case NOBLE_HOUSE_OSSUARY: return 7;
            case CULTIST: case HERETIC: return 10;
            case ROGUE_MACHINE: return 12;
            case MUTANT: return 3;
            default: return 4;
        }
    }

    String npcIntentLabel(NpcEntity npc) {
        if (npc == null) return "Unknown";
        if ("Hostile".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) {
            int d = Math.abs(npc.x - playerX) + Math.abs(npc.y - playerY);
            return d <= 1 ? "Attacking the player" : "Closing to attack";
        }
        if ("Guard".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Holding guard position";
        if ("Patrol".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Patrolling";
        if ("Search Needs".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Seeking supplies or rest";
        if ("Trade".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Maintaining trade post";
        if ("Prayer".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state) || "Pilgrim Service".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Religious service";
        if ("Jostled".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Recovering from crowd pressure";
        if ("Sleep".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Sleeping";
        if ("Inspect".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return "Inspecting machinery or doctrine";
        return "Idling or wandering";
    }

    int npcVisionRange(NpcEntity npc) {
        if (npc == null) return 5;
        int base = 5 + Math.max(0, npc.idleBias);
        if (npc.faction == Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS || npc.faction == Faction.IMPERIAL_GUARD || npc.faction == Faction.SORORITAS) base += 3;
        if (npc.faction == Faction.MUTANT) base -= 1;
        if (npc.faction == Faction.ROGUE_MACHINE) base += 4;
        if ("Guard".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state) || "Patrol".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) base += 2;
        if ("Sleep".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) base = 1;
        base += npcMotionVisionModifier(npc);
        return Math.max(1, Math.min(14, base));
    }

    int npcHearingRange(NpcEntity npc) {
        if (npc == null) return 6;
        int base = 6 + Math.max(0, npc.idleBias);
        if (npc.faction == Faction.MUTANT) base += 3;
        if (npc.faction == Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS || npc.faction == Faction.IMPERIAL_GUARD || npc.faction == Faction.SORORITAS) base += 2;
        if (npc.faction == Faction.ROGUE_MACHINE) base += 4;
        if ("Sleep".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) base -= 3;
        base += npcMotionHearingModifier(npc);
        return Math.max(2, Math.min(18, base));
    }

    int npcFacingDx(NpcEntity npc) {
        if (npc == null) return 1;
        if ("Hostile".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return Integer.compare(playerX, npc.x);
        if (npc.needTarget != null) return Integer.compare(npc.needTarget.x, npc.x);
        if (Math.abs(npc.homeX - npc.x) > Math.abs(npc.homeY - npc.y)) return Integer.compare(npc.homeX, npc.x);
        int seed = Math.floorMod(Objects.hash(npc.id, turn / 6), 4);
        return seed == 0 ? 1 : (seed == 1 ? -1 : 0);
    }

    int npcFacingDy(NpcEntity npc) {
        if (npc == null) return 0;
        if ("Hostile".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) return Integer.compare(playerY, npc.y);
        if (npc.needTarget != null) return Integer.compare(npc.needTarget.y, npc.y);
        if (Math.abs(npc.homeY - npc.y) >= Math.abs(npc.homeX - npc.x) && npc.homeY != npc.y) return Integer.compare(npc.homeY, npc.y);
        int seed = Math.floorMod(Objects.hash(npc.id, turn / 6), 4);
        return seed == 2 ? 1 : (seed == 3 ? -1 : 0);
    }

    Point npcProjectedStep(NpcEntity npc) {
        if (world == null || npc == null) return null;
        int tx = npc.x, ty = npc.y;
        if ("Hostile".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) { tx = playerX; ty = playerY; }
        else if (npc.needTarget != null) { tx = npc.needTarget.x; ty = npc.needTarget.y; }
        else if ("Guard".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state) && Math.abs(npc.x-npc.homeX)+Math.abs(npc.y-npc.homeY) > 2) { tx = npc.homeX; ty = npc.homeY; }
        else if ("Patrol".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state) || "Wander".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state) || "Idle".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state) || "Inspect".equalsIgnoreCase(npc.state)) {
            int[][] dirs={{1,0},{-1,0},{0,1},{0,-1},{0,0}};
            int[] d = dirs[Math.abs((npc.id.hashCode()+Math.max(1,turn)*31)) % dirs.length];
            int wx = npc.x + d[0], wy = npc.y + d[1];
            if (world.walkable(wx, wy) && world.npcAt(wx, wy) == null && !(wx == playerX && wy == playerY)) return new Point(wx, wy);
            return new Point(npc.x, npc.y);
        } else return new Point(npc.x, npc.y);
        int dx = Integer.compare(tx, npc.x), dy = Integer.compare(ty, npc.y);
        Point p1 = Math.abs(tx-npc.x) > Math.abs(ty-npc.y) ? new Point(npc.x + dx, npc.y) : new Point(npc.x, npc.y + dy);
        if (world.walkable(p1.x, p1.y) && !(p1.x == playerX && p1.y == playerY) && world.npcAt(p1.x, p1.y) == null) return p1;
        Point p2 = Math.abs(tx-npc.x) > Math.abs(ty-npc.y) ? new Point(npc.x, npc.y + dy) : new Point(npc.x + dx, npc.y);
        if (world.walkable(p2.x, p2.y) && !(p2.x == playerX && p2.y == playerY) && world.npcAt(p2.x, p2.y) == null) return p2;
        return new Point(npc.x, npc.y);
    }

    boolean npcVisionContains(NpcEntity npc, int x, int y, IntentReadResult read) {
        if (npc == null || read == null) return false;
        if (x == npc.x && y == npc.y) return true;
        int dx = x - npc.x, dy = y - npc.y;
        int fx = read.facingDx, fy = read.facingDy;
        if (fx == 0 && fy == 0) { fx = 1; fy = 0; }
        double forward = dx * fx + dy * fy;
        double side = Math.abs(dx * fy - dy * fx);
        double vr = Math.max(1, read.visionRange);
        if (forward >= 0) return (forward*forward)/((vr+1)*(vr+1)) + (side*side)/Math.max(1.0, (vr*0.65)*(vr*0.65)) <= 1.0;
        double rear = -forward;
        return (rear*rear)/Math.max(1.0, (vr*0.35)*(vr*0.35)) + (side*side)/Math.max(1.0, (vr*0.45)*(vr*0.45)) <= 1.0;
    }

    void drawLookIntentOverlay(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        NpcEntity npc = selectedLookNpc();
        if (npc == null) return;
        IntentReadResult read = intentReadFor(npc);
        if (!read.available || read.degree < 2) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        int cx = ox + (npc.x - camX) * cellW + cellW/2;
        int cy = oy + (npc.y - camY) * cellH + cellH/2;
        if (read.degree >= 3) {
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.16f));
            gg.setColor(new Color(245, 205, 90));
            int span = Math.max(read.visionRange, read.hearingRange) + 1;
            for (int x=Math.max(0, npc.x-span); x<=Math.min(world.w-1, npc.x+span); x++) for (int y=Math.max(0, npc.y-span); y<=Math.min(world.h-1, npc.y+span); y++) {
                if (x < camX || y < camY || x >= camX + cols || y >= camY + rows) continue;
                if (npcVisionContains(npc, x, y, read) && hasLineOfSight(npc.x, npc.y, x, y)) {
                    gg.fillRect(ox + (x-camX)*cellW + 2, oy + (y-camY)*cellH + 2, Math.max(2, cellW-4), Math.max(2, cellH-4));
                }
            }
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.55f));
            gg.setColor(new Color(115, 190, 230));
            int rx = read.hearingRange * cellW;
            int ry = read.hearingRange * cellH;
            gg.drawOval(cx-rx, cy-ry, rx*2, ry*2);
        }
        if (read.degree >= 2 && (read.projectedX != npc.x || read.projectedY != npc.y)) {
            int tx = ox + (read.projectedX - camX) * cellW + cellW/2;
            int ty = oy + (read.projectedY - camY) * cellH + cellH/2;
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.75f));
            gg.setColor(new Color(200, 230, 180));
            gg.drawLine(cx, cy, tx, ty);
            gg.drawRect(tx-cellW/4, ty-cellH/4, Math.max(3, cellW/2), Math.max(3, cellH/2));
        }
        if (read.attackLine) {
            Stroke old = gg.getStroke();
            gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(Math.max(1.0f, cellW/14.0f), BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 1.0f, new float[]{6.0f, 5.0f}, 0.0f));
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.82f));
            gg.setColor(new Color(245, 85, 70));
            int px = ox + (playerX - camX) * cellW + cellW/2;
            int py = oy + (playerY - camY) * cellH + cellH/2;
            gg.drawLine(cx, cy, px, py);
            gg.setStroke(old);
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }

    boolean corridorArtRotatesEastWest(char ch, int worldX, int worldY) {
        // 0.9.10fn/ji: road art resolves through compiled road shape keys, while
        // corridor art now follows the compiled same-family corridor orientation.
        // Maintenance/exterior/sewer corridor runs therefore orient toward the next
        // nearest tile of the same corridor type instead of borrowing unrelated halls.
        if (ch == ';' || ch == '_') return false;
        if (world == null || !images.corridorArtUsesNorthSouth(ch)) return false;
        CompiledTileDescriptor d = tileDescriptorForRenderedGlyph(ch, worldX, worldY);
        if (d != null && "corridor".equals(d.baseLayer)) return "east_west".equals(d.shape);
        boolean ew = corridorLikeForArt(worldX-1, worldY) || corridorLikeForArt(worldX+1, worldY);
        boolean ns = corridorLikeForArt(worldX, worldY-1) || corridorLikeForArt(worldX, worldY+1);
        return ew && !ns;
    }

    boolean corridorLikeForArt(int x, int y) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(x,y)) return false;
        char t = world.tiles[x][y];
        return world.roomIds[x][y] < 0 && (world.isCorridorGlyph(t) || t == 'D' || t == '/' || t == '|');
    }

    BufferedImage tileImageForRenderedGlyph(char ch) { return semanticTileImageForRenderedGlyph(ch, -1, -1); }

    CompiledTileDescriptor tileDescriptorForRenderedGlyph(char ch, int worldX, int worldY) {
        return TileDataCompilationAuthority.resolve(world, worldX, worldY, ch);
    }

    BufferedImage semanticTileImageForRenderedGlyph(char ch, int worldX, int worldY) {
        // 0.9.10fn: the renderer no longer treats a raw ASCII glyph as the complete
        // visual identity.  Stage 9 hardens this further: once a descriptor has a
        // semantic asset ID, a missing registry image produces a typed missing tile
        // instead of silently falling through to unrelated legacy art.
        CompiledTileDescriptor d = tileDescriptorForRenderedGlyph(ch, worldX, worldY);
        if (d != null) {
            if (d.hasOverlay()) {
                BufferedImage overlay = images.getSemanticAssetImage(d.overlayAssetId);
                if (overlay != null) return overlay;
                if (d.overlayAssetId != null && !d.overlayAssetId.isBlank()) return AssetManager.missingAssetImage(assetTypeForDescriptor(d));
                overlay = images.getTile(d.overlayArtKey, ch);
                if (overlay != null) return overlay;
            }
            BufferedImage primary = images.getSemanticAssetImage(d.primaryAssetId);
            if (primary != null) return primary;
            if (d.primaryAssetId != null && !d.primaryAssetId.isBlank()) return AssetManager.missingAssetImage(assetTypeForDescriptor(d));
            primary = images.getTile(d.primaryArtKey, ch);
            if (primary != null) return primary;
            if (d.primaryArtKey != null && d.primaryArtKey.matches("road_.*_v[1-5]")) {
                String base = d.primaryArtKey.replaceAll("_v[1-5]$", "");
                primary = images.getTile(base, ch);
                if (primary != null) return primary;
            }
            if (d.underlayArtKey != null) {
                BufferedImage under = images.getSemanticAssetImage(d.underlayAssetId);
                if (under != null) return under;
                if (d.underlayAssetId != null && !d.underlayAssetId.isBlank()) return AssetManager.missingAssetImage(assetTypeForDescriptor(d));
                under = images.getTile(d.underlayArtKey, d.underlayGlyph == null ? '.' : d.underlayGlyph.charValue());
                if (under != null) return under;
            }
        }
        return images.getTile(ch);
    }

    AssetType assetTypeForDescriptor(CompiledTileDescriptor d) {
        if (d == null) return AssetType.UNKNOWN;
        String layer = (d.baseLayer == null ? "" : d.baseLayer).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        String family = (d.family == null ? "" : d.family).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (layer.contains("wall") || family.contains("wall")) return AssetType.WALL_TILE;
        if (layer.contains("road") || family.contains("road")) return AssetType.ROAD_TILE;
        if (layer.contains("sidewalk") || family.contains("sidewalk")) return AssetType.SIDEWALK_TILE;
        if (layer.contains("corridor") || family.contains("corridor") || family.contains("sewer") || family.contains("maintenance")) return AssetType.CORRIDOR_TILE;
        if (layer.contains("door") || family.contains("door") || layer.contains("fixture") || family.contains("fixture")) return AssetType.FIXTURE;
        if (layer.contains("corpse") || family.contains("corpse") || family.contains("decay")) return AssetType.CORPSE_DECAY;
        return AssetType.FLOOR_TILE;
    }

    String roadSemanticKeyForArt(int worldX, int worldY, char fallbackGlyph) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(worldX, worldY)) return fallbackGlyph == '_' ? "road_sidewalk" : "road_north_south";
        if (fallbackGlyph == '_' && !sidewalkPromotesToRoadForArt(worldX, worldY)) return "road_sidewalk";
        String shape = TileDataCompilationAuthority.roadShape(world, worldX, worldY);
        if (shape == null || shape.isBlank()) return fallbackGlyph == '_' ? "road_sidewalk" : "road_north_south";
        return "road_" + shape;
    }

    String roadVariantKeyForArt(String semantic, int worldX, int worldY) {
        if (semantic == null || worldX < 0 || worldY < 0) return semantic;
        if (semantic.startsWith("road_corner_") || semantic.startsWith("road_end_") || semantic.startsWith("tile_road_corner_") || semantic.startsWith("tile_road_end_")) return semantic;
        if (!(semantic.equals("road_north_south") || semantic.equals("road_east_west") || semantic.equals("road_intersection") || semantic.equals("road_sidewalk") ||
              semantic.equals("tile_road_north_south") || semantic.equals("tile_road_east_west") || semantic.equals("tile_road_intersection") || semantic.equals("tile_road_sidewalk"))) return semantic;
        int variant = 1 + Math.abs(Objects.hash(worldX / 3, worldY / 3, semantic)) % 5;
        return semantic + "_v" + variant;
    }

    boolean roadRunsEastWest(int worldX, int worldY) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(worldX, worldY)) return false;
        boolean west = roadLaneForArt(worldX-1, worldY);
        boolean east = roadLaneForArt(worldX+1, worldY);
        boolean north = roadLaneForArt(worldX, worldY-1);
        boolean south = roadLaneForArt(worldX, worldY+1);
        boolean ewOpposed = west && east;
        boolean nsOpposed = north && south;
        if (ewOpposed && !nsOpposed) return true;
        if (nsOpposed) return false;
        return (west || east) && !(north || south);
    }

    boolean sidewalkPromotesToRoadForArt(int worldX, int worldY) {
        return TileDataCompilationAuthority.sidewalkPromotesToRoad(world, worldX, worldY);
    }

    boolean roadLaneForArt(int x, int y) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(x,y) || world.tiles[x][y] != ';') return false;
        if (world.roomIds != null && x >= 0 && y >= 0 && x < world.roomIds.length && y < world.roomIds[x].length && world.roomIds[x][y] >= 0) return false;
        return true;
    }

    boolean sidewalkForArt(int x, int y) {
        return world != null && world.inBounds(x,y) && world.tiles[x][y] == '_';
    }

    boolean roadLikeForArt(int x, int y) {
        // 0.9.10fs: sidewalks are street-family tiles, not road-connectivity tiles.
        // Counting them as roads made lane tiles see four neighbors and render as intersections.
        return roadLaneForArt(x,y);
    }

    boolean isWallGlyphForArt(char ch) {
        return ch == '#' || ch == '%' || ch == '&' || ch == '^' || ch == '8' || ch == '0';
    }

    boolean isTerrainGlyphForArt(char ch) {
        return ch == ' ' || ch == '.' || ch == ',' || ch == '`' || ch == '+' || ch == '=' || ch == ':' || ch == '-' || ch == '~' || ch == ';' || ch == '_' ||
               isWallGlyphForArt(ch) || ch == '/' || ch == '|' || ch == 'L' || ch == 'V' || ch == 'X' || ch == 'D';
    }

    boolean isOverlayGlyphForArt(char ch) {
        return TileDataCompilationAuthority.overlayAliasForGlyph(ch) != null;
    }

    char inferredUnderlayGlyphForOverlay(char ch, int worldX, int worldY) {
        return TileDataCompilationAuthority.inferredUnderlayGlyph(world, worldX, worldY, ch);
    }

    BufferedImage underlayImageForOverlayGlyph(char ch, int worldX, int worldY) {
        CompiledTileDescriptor d = tileDescriptorForRenderedGlyph(ch, worldX, worldY);
        if (d == null || !d.hasOverlay()) return null;
        return images.getTile(d.underlayArtKey, d.underlayGlyph == null ? '.' : d.underlayGlyph.charValue());
    }


    void drawCachedMapImage(Graphics2D g, BufferedImage img, int x, int y, int w, int h) {
        RenderImageScaleCacheAuthority.draw(g, img, x, y, w, h);
    }

    void drawMapTileIcon(Graphics2D g, char ch, int worldX, int worldY, int px, int py, int w, int h, float alpha, boolean tintOwnership) {
        if (ch == InterstitialInfrastructureApi.VOID_SPACE) {
            Graphics2D voidG = (Graphics2D) g.create();
            voidG.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.max(0.05f, Math.min(1.0f, alpha))));
            voidG.setColor(Color.BLACK);
            voidG.fillRect(px, py, w, h);
            voidG.dispose();
            return;
        }
        CompiledTileDescriptor descriptor = tileDescriptorForRenderedGlyph(ch, worldX, worldY);
        BufferedImage img = semanticTileImageForRenderedGlyph(ch, worldX, worldY);
        BufferedImage underlay = underlayImageForOverlayGlyph(ch, worldX, worldY);
        boolean rotateCorridorEastWest = tileIconMode() && img != null && corridorArtRotatesEastWest(ch, worldX, worldY);
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.max(0.05f, Math.min(1.0f, alpha))));
        if (img != null) {
            if (underlay != null) drawCachedMapImage(gg, underlay, px, py, w, h);
            if (rotateCorridorEastWest) {
                gg.rotate(Math.PI / 2.0, px + w / 2.0, py + h / 2.0);
                drawCachedMapImage(gg, img, px, py, w, h);
            } else drawCachedMapImage(gg, img, px, py, w, h);
        }
        else {
            gg.setColor(colorForTile(worldX, worldY, ch));
            gg.fillRect(px, py, w, h);
            gg.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,120));
            gg.drawRect(px, py, Math.max(1,w-1), Math.max(1,h-1));
        }
        if (tintOwnership) {
            Faction owner = Faction.NONE;
            if (isInClaimedRoom(worldX, worldY) && (ch == '.' || ch == '+' || ch == ',' || ch == '`' || ch == ';' || ch == ':' || ch == '=' || ch == '-' || ch == '~')) owner = activeFaction();
            else if (world != null) owner = world.roomFaction(world.roomIdAt(worldX, worldY));
            if (owner != Faction.NONE) overlayColor(gg, px, py, w, h, colorForFaction(owner), 0.22f);
        }
        if (isWallGlyphForArt(ch)) {
            overlayColor(gg, px, py, w, h, new Color(16, 12, 8), 0.52f);
            gg.setColor(new Color(70, 54, 34, 105));
            gg.drawRect(px + 2, py + 2, Math.max(1, w - 5), Math.max(1, h - 5));
        } else if (descriptor != null && descriptor.isRoad && !descriptor.isSidewalk) {
            gg.setColor(new Color(10, 10, 12, 75));
            gg.fillRect(px, py, w, h);
            drawRoadDirectionLines(gg, descriptor.shape == null ? "north_south" : descriptor.shape, px, py, w, h);
        } else if (descriptor != null && descriptor.isSidewalk) {
            gg.setColor(new Color(20, 20, 18, 36));
            gg.fillRect(px, py, w, h);
        }
        gg.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,90));
        gg.drawRect(px, py, Math.max(1,w-1), Math.max(1,h-1));
        gg.dispose();
    }


    void drawRoadDirectionLines(Graphics2D g, String shape, int px, int py, int w, int h) {
        int cx = px + w / 2;
        int cy = py + h / 2;
        boolean west = false, east = false, north = false, south = false;
        if ("intersection".equals(shape)) { west = east = north = south = true; }
        else if ("east_west".equals(shape)) { west = east = true; }
        else if ("north_south".equals(shape)) { north = south = true; }
        else if ("corner_west_north".equals(shape)) { west = true; north = true; }
        else if ("corner_west_south".equals(shape)) { west = true; south = true; }
        else if ("corner_east_north".equals(shape)) { east = true; north = true; }
        else if ("corner_east_south".equals(shape)) { east = true; south = true; }
        else if ("end_west".equals(shape)) west = true;
        else if ("end_east".equals(shape)) east = true;
        else if ("end_north".equals(shape)) north = true;
        else if ("end_south".equals(shape)) south = true;
        else { north = south = true; }
        g.setColor(new Color(185, 165, 94, 145));
        if (west) g.drawLine(px + 2, cy, cx, cy);
        if (east) g.drawLine(cx, cy, px + w - 3, cy);
        if (north) g.drawLine(cx, py + 2, cx, cy);
        if (south) g.drawLine(cx, cy, cx, py + h - 3);
    }

    void drawMapObjectIcon(Graphics2D g, BaseObject obj, int px, int py, int w, int h, Color tint) {
        char symbol = obj == null ? '?' : obj.symbol;
        String semanticKey = obj == null ? null : TileArtSystem.semanticKeyForBuildName(obj.name);
        BufferedImage img = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForBaseObject(obj);
        if (img == null) img = images.getTile(semanticKey, symbol);
        if (img != null) drawCachedMapImage(g, img, px, py, w, h);
        else {
            g.setColor(new Color(25,25,22)); g.fillRect(px, py, w, h);
            g.setColor(new Color(180,210,150)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(symbol), px + Math.max(2,w/3), py + Math.max(12,(h*2)/3));
        }
        if (tint != null) {
            Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
            overlayColor(gg, px, py, w, h, tint, Math.max(0.05f, Math.min(0.45f, tint.getAlpha()/255f)));
            gg.dispose();
        }
        if (obj != null && obj.underConstruction) {
            Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
            Color built = new Color(170, 230, 155);
            Color stage = ProgressiveConstructionAuthority.constructionOverlayColor(obj, built);
            overlayColor(gg, px, py, w, h, stage, Math.max(0.18f, Math.min(0.65f, stage.getAlpha()/255f)));
            int pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, obj.constructionVisualProgress));
            int barW = Math.max(4, w - 4);
            int fillW = Math.max(0, (barW * pct) / 100);
            int barX = px + 2;
            int barY = py - Math.max(4, h / 7);
            gg.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,180));
            gg.fillRect(barX - 1, barY - 1, barW + 2, Math.max(4, h / 8) + 2);
            gg.setColor(new Color(175, 220, 255, 230));
            gg.fillRect(barX, barY, fillW, Math.max(3, h / 8));
            gg.setColor(new Color(235, 245, 255, 220));
            gg.drawRect(barX - 1, barY - 1, barW + 1, Math.max(4, h / 8) + 1);
            gg.dispose();
        }
        g.setColor(obj != null && obj.underConstruction ? new Color(175,220,255) : new Color(205,235,180));
        g.drawRect(px, py, Math.max(1,w-1), Math.max(1,h-1));
    }


    void drawMapFeatureIcon(Graphics2D g, MapObjectState obj, int px, int py, int w, int h, Color tint) {
        char symbol = obj == null ? '?' : obj.glyph;
        String semanticKey = TileArtSystem.semanticKeyForMapObject(obj);
        BufferedImage img = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForMapObject(obj);
        if (img == null) img = images.getTile(semanticKey, symbol);
        if (img != null) drawCachedMapImage(g, img, px, py, w, h);
        else {
            g.setColor(new Color(18,24,20)); g.fillRect(px, py, w, h);
            g.setColor(new Color(170,225,170)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(symbol), px + Math.max(2,w/3), py + Math.max(12,(h*2)/3));
        }
        if (tint != null) {
            Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
            overlayColor(gg, px, py, w, h, tint, Math.max(0.05f, Math.min(0.40f, tint.getAlpha()/255f)));
            gg.dispose();
        }
        g.setColor(new Color(190,230,180));
        g.drawRect(px, py, Math.max(1,w-1), Math.max(1,h-1));
    }


    BufferedImage activePortraitImage() {
        if (!options.importedPortraits || active == null) return null;
        NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry locked = NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.unlockedEntry(cachedOperatorProfileName, active.name);
        if (locked != null) {
            active.nameLockedProfileKey = locked.key;
            BufferedImage img = images.getNameLockedProfilePortrait(locked.key);
            if (img != null) return img;
        }
        return images.getPortrait(active.portraitSheet, active.portraitIndex);
    }

    void drawPlayerMapIcon(Graphics2D g, int px, int py, int w, int h) {
        BufferedImage face = activePortraitImage();
        if (face != null) drawCachedMapImage(g, face, px, py, w, h);
        else { g.setColor(Color.WHITE); g.drawString("@", px + Math.max(2,w/3), py + Math.max(12,(h*2)/3)); }
        overlayColor(g, px, py, w, h, new Color(255,255,255), 0.10f);
        g.setColor(new Color(245,245,245));
        g.drawRect(px, py, Math.max(1,w-1), Math.max(1,h-1));
        drawPlayerActionCountdownOverlay(g, px, py, w, h);
    }

    void drawPlayerActionCountdownOverlay(Graphics2D g, int px, int py, int w, int h) {
        if (singlePlayerSectorBridge == null || !singlePlayerSectorBridge.localPlayerActionGated()) return;
        String overlay = singlePlayerSectorBridge.activeActionCountdownOverlay();
        if (overlay == null || overlay.isBlank()) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        try {
            int bubbleH = Math.max(16, Math.min(28, h / 2 + 8));
            int bubbleW = Math.max(w, Math.min(w + 34, overlay.length() * Math.max(7, bubbleH / 2)));
            int bx = px + w / 2 - bubbleW / 2;
            int by = py - Math.max(10, bubbleH / 2);
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.88f));
            gg.setColor(new Color(8, 12, 10, 224));
            gg.fillRoundRect(bx, by, bubbleW, bubbleH, 10, 10);
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver);
            gg.setColor(new Color(255, 235, 160));
            gg.drawRoundRect(bx, by, bubbleW, bubbleH, 10, 10);
            Font oldFont = gg.getFont();
            int size = Math.max(12, Math.min(20, bubbleH - 5));
            gg.setFont(new Font("SansSerif", Font.BOLD, size));
            FontMetrics fm = gg.getFontMetrics();
            int tx = bx + Math.max(3, (bubbleW - fm.stringWidth(overlay)) / 2);
            int ty = by + ((bubbleH - fm.getHeight()) / 2) + fm.getAscent();
            gg.drawString(overlay, tx, ty);
            gg.setFont(oldFont);
        } finally {
            gg.dispose();
        }
    }

    void drawNpcMapIcon(Graphics2D g, NpcEntity npc, int px, int py, int w, int h) {
        BufferedImage face = options.importedPortraits ? images.getNpcPortraitFor(npc) : null;
        if (face != null) drawCachedMapImage(g, face, px, py, w, h);
        else { g.setColor(npcColor(npc.faction)); g.fillRect(px, py, w, h); g.setColor(Color.BLACK); g.drawString(String.valueOf(npc == null ? '?' : npc.symbol), px + Math.max(2,w/3), py + Math.max(12,(h*2)/3)); }
        overlayColor(g, px, py, w, h, npcColor(npc == null ? Faction.NONE : npc.faction), npc != null && npc.isAnimalActor() ? 0.14f : 0.22f);
        int stroke = Math.max(1, Math.min(3, Math.max(w, h) / 22));
        Stroke oldStroke = g.getStroke();
        if (npc != null && npc.isAnimalActor()) {
            g.setColor(npc.isPetActor() ? new Color(130, 220, 145) : new Color(105, 150, 95));
            g.setStroke(new BasicStroke(stroke));
            g.drawRoundRect(px + stroke/2, py + stroke/2, Math.max(1,w-stroke), Math.max(1,h-stroke), Math.max(4,w/5), Math.max(4,h/5));
        } else {
            Color rankColor = rankColor(npc == null ? 8 : npc.factionRank);
            g.setColor(rankColor);
            g.setStroke(new BasicStroke(stroke));
            g.drawRect(px + stroke/2, py + stroke/2, Math.max(1,w-stroke), Math.max(1,h-stroke));
            drawRankBadge(g, npc == null ? 8 : npc.factionRank, px, py, w, h);
        }
        g.setStroke(oldStroke);
    }

    Color rankColor(int rank) {
        switch(Math.max(1, Math.min(8, rank))) {
            case 1: return new Color(255, 216, 80);
            case 2: return new Color(225, 225, 235);
            case 3: return new Color(220, 76, 64);
            case 4: return new Color(90, 155, 245);
            case 5: return new Color(90, 210, 120);
            case 6: return new Color(230, 155, 55);
            case 7: return new Color(105, 210, 220);
            default: return new Color(150, 150, 155);
        }
    }

    void drawRankBadge(Graphics2D g, int rank, int px, int py, int w, int h) {
        int r = Math.max(1, Math.min(8, rank));
        int size = Math.max(8, Math.min(16, Math.min(w, h) / 2));
        int bx = px + w - size - Math.max(1, w / 18);
        int by = py + Math.max(1, h / 18);
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING, RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
        gg.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,190));
        gg.fillRoundRect(bx, by, size, size, Math.max(3,size/3), Math.max(3,size/3));
        gg.setColor(rankColor(r));
        int cx = bx + size/2, cy = by + size/2;
        int pad = Math.max(2, size/6);
        if (r == 1) {
            Polygon star = new Polygon();
            for(int i=0;i<10;i++){ double a=-Math.PI/2 + i*Math.PI/5; int rad=(i%2==0)?size/2-pad:size/4; star.addPoint(cx+(int)Math.round(Math.cos(a)*rad), cy+(int)Math.round(Math.sin(a)*rad)); }
            gg.fillPolygon(star);
        } else if (r == 2) {
            Polygon diamond = new Polygon(new int[]{cx,bx+size-pad,cx,bx+pad}, new int[]{by+pad,cy,by+size-pad,cy}, 4);
            gg.fillPolygon(diamond);
        } else if (r == 3) {
            Polygon tri = new Polygon(new int[]{cx,bx+size-pad,bx+pad}, new int[]{by+pad,by+size-pad,by+size-pad}, 3);
            gg.fillPolygon(tri);
        } else if (r == 4) {
            gg.fillRect(bx+pad, by+pad, Math.max(2,size-pad*2), Math.max(2,size-pad*2));
        } else if (r == 5) {
            Polygon chev = new Polygon(new int[]{bx+pad,cx,bx+size-pad,bx+size-pad,cx,bx+pad}, new int[]{by+size/2,by+pad,by+size/2,by+size-pad,by+size/2+pad,by+size-pad}, 6);
            gg.fillPolygon(chev);
        } else if (r == 6) {
            gg.fillRoundRect(bx+pad, by+size/3, size-pad*2, Math.max(2,size/3), 2, 2);
        } else if (r == 7) {
            gg.fillOval(bx+pad, by+pad, Math.max(2,size-pad*2), Math.max(2,size-pad*2));
        } else {
            gg.drawLine(bx+pad, by+pad, bx+size-pad, by+size-pad);
            gg.drawLine(bx+size-pad, by+pad, bx+pad, by+size-pad);
        }
        gg.setColor(new Color(255,255,230,210));
        gg.drawRoundRect(bx, by, size-1, size-1, Math.max(3,size/3), Math.max(3,size/3));
        gg.dispose();
    }

    void overlayColor(Graphics2D g, int x, int y, int w, int h, Color c, float alpha) {
        Composite old = g.getComposite();
        g.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.max(0.0f, Math.min(1.0f, alpha))));
        g.setColor(c);
        g.fillRect(x, y, w, h);
        g.setComposite(old);
    }

    void drawRecentActionFeed(Graphics2D g) {
        Rectangle map = mapRect();
        Rectangle tactical = tacticalSlateRect();
        int x = tactical.x;
        int w = tactical.width;
        int y;
        int h;
        if (tacticalSlateVisible) {
            h = Math.max(64, Math.min(90, tactical.y - (map.y + map.height) - 6));
            y = Math.max(map.y + map.height + 2, tactical.y - h - 4);
            if (y + h > tactical.y - 2) h = Math.max(48, tactical.y - y - 3);
        } else {
            y = tactical.y;
            h = tactical.height;
        }
        g.setColor(new Color(0, 0, 0, tacticalSlateVisible ? 222 : 236));
        g.fillRoundRect(x, y, w, h, 12, 12);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, x, y, w, h, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "recent-actions-feed", x, y, w, h);
        Font labelFont = smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-4f));
        g.setFont(labelFont);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        g.drawString(tacticalSlateVisible ? "RECENT ACTIONS" : "RECENT EVENTS — EXTERNAL AWARENESS", x + 12, y + 16);
        int bodyX = x + 12, bodyY = y + 22, bodyW = w - 24, bodyH = Math.max(14, h - 28);
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(bodyX, bodyY, bodyW, bodyH);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-3f)));
        fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineH = Math.max(12, fm.getHeight());
        int maxLines = Math.max(1, bodyH / lineH);
        ArrayList<String> source = new ArrayList<>();
        for (int i = Math.max(0, eventLog.size() - 80); i < eventLog.size(); i++) {
            String line = eventLog.get(i);
            if (recentFeedExternalAwarenessEligible(line)) source.add(line);
        }
        if (source.isEmpty()) source.add("No external events in immediate awareness.");
        java.util.List<String> wrapped = TextLayoutAuthority.wrapAllPixels(g, g.getFont(), source, bodyW - 8);
        int start = Math.max(0, wrapped.size() - maxLines);
        int yy = bodyY + fm.getAscent();
        for (int i = start; i < wrapped.size(); i++) {
            String line = wrapped.get(i);
            g.setColor(actionFeedColor(line));
            g.drawString(line, bodyX, yy);
            yy += lineH;
            if (yy > bodyY + bodyH) break;
        }
        g.setClip(old);
    }

    Color actionFeedColor(String line) {
        String low = line == null ? "" : line.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (low.contains("damage") || low.contains("wound") || low.contains("lost") || low.contains("failed") || low.contains("alert") || low.contains("warning")) return new Color(235, 105, 86);
        if (low.contains("bought") || low.contains("purchased") || low.contains("found") || low.contains("scavenged") || low.contains("gained") || low.contains("recovered")) return new Color(132, 220, 132);
        if (low.contains("heard") || low.contains("noise") || low.contains("voice") || low.contains("boots") || low.contains("murmurs")) return new Color(218, 190, 95);
        return optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN);
    }

    boolean recentFeedExternalAwarenessEligible(String line) {
        if (line == null || line.isBlank()) return false;
        String low = line.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (low.startsWith("you ") || low.startsWith("your ") || low.startsWith("equipped ") || low.startsWith("equipment:") || low.startsWith("selected ")) return false;
        if (low.startsWith("inventory") || low.startsWith("cannot ") || low.startsWith("no direct use") || low.startsWith("finalized character:")) return false;
        if (low.contains(" player ") && (low.contains("moves") || low.contains("wait") || low.contains("equips") || low.contains("uses"))) return false;
        if (low.startsWith("world selected:") || low.startsWith("world generated:") || low.startsWith("profile-linked dossier")) return false;
        return true;
    }

    void toggleTacticalSlate() {
        tacticalSlateVisible = !tacticalSlateVisible;
        DebugLog.audit("TACTICAL_SLATE", "visible=" + tacticalSlateVisible + " source=F1 state=" + stateSummary());
        repaint();
    }

void drawCommandTablet(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY) {
        Rectangle r = tacticalSlateRect();
        g.setColor(new Color(0, 0, 0, 242));
        g.fillRect(r.x, r.y, r.width, r.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, r.x, r.y, r.width, r.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "tactical-slate", r.x, r.y, r.width, r.height);
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(r.x + 12, r.y + 8, Math.max(1, r.width - 24), Math.max(1, r.height - 16));
        Font labelFont = smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-4f));
        g.setFont(labelFont);
        g.setColor(new Color(210, 190, 126));
        g.drawString("TACTICAL SLATE", r.x + 14, r.y + 15);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-2f)));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        String nameLine = active == null ? "No active character" : active.name + " | " + active.job;
        ArrayList<String> slate = new ArrayList<>();
        slate.add(nameLine + " | Survival " + timeText() + " | World " + worldTimeText() + " | Food " + food + "/15 Water " + water + "/15 | Sleep " + (sleepNeed / TURNS_PER_HOUR) + "h/26h | Heat " + gangHeat + " Suspicion " + suspicion + " | XP " + xp + " KC " + knowledgeCredits + " | Camera " + camX + "," + camY + " | Zoom " + options.worldZoomLabel());
        slate.add("Move " + movementModeLabel() + " range " + movementModeRange() + " cost " + movementTurnCost() + " | " + activeMotionStateLabel() + " facing " + facingLabel() + " | vision " + visionRange() + " hearing " + hearingRange());
        slate.add(portableLightStatusLine());
        WorldSnapshot serverSnapshot = singlePlayerSectorBridge == null ? null : singlePlayerSectorBridge.latestWorldSnapshot();
